47 - ##ੰਲਕਾ ਗੰਨਾ		 English (Meaning Translation)

**Gurmat Preaching and Amrit Prachar**
Listeners of Bhai Hira Singh Ji's Kirtan often used to say that... he used to bind them such that the whole Sangat seemed 'mesmerized'.
...When I read an article published after his passing [in] **'Khalsa Advocate' 18.9.1926**, these lines of that article drew my attention...:
"We remember those words which an Arya [Samaji] said to his companion in Sindh - 'Come quickly after listening to Bhai Sahib's Kirtan, no need to listen to the explanation (Vyakhiya), because I have heard that he fills some such magic in his speech that heart gets tempted to become a Sikh and thus many people of other religions abandon their previous faith.'"

I kept thinking about this for a long time, 'Did he really have such magic?' Then I read somewhere else, 'Bhai Hira Singh Ji's speech had the effect of magic.' And then more that 'The effect of his magic-speech was such that atheists used to become believers.' All these things were somewhat surprising, and I kept reflecting on this for long.

Once I mentioned this 'magic-speech' to **Respected Bhai Sahel Singh Ji Chawla** (1903-2001). He was a great lover of Guru's house and practitioner of Naam. He immediately narrated an eye-witness scene to me which he had seen at the time of Amrit Prachar held at a religious Diwan in Faruka; he was also a student there at that time. It is as follows:

[A student] came with a cleaner shave than before. On being asked by companions he said, "Today Bhai Sahib Ji has to inspire for Amrit Prachar and I have got shaved properly so that I don't get trapped in this loop." But when he wore the dress and came out in the form of procession, that very student, wearing a beautiful turban and Kirpan, was included in that Jatha. On asking he told, "There was some such magic effect in Bhai Hira Singh Ji's speech that I could not remain without the gift of Amrit. I was explained a lot that I am Sehajdhari yet..."

Notes
- Corrected likely OCR word: "ਮਿਸਮਿਰਾਈਜ਼" -> "Mesmerized".
- Corrected likely OCR word: "ਹਜਾਮਤ" -> "Hajaamat" (Shave).

ਤੇ ਅਮਤ ਪਰਚਾਰ ਹੁੰਦਾ ਤੇ ਬਹੁਤ ਸਾਰੇ ਪ੍ਰਾਣੀ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਛੱਕ ਕੇ ਤਿਆਰ-ਬਰ-ਤਿਆਰ ਹੁੰਦੇ, ਕਈ
ਕੀਤਾ ਕਿ ਆਪਣੇ ਸਹੁਰੇ
ਸੰਨ 1914 ਦੇ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਵਿੱਚ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਨੇ ਇਹ ਨਿਸ਼ਚਾ
ਪਰਿਵਾਰ ਦੇ ਸਬੰਧੀ ਜੋ ਅਜੇ ਤਕ ਸਹਿਜਧਾਰੀ ਸਨ, ਐਤਕੀਂ ਸਾਰੇ ਇਕੱਠੇ ਗੁਰੂ ਕੇ ਜਹਾਜ਼ ਚੜ੍ਹਾ
ਹੋਣੇ ਹਨ। ਸੰਤ ਅਤਰ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੂੰ ਬੇਨਤੀ ਕਰਕੇ ਲੈ ਆਏ ਤੇ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਦਾ ਐਸਾ ਰੰਗ ਬੱਝਾ ਜੋ
ਕਰਿਣ ਤੋਂ ਬਾਹਰ ਹੈ। ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਦੇ ਸਹੁਰਾ, ਭਾਈ ਦੂਨੀ ਚੰਦ ਜੀ ਪੰਜ ਭਰਾ ਸਨ, ਅਗੋਂ ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ
ਦੇ ਪੁੱਤਰ ਤੇ ਹੋਰ ਸਨਬੰਧੀ, ਤਕਰੀਬਨ 40-45 ਸੱਜਣ, ਸਾਰਿਆਂ ਨੂੰ ਇਕੱਠਾ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਛਕਾ ਕੇ
ਸਿੰਘ ਸਜਾਇਆ। ਜਦ ਸਾਰੇ ਸਿੰਘ ਸੋਹਣੇ ਦਸਤਾਰੇ, ਕਛੈਰਰੇ, ਕ੍ਰਿਪਾਨਾਂ ਤੇ ਕੇਸਰੀ ਕਮਰਬੰਦ ਸਜਾ
ਕੇ ਜਲੂਸ ਦੀ ਸ਼ਕਲ ਵਿੱਚ 'ਸੋ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਗੁਰ ਤੇ ਪਾਇਆ..." ਪੜ੍ਹਦੇ ਬਾਹਰ ਨਿਕਲੇ ਤਾਂ ਇੱਕ ਬੜਾ
ਮਨਮੋਹਣਾ ਦ੍ਰਿਸ਼ ਬੱਝਾ।
ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਇੱਕ ਬੱਚੇ ਦਾ ਜ਼ਿਕਰ ਵਰਨਣ-ਯੋਗ ਹੈ। ਇਹ ਸੀ ਭਾਈ ਖੇਮ ਚੰਦ ਦਾ ਛੋਂਟਾ
ਪੁੱਤਰ ਅਰਜਨ ਦਾਸ, ਜਿਸਦੀ ਉਮਰ ਉਸ ਵਕਤ 12 ਵਰ੍ਹੇ ਦੀ ਸੀ। ਭਾਈ ਖੇਮ ਚੰਦ (ਰਿਸ਼ਤੇ
ਵਿੱਚ ਉਹ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੀ ਸੁਪਤਨੀ ਦੇ ਸਕੇ ਚਾਚਾ ਜੀ ਸਨ) ਦੇ ਵੱਡੇ ਪੁੱਤਰ, ਭਾਈ
ਖੁਸ਼ਾਲ ਸਿੰਘ, ਪਹਿਲਾਂ ਕਿਸੇ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਅਵਸਰ 'ਤੇ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਛੱਕ ਕੇ ਸਿੰਘ ਸੱਜ ਚੁੱਕੇ ਸਨ। ਇਸ
ਵਾਰੀ ਅਰਜਨ ਦਾਸ ਨੇ ਸਿੰਘ ਸੱਜਣ ਦਾ ਨਿਸ਼ਚਾ ਕਰ ਲਿਆ ਤੇ ਇਸ ਮੰਤਵ ਲਈ ਦੀਵਾਨ
ਸਮਾਗਮ ਤੋਂ ਮਹੀਨਾ-ਦੋ ਮਹੀਨੇ ਪਹਿਲਾਂ ਹੀ ਕੇਸ ਰੱਖਣੇ ਸ਼ੁਰੂ ਕਰ ਦਿੱਤੇ। ਜਦ ਭਾਈ ਖੇਮ ਚੰਦ
ਬਿਸਤਰੇ 'ਤੇ ਹੀ ਰਹਿੰਦੀ ਸੀ ਤੇ ਉਹ ਆਖਦੇ ਸਨ ਕਿ ਜੇਕਰ ਇਸਨੇ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਛੱਕ ਲਿਆ ਤਾਂ
ਇਸਦੇ ਕੇਸ ਕੌਣ ਸਾਂਭੇਗਾ। ਚੁਨਾਂਚਿ ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਨੇ ਲਾਲੂ ਨਾਂਈ ਨੂੰ ਘਰ ਬੁਲਵਾ ਭੇਜਿਆ। ਪਰ ਜਦ
ਅਰਜਨ ਨੂੰ ਪਤਾ ਲੱਗਾ ਤਾਂ ਉਹ ਨੰਗੇ ਪੈਰੀਂ ਹੀ ਘਰੋਂ ਨੱਸ ਗਿਆ ਤੇ ਸ਼ਾਮਾਂ ਵੇਲੇਂ ਘਰ ਮੁੜਿਆ।
ਤੇ ਚ ਦੇ ਪੇਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਲਿਆ ਰਿਹਾ। ਇੱ ਉਹ ਚਰੀ ਦੇ ਿੰਟੇ ੋਰ ਕੇ ਦਾਣੇ ਚਬਦਾ ਰਿਹਾ
ਰਾਨਮ/ਤ' ਪਰਚਾਰ ਤੇ ਆੰਮਤ` ਪ੍ਚਾਰ` - “/		 English (Meaning Translation)

...[but on my insistence] I was administered Amrit there and then.
Since their business etc...

It was his effort that whichever good Giani or Preacher... he saw/knew, he would bring him to Diwans of Faruka, Sillanwali etc. and bless the Sangat by listening to Guru's praise.
**Sant Attar Singh Ji**, **Sant Gurbakhsh Singh Ji Sant Sangat Singh Ji**, **Bhai Sudh Singh Pradhan Singh Ji**, **Giani Thakur Singh Ji**, **Bhai Samund Singh Ji**... [used to come].
And Amrit Prachar used to take place and many souls used to take Amrit and become Tyar-Bar-Tyar.

In the Diwan of year **1914**, Bhai Sahib made this resolve that [all] relatives of his in-laws family who were Sehajdhari till now, this time all of them together should board the Guru's ship...
He requested Sant Attar Singh Ji and brought him, and such a color of preaching was bound that it is beyond description. Bhai Sahib's father-in-law **Bhai Duni Chand Ji** were five brothers. Further their sons and other relatives, about **40-45 gentlemen**, making all of them take Amrit together, they were adorned as Singhs.
When all the Singhs, adorned with beautiful turbans, Kachheras, Kirpans and saffron Kamarbands (waistbands), came out in the form of a procession singing "So Amrit Gur Te Paya...", a very captivating scene was created.

The mention of a child among these is noteworthy. This was **Arjan Das**, the younger son of **Bhai Khem Chand**, whose age was 12 years at that time. The elder son of Bhai Khem Chand (in relation he was the real uncle/Chacha of Bhai Hira Singh Ji's wife), **Bhai Khushal Singh**, had already taken Amrit and become a Singh on some earlier Diwan occasion. This time **Arjan Das** resolved to become a Singh and for this purpose started keeping hair (Kes) a month or two before the Diwan. When Bhai Khem Chand [came to know? or wife?], [she] used to stay on bed and she said, "If he takes Amrit, who will take care of his hair?"
Accordingly, she sent for **Lalu Barber** to home. But when Arjan came to know, he ran away from home barefoot and returned in the evening.
...remained hiding in the fields. There he kept chewing grains breaking the cobs of Chari (fodder crop).

Notes
- Corrected likely OCR word: "ਲਾਲੂ ਨਾਂਈ" -> "Lalu Nai" (Barber name).
- Corrected likely OCR word: "ਚਰੀ" -> "Chari" (Fodder crop).

ਤੇ ਭਾਈ ਖੈਮ ਚੰਦ ਨੇ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਛੱਕਣ ਦੀ ਆਗਿਆ ਦੇ ਦਿੱਤੀ । ਇਹੀ ਸ੍ਰ. ਅਰਜਨ ਸਿੰਘ ਜਰ

ਹੈ। ਇਹ ਵਿਥਿਆ ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਨੇ ਆਪ ਲੇਖਕ ਨੂੰ ਲੁਧਿਆਣੇ 20 ਮਈ 1979 ਨੂੰ ਸੁਣਾਈ, ਤੇ
ਕਹਿਣ ਲੱਗੇ 'ੈਂ ਤਾਂ ਸਿੱਖੀ ਬਹੁਤ ਮਹਿੰਗੀ ਲਈ ਸੀ।' (ਸ਼ੋਕ ਹੈ ਕਿ ਸ੍ਰ. ਅਰਜਨ ਸਿੰਘ (ਜਨਮ
1903) 12.11.1988 ਨੂੰ ਗੁਰਪੁਰੀ ਸਿਧਾਰ ਗਏ।)
ਇਹੋ ਜਿਹੀ ਸੀ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਦੇ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਦੀ ਖਿੱਚ।
ਮੰਡੀ ਬਹਾਉਦੀਨ (ਗੁਜਰਾਤ, ਪਾਕਿਸਤਾਨ) ਦੇ ਇੱਕ ਧਾਰਮਿਕ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਦੇ ਅਵਸਰ 'ਤੇ
ਹੋਏ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਬਾਰੇ ਭਾਈ ਸੁੱਧ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਰਾਗੀ, ਜੋ ਕਿ ਉੱਥੇ ਪੁੱਜੇ ਹੋਏ ਸਨ, ਨੇ ਆਪਣੀ
'ਇਸ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਵਿੱਚ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੇ ਚਾਰ ਅਪੀਲਾਂ ਕੀਤੀਆਂ, ਪਹਿਲੀ
ਕਾਮਯਾਬੀ ਹੋਈ । ਸੰਗਤਾਂ ਬੱਦਲ ਦੀ ਤਰ੍ਹਾਂ ਵੱਸੀਆਂ ਤੇ ਝੋਲੀਆਂ ਭਰ ਦਿੱਤੀਆਂ।
ਤੀਜੇ ਦਿਨ ਸ਼ਾਮ ਦੇ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਵਿੱਚ ਮੈਨੂੰ (ਭਾਈ ਸੁਧ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੂੰ) ਨਾਲ ਲੈ ਕੇ ਆ ਗਏ
ਤੋਂ ਖਾਲੀ ਜਾਣ ਵਾਲੀ ਗੱਲ ਹੈ। ਦੀਵਾਨ ਭਰਿਆ ਹੋਇਆ ਸੀ। ਭਾਈ ਕਰਤਾਰ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ
ਉਹ ਭਾਸ਼ਨ ਸਮਾਪਤ ਕਰਕੇ ਬੈਠ ਗਏ। ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੇ ਸਟੇਜ 'ਤੇ ਮੈਨੂੰ ਖੜ੍ਹਾ ਕਰ
ਬਦਲ ਵਾਂਗ ਮਾਇਆ ਦਾ ਮੀਂਹ ਵਰਸਾ ਕੇ ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਮੰਗਾਂ ਨੂੰ ਸਵੀਕਾਰ ਕੀਤਾ ਹੈ ਪਰ ਇੱਕ ਮੰਗ,
ਇੱਕ ਭੁੱਖ ਅਜੇ ਬਾਕੀ ਹੈ। ਭਾਈ ਸੁੱਧ ਸਿੰਘ ਤੁਹਾਡਾ ਕੀਰਤਨੀਆ ਹੈ, ਇਹ ਸੇਵਕ ਝੋਲੀ ਅੱਡ
ਕੇ ਕੁਝ ਮੰਗਦਾ ਹੈ। ਆਪ ਆਪਣੇ ਸੇਵਕ ਦੀ ਝੋਲੀ ਭਰ ਦੇਵੋ। ਇਹ ਮੰਗਦਾ ਹੈ ਅੱਜ ਕੌਈ
ਰਸੀ ਕਸਾਧਰੀ ਬਣੇ ਅਤੇ ਕਲਗੀਆਂ ਵਾਲੋ ਦਾ ਬੇਟਾ ਬਣ ਕੇ ਖਾਲਸਾ ਪੰਥ
ਵਹਾ, ਮੈ ਪਰਿਵਾਰ ਸਮੇਤ ਹਾਜ਼ਰ ਰਾਂ, ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਛਕਾਉ ਸਿੰਘ ਸਜਾਊ, ਜੇ ਕਾਰੇ ਗੱਜੇ, ਉਤਸਾਂ
ਅਰ ਡਾ. ਤਾਈ ਨੈਣ ਦਾਸ, ਤੀਜਾ ਭਾਈ ਸੋਹਨ ਲਾਲ ਤੇ ਇਸੇ ਤਰ੍ਹਾਂ ਅੱਧੇ ਘੰਟੇ ਵਿੱਚ
ਨਾਰਾਂ ਸਹਿਜਧਾਰੀ ਘਰਾਣੇ ਸਿੱਖੀ ਮੰਭਲ ਵਿੱਚ ਆਏ।'
(ਖ਼ਾਲਸਾ ਸਮਾਚਾਰ 309:192'/
੨੧ ੨੪ ੧੫ & ਤੂ.
੪੪੬੧ ੪੧੧ ੪੩ ੪੬੧ ੩੧		 English (Meaning Translation)

...lived on chewing sorghum [stalks]... He insisted that 'I will take Amrit only from the hands of Bhai Hira Singh Ji (who was his brother-in-law in relation).'
A letter was sent to **Bhai Khushal Singh** (his elder brother) who was working in Karachi at that time...
The Chaudhary of the village **Bhai Tarlok Singh Ji** explained to **Bhai Khem Chand** not to trouble the child, lest he takes some other [drastic] step. Upon this Bhai Khem Chand gave permission to take Amrit.
This is the same **Sardar Arjan Singh** whose firm is famous in Delhi and Bombay by the name of **'Arjan Singh Khem Chand'**. He himself narrated this story to the author in Ludhiana on **20 May 1979**, and said, "I had earned Sikhism at a very high cost." (It is sad that S. Arjan Singh (born 1903) passed away on 12.11.1988).

Such was the attraction of Bhai Sahib's Amrit Prachar.
Regarding an Amrit Prachar held on the occasion of a religious Diwan at **Mandi Bahauddin** (Gujarat, Pakistan), **Bhai Sudh Singh Ji Ragi**, who had reached there, wrote in his [article]:
"In this Diwan Bhai Hira Singh Ji made four appeals, [three] were successful... Sangats rained money like cloud and filled the bags.
On the third day in the evening Diwan, he took me (Bhai Sudh Singh Ji) along... The Diwan was full. **Bhai Kartar Singh Ji**... finished his speech and sat down. Bhai Hira Singh Ji made me stand on the stage [and said]:
'...Like a cloud you have rained money and accepted those demands, but one demand, one hunger is still left. Bhai Sudh Singh is your Kirtaniya, this servant asks for something by spreading his shirt-front (Jholi). Fill the bag of your servant. He asks that today some Keshadhari (with hair) become firm [Singh?], and becoming son of the Plume-Wearer (Guru Gobind Singh), increase the glory of Khalsa Panth...'
...I am present with family, administer Amrit to us, make us Singhs...
...Bhai Nain Das, third Bhai Sohan Lal and similarly in half an hour... many Sehajdhari families entered the sphere of Sikhism." (Khalsa Samachar 30.9.192[?])

Notes
- Corrected likely OCR word: "ਚਰ੍ਹੀ" -> "Chari" (Sorghum/Fodder).
- Corrected likely OCR word: "ਜੀਜਾ ਜੀ" -> "Jija Ji" (Sister's husband).
- Corrected likely OCR word: "ਆਪਾ ਵਾਰੇ" -> "Apa Vare" (Sacrifice self/Surrender).

ਭਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਜੰ ਜੀ ਠੀਕ ਪੰਜ ਵਜ ਪੰਚ ਗਏ। ਨਸ਼ਰ ਤੋਂ ਆਪ ਅੱ ਰੱਖ
ਸਨ। ਆਉਂਦਿਆਂ ਹੀ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਸੁਰੂ ਕੀਤਾ। ਕਲਗੀਧਰ ਮਿਤ ਕਿ ਕੋਈ ਸਹਿਜਧਾਰੀ
ਦਰਸ਼ਨ ਕਰਾ ਦਿੱਤੇ। ਬੜੇ ਪਰੇਮ ਵਿੱਚ ਗੱਦ-ਗੱਦ ਹੋ ਕੇ ਆਵਾ ਬਾ ਦ।' ਦੋ
ਦੇ ਕਰਗ਼ੀਧਰ ਪਿਤਾ ਦੀ ਗੋਦ ਵਿੱਚ ਬੈਠੇ ਤੇ ਸਿੰਘ ਸੱਜ ਕੇ ਗੁਰੂ ਕਾ ਲਾਡਲਾ ਬਦ
“ਰੀ ਆਪ ਨੇ ਸੱਦ ਲਾਈ ਸੀ ਕਿ ਦਾਸ ਦੇ ਚਾਚਾ ਭਾਈ ਆਸਾ ਨੰਦ ਜੀ ਉੱਠ ਖ਼ ਵੱਟ ਤ
ਆਸਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਰਖਿਆ ਗਿਆ। ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਦਾ ਪਰਿਵਾਰ ਗੁਰੂ ਮਿਹਰ ਹੇਠ ਵੱਧ ਫੁੱਲ ਰਿਹਾ ਹੈ। ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ
ਦੇ ਪੁੱਤਰ ਸਰਦਾਰ ਜਸਵੰਤ ਸਿੰਘ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਵੇਲੇ ਉਠ ਕੇ ਰੇਜ਼ ਘਰ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਕਰਦੇ ਹਨ। ਪਰਿਵਾਰ
ਗੁਰੂ ਚਰਨਾਂ ਦਾ ਭੌਰਾ ਹੈ।
ਅੱਗੇ ਚਲ ਕੇ ਸਰਦਾਰ ਸੁੰਦਰ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਲਿਖਦੇ ਹਨ, 'ਜਦੋਂ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਮਰਦਾਨ ਹੁੰਦੇ
ਸੀ ਤਾਂ ਦਾਸ ਨੂੰ ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਦੇ ਨੇੜੇ ਹੋਣ ਦਾ ਕਈ ਵਾਰ ਸਮਾਂ ਮਿਲਿਆ। ਜਦੋਂ ਦੇਖੋ ਆਪ ਗੁਰਬਾਣੀ
ਦਾ ਪਾਠ ਹੀ ਕਰਦੇ ਹੁੰਦੇ ਸੀ। ਦਾਸ ਨੇ ਵੀ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਤੋਂ ਛੱਕਿਆ ਸੀ।'
(ਖ਼ਾਲਸਾ ਸਮਾਚਾਰ, 28-8-1952)
ਸਰਗੋਧੇ ਦੀ ਬਾਰ ਵਿੱਚ ਕਈ ਚੱਕ ਸਿੱਖਾਂ ਦੇ ਸਨ ਜਿੱਥੇ ਸਿੱਖ ਫ਼ੌਜੀ ਪੈਨਸ਼ਨ ਪਾ ਕੇ ਆਬਾਦ
ਸਨ। ਚੱਕ 64 ਦੀ ਆਬਾਦੀ ਤਾਂ ਮਸਾਂ 50-60 ਘਰਾਂ ਦੀ ਸੀ ਪਰ ਗੁਰੂ ਪਿਆਰੇ ਭਾਈ ਪ੍ਰੇਮ
ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੇ ਉਦਮ ਨਾਲ ਇਥੇ 4-5 ਧਾਰਮਿਕ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਬੜੀ ਧੂਮ-ਧਾਮ ਨਾਲ ਸੱਜੇ ਜਿਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ
ਬਾਰ ਦੇ ਸਾਰੇ ਚੱਕਾਂ ਦੇ ਸਿੱਖ ਹਾਜ਼ਰੀ ਭਰਦੇ ਤੇ ਲਾਭ ਉਠਾਉਂਦੇ।
_ ਮਨ 1913-14 ਦੀ ਗੱਲ ਹੈ ਕਿ ਸਿਲਾਂਵਾਲੀ (ਜ਼ਿਲ੍ਹਾ ਸਰਗੋਧਾ) ਦੇ ਨੇੜੇ ਇਸ ਚੱਕ 64
ਮੁਕਰਿਆਂ ਉਸ ਤਫਣਾ ਇਆ ਜਿਸ ਵਿੱਚ ਭਾਈ ਮਹਾਂ ਸਿੰਘ ਦੀ ਸ਼ਹੀਦੀ ਦਾ ਜ਼ਿਕਰ
ਰਗ ਉਸ ਆਤਮਾ ਦੇ ਵਿਯੋਗ 'ਤੇ ਕਲਗੀ ਵਾਲੇ ਦੀ ਗੋਦ ਵਿੱਚ ਰਖੇ ਉਸ ਦੇ ਸੀਸ
ਬੜੇ ਵੈਰਾਗ ਛਪ ਹੋਆ ਤਾਂ ਸੈਗਤਾਂ ਦੇ ਨੈਣ ਵਗ੍ਹ ਤੂਰ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਖ਼ੁਦ ਵੀ
ਸਾਹਿਬ ਉਠ ਪਲ ਰਗ ਦੇ ਖ਼ਾਤਮੇ 'ਤੋਂ ਮਾਇਆ ਵੱਸਣੀ ਸੁਰੂ ਹੋਈ ਤਾਂ ਭਾਈ
੩ ਢੁਨ ਖਲੋਤੇ ਤੋਂ ਝੋਲੀ ਅੱਡ ਕੇ ਬਿਨੈ ਕੀਤੀ, 'ਸਾਧ ਸੰਗਤ ਜੀ ! ਮਾਇਆ ਸਾਂਭ ਰੱਖੋ,

ਰਾਨਆ/ਤ' ਪਚਾਨ'` ਤੰ ਆੱਸ੍ਰਤ ਪਰਚਾਰ - 45		 English (Meaning Translation)

**Sardar Sundar Singh Ji Majithia** writes in one of his articles:
"...Bhai Hira Singh Ji reached exactly at 5 o'clock. He had brought [ragis?] from the town. As soon as he came, he started Kirtan. He prayed to Kalgidhar Father, 'May some Sehajdhari have the glimpse [of becoming a Singh].'
In great love and emotion, he raised a call... 'Who will sit in the lap of Kalgidhar Father and becoming a Singh, become the beloved of the Guru?'
...At once he called out that the servant's uncle **Bhai Asa Nand Ji** should get up...
[He took Amrit and] was named **Asa Singh**. His family is blooming under Guru's grace. His son **Sardar Jaswant Singh** wakes up at Amrit Vela and performs Kirtan at home daily. The family is a beetle (follower) of Guru's feet."

Further Sardar Sundar Singh Ji writes, "When Bhai Sahib used to be in **Mardan**, Das (I) got the opportunity to be near him many times. Whenever seen, he used to be reciting Gurbani. Das (I) also took Amrit from Bhai Sahib." (Khalsa Samachar, 28-8-1952)

In the 'Bar' (Canal colony area) of **Sargodha**, there were many 'Chakks' (villages) of Sikhs where Sikh army-men were settled after pension. The population of **Chakk 64** was hardly 50-60 households, but with the effort of Guru-beloved **Bhai Prem Singh Ji**, 4-5 religious Diwans were held here with great pomp in which Sikhs from all Chakks of the Bar used to attend and take benefit.

It is a matter of year **1913-14** that near **Sillanwali** (District Sargodha) in this Chakk 64...
[Bhai Sahib] narrated that Sakhi in which the martyrdom of **Bhai Maha Singh** is mentioned...
Upon the separation of that soul, keeping his head in the lap of the Plume-Wearer...
When deep dispassion arose, tears flowed from the eyes of Sangats, Bhai Sahib himself was also [in tears]. When money started raining after the end of the [Diwan?], Bhai [Sahib] stood up and spreading his Jholi requested, 'Sadh Sangat Ji! Keep the money... [I want heads/commitment]'

ਲੀ
/ ਹੜ, ਨਾ ਤੂੰ ਤਰ		 English (Meaning Translation)

'...If the Plume-Wearer Satguru is dear [to you], then get ready to take Amrit... And O Sehajdhari brothers! Guru sacrificed himself [for you], become Amritdhari Singhs, keep Guru['s form] and enjoy the Sikh faith.'
Hearing his words, many Sehajdharis presented themselves to take Amrit. It is especially important to mention two of them.

One gentleman **Bhai Ladha Ram Dhamija** used to run a shop in **Chakk No. 126**. His wife's name was **Ram Bai**. There was no Keshadhari Sikh in their family... Bhai Ladha Ram stood up and asked for the gift of Amrit and became Singh along with his family. Then his name was kept **Ladha Singh** and sons' names **Ram Singh** and **Harnam Singh**.

When this family returned home after becoming Singhs, Bhai Ladha Singh's elder brother **Bhai Kaura Ram** got very angry and said, "You didn't even ask us... went and made the Ardas (commitment) yourself; you separate from us and don't show your face to us." In earlier times, there used to be much fear of elder brothers and they were respected like fathers. So Bhai Ladha Singh Ji got scared and remained silent for some time. But he meditated on Satguru Kalgidhar and prayed in his heart, "O Satguru! You yourself be kind." After a short while, he said to the elder brother with respect, "We have done a good deed from our side, but do you want that we should return the Ardas (break the vow)?"

Hearing the words "Return the Ardas?", Bhai Kaura Ram was stunned and got terrified; saying, "No, No. Ardas performed in Guru's presence cannot be returned. I made a mistake, pray for me, ask forgiveness for my mistake!"

After some time when the marriage of Bhai Ladha Singh's daughter was fixed, a dispute arose in the house. The brother of Bhai Ladha Singh's wife Ram Bai was of staunch Sanatan views. He said that if the marriage is done according to Gurmat (Anand Karaj), then the maternal family (Nanke) will not sit [in the ceremony]. But Bibi Ram Bai said, "We are not to turn away from the Guru, the promise we made to Bhai Hira Singh Ji in Guru's presence, we have to fulfill that. So whether brothers sit in the marriage or not, the marriage will be according to Gurmat only."

Then Ram Bai brought... brother... who came to explain... "Jajmani! This is the first marriage in your house, do not do this wrong work... lest some trouble befalls your family." Bhai Ladha Singh and Bibi Ram Bai remained firm...
Finally, the Anand Karaj was performed according to Gur-Maryada and everyone...
Bhai Hira Singh Ji was not just a Ragi, but a purely devoted... filled with emotions of faith...
With the intoxication of Naam-Khumari his beautiful eyes remained intoxicated...

Notes
- Corrected likely OCR word: "ਅਰਦਾਸ ਮੋੜ" -> "Ardas Mod" (Revoke/Return the prayer/vow).

ਗੁਰਮਤ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਤੰ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ - 47		 English (Meaning Translation)

...eyes that could meet [God?].
...used to perform Katah and Amrit Prachar.
...with great spiritual experience...
On the Gurpurab of Vaisakhi [1918], **Sant Attar Singh Ji Mastuana** [came]...
Two days before Vaisakhi, Baba [Attar Singh] Ji...
...famous historian... daily Sri Guru [Granth]...
...started giving motivation to [Sangats?]. This [is about] year 1917 or...
**Bhai Hira Singh Ji**...
**[Baba] Hoti Mardan (1882-?)**...
...sent a message to **Sant Singh Ji** that Sant [Attar Singh] should make some effort for Sehajdharis to become Keshadhari.
[Looking at Bhai Hira Singh], Sant Ji said that on the day of Vaisakhi...
...that report which was in Persian language, you recite it to the Sangat in its original form.
[Bhai Hira Singh] Ji recited that report in Persian language and told its meanings:
*Hamah Ha Yak Mazhabe Shawad*
(You all should come into one religion)
*Har Char Baran Kaume Hanood Baham*
(All four castes of Hindus together)
*Yake Khud Ra Bar Digre Tarjih Na Dahad*
(No one should consider himself superior to another)
*Piyale Man Gariifta Marduma Har Chahar Yag Ja Nash Bikhurand*
*Az Yag Lota*
(People of all four [castes] should take the bowl held by me and drink from one place/pot)
(Hearing this, many Brahmins and Khatris got up [and left])
*Hazar Kass Raza Dadand*
(Thousand people gave consent)

This was the account of the day of Amrit administration written in **Aurangzeb's Daily Diary** (Roznamcha), which Bhai Hira Singh Ji narrated to the Sangat and Sikh Sehajdharis. When Bhai [Sahib narrated that] **20,000** people took Amrit, then **Sant Baba Attar Singh Ji** said, "O Sehajdhari gentlemen! Is there anyone among you, who takes the pledge to become Keshadhari right now?"
...[Someone] stood up and said, "I should be given the gift of Amrit."
Then what was there, from among Sehajdhari Sikhs **Nand Lal Ji** of Mandi, **Asa Nand Ji** of [Rina?], and **Lal Chand Ji**... and many other... got up and writing their names kept sitting on one side.

ਭੀ ਹੈਡ ਭਰਾ ਹੀ

੭		 English (Meaning Translation)

...On that day such a large number of poor and rich Sehajdhari Sikhs taking Amrit and [becoming Singhs], this was not the [magic] of Sant Attar Singh Ji and Bhai Hira Singh Ji alone.
...It was an effort made with the support of [Guru's Feet], which was a miracle.

Bhai Hira Singh Ji usually used to sing a Ghazal in memory of Sahib Kalgidhar Ji with great faith and devotion. It is this:

*Mai Lekar Teg-e-Barahna, Kalgidhar Ji Aate Hain*
(Taking a naked sword, Kalgidhar Ji comes)
...
*Pakad Khench Kar Satgur Us Ko Tambu Mein Le Jate Hain*
(Catching and pulling, Satguru takes him into the tent)
*Algarz Sabh Sangat Mein Se, Sikh Guru Ke Nikle Paanch!*
(In short, from the whole congregation, five Sikhs of the Guru came out!)
*Un Ko Daste Mubarak Se Phir Aake Hayat Pilate Hain*
(Then coming back, he feeds them Life [Amrit] from his blessed hands)
*Abdi Jeevan Un Ko Bakhsha, Aaj Talak Woh Zinda Hain*
(He bestowed eternal life upon them, they are alive till today)
*Un Ke Sadke Hamre Jaise Papi Bhi Gat Pate Hain*
(By their grace, even sinners like us get salvation)

Actually, there was a passion and a yearning inside Bhai Hira Singh Ji that the preaching of Sikhism should happen in the whole world. In this regard, some words of one of his speeches are as follows, which were given in the Golden Jubilee Book of Sikh Educational Conference:
Appealing [he] said, "Khalsa will roar like a lion in the forest and bushes... When will these great words come true?
In the world, the wealthy and powerful are in unrest, those who take pride in cannons and guns are seeing themselves empty inside. This heat of the world has to be removed, and peace in the world has to come through your hands and your Sikh religion. Arise, get organized and jump into Dharma Prachar and show by becoming at least one crore Khalsa.
The work of Dharma Prachar should not be left sitting in hope of Granthis of Gurdwaras and preachers countable on fingers, this work should be done by every Sardar, Raja, Maharaja, worker and businessman."

Notes
- Corrected likely OCR word: "ਤੇਗ਼ੇ ਬਰਹਨਾ" -> "Teg-e-Barahna" (Naked Sword).
- Corrected likely OCR word: "ਹਯਾਤ" -> "Hayat" (Life/Amrit).

ਇਤਿਹਾਸ ਵਿੱਚ ਭਾਵੇਂ ਅਨੰਦ ਕਾਰਜ ਦਾ ਜ਼ਿਕਰ ਛੇਵੇਂ ਪਾਤਸ਼ਾਹ ' ਹਰਿਗੋਬਿੰ
ਬੀ ਵੀਰੋ ਦਾ ਅਨੰਦ ਕਾਰਜ ਪਿੰਡ ਝਬਾਲ ਵਿੱਚ ਕੀਤਾ ਸੀ, ਪਰ ਸਮਾਂ ਪਾ ਕੇ ਬ੍ਰਾਹਮਣੀ
ਰਿਵਾਜ ਮੁੜ ਪ੍ਰਚੱਲਤ ਹੋਂ ਗਿਆ ਅਤੇ ਮਹਾਰਾਜਾ ਰਣਜੀਤ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੇ ਸਮੇਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਬ੍ਰਾਹਮਣੀ
ਧੁਰ ਨੰ ਵਿਸੇਸ਼ ਮਹੱਤਵ ਮਿਲਣ ਕਾਰਣ ਇਹ ਰੀਤੀ ਬਿਲਕੁਲ ਹੀ ਖ਼ਤਮ ਹੋ ਗਈ।
ਫਿਰ ਸਿੱਖ ਰਾਜ ਤੋਂ ਬਾਅਦ ਬਾਬਾ ਦਰਬਾਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ (1814-1870) ਜੋ ਨਿਰੰਕਾਰੀ
ਸੰਪਰਦਾਇ ਦੇ ਬਾਨੀ, ਬਾਬਾ ਦਿਆਲ ਜੀ (1783-1855) ਦੇ ਵੱਡੇ ਸਪੁੱਤਰ ਤੇ
ਸਨ, ਨੇ ਮਾਰਚ 1855 ਵਿੱਚ ਇੱਕ ਖੁੱਲ੍ਹੇ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਵਿੱਚ ਅਨੰਦ ਵਿਆਹ ਗੁਰਮਰਿਆਦਾ ਅਨੁਸ਼ਾਰ
ਕੀਤਾ ਤੇ ਇਹ ਰਸਮ ਆਪਣੇ ਰਾਵਲਪਿੰਡੀ ਦੇ ਗੁਰਦੁਆਰੇ ਵਿੱਚ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰੀ, ਜੋ ਬਾਹਰ ਸੰਗਤਾਂ
ਵਿੱਚ ਵੀ ਸ਼ੁਰੂ ਹੋਂ ਗਈ ਪਰ ਵਿਰੋਧਤਾ ਹੁੰਦੀ ਰਹੀ।
ਜਦ ਸਿੰਘ ਸਭਾ ਦੇ ਸੇਵਕਾਂ ਦੇ ਉਦਮ ਨਾਲ ਗੁਰਮਰਯਾਦਾ ਦਾ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਸ਼ੁਰੂ ਹੋਇਆ ਤਾੰ
ਜਰ ਕਾਨੂੰਨੀ ਦੱਸ ਕੇ ਅੜਚਨਾਂ ਪਾਉਣੀਆਂ ਸ਼ੁਰੂ ਕੀਤੀਆਂ ਗਈਆਂ। ਅਦਾਲਤਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਮੁਕੱਦਮੇ
ਖੜ੍ਹੇ ਕਰਕੇ ਕਈ ਅਨੰਦ ਵਿਆਹ ਵਿਧਾਨ ਤੋਂ ਵਿਰੁੱਧ ਹੋਣ ਦੇ ਫ਼ਤਵੇ ਲਾਏ ਗਏ।
ਇਸ ਔਕੜ ਤੋਂ ਛੁਟਕਾਰਾ ਪਾਉਣ ਖਾਤਰ ਅਨੰਦ ਮੈਰਿਜ ਐਕਟ ਪਾਸ ਕਰਾਇਆ ਗਿਆ|
ਰਿਹ ਬਿਲ ਪਿਲੋਂ ਰਿਆਸਤ ਨਾਭਾ ਦੇ ਯੁਵਰਾਜ ਟਿਕਾ ਰਿਪੂਦਮਨ ਸਿੰਘ, ਜੋ ਉਦੋਂ ਵਾਇਸਰਾਏ
ਦੀ ਗੌਸਲ ਦੇ ਮੈਂਬਰ ਸਨ, ਨੇ 30 ਅਕਤੂਬਰ 198 ਨੂੰ ਪੇਸ਼ ਕੀਤਾ ਤੇ ਪਿੱਛੋਂ ਇਸੇ ਕੌਂਸਲ ਦੀ
ਉਪੋਕਤ ਪੋਜ਼ੀਸ਼ਨ 'ਤੇ ਪੁੱਜ ਕੇ ਸਰਦਾਰ ਸੁੰਦਰ ਸਿੰਘ ਮਜੀਠੀਆ ਨੇ 22 ਅਕਤੂਬਰ 1909 ਨੂੰ
ਪਾਸ ਕਰਾਇਆ। _
ਇਸ ਐਕਟ ਦੇ ਪਾਸ ਹੋਣ ਨਾਲ ਅਦਾਲਤੀ ਔਕੜਾਂ ਤਾਂ ਘੱਟ ਗਈਆਂ ਪਰ ਸਮਾਜਕ ਤਰ
'ਤੇ ਵਿਰੋਧ ਕਾਫੀ ਚਿਰ ਪਿਛੇ ਵੀ ਹੁੰਦਾ ਰਿਹਾ। _
ਕਪ ਨਹ ਸੀ ਇਆ ਤੱ ਬਚਦੇ ਵਧ ਆਮ ਦੀ ਕਦ
ਕਾਰਜਾਂ ਵਿਰੁੱਧ ਜੋੜ ਕੇ ਪਰਚਾਰੇ ਗਏ। ਮਿਸਾਲ ਵਜੋਂ ਕਿ ਸੱਥ ਇਸ ਤਰ੍ਹਾਂ ਕਰਨ ਨ ਹਨ"
ਇਹੋ ਜਿਹੇ ਗ਼ਲਤ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਦਾ ਸਦਕਾ ਤੇ ਸਮਾਜਕ ਵਿਰੋਧ ਕਾਰਣ ਚੰਗੇ ਸਿੱਖ “ਜਦ
ਕਾਰਜ ਕਰਨ ਤੋਂ ਸੰਕੋਚ ਕਰਦੇ ਸਨ | ੨
ਲਾਂ		 English (Meaning Translation)

Although mention of Anand Karaj is found in history [during time of] **Sixth Patshah** [Guru] Hargobind...
Bibi Viro's Anand Karaj was performed in village **Jhabal**, but with passage of time Brahmanical rituals became prevalent again and in the time of **Maharaja Ranjit Singh Ji** due to special importance given to Brahmanical [priests], this tradition almost vanished.

Then after Sikh Raj, **Baba Darbara Singh Ji (1814-1870)**, who was the eldest son and successor of **Baba Dyal Ji (1783-1855)**, founder of **Nirankari Samparda**, performed Anand Vivah in an open Diwan according to Gur-Maryada in **March 1855** and preached this ritual in his Gurdwara at **Rawalpindi**, which started outside in Sangats also but opposition continued.

When with the effort of Singh Sabha servants, preaching of Gur-Maryada started, then citing it as illegal, obstacles were started. By raising lawsuits in courts, fatwas were issued declaring many Anand Vivahs as against the law.
To get rid of this difficulty, **Anand Marriage Act** was passed.
This Bill was first presented by **Tika Ripudaman Singh**, Yuvaraj of Nabha State, who was then a member of Viceroy's Council, on **30 October 1908**, and later reaching the same position in the Council, **Sardar Sundar Singh Majithia** got it passed on **22 October 1909**.

With the passing of this Act, legal difficulties reduced but opposition on social level continued for a long time.
...against Anand Karaj... preached. For example that "Sikhs should not do this..."
Due to such wrong propaganda and social opposition, even good Sikhs hesitated to perform Anand Karaj.

- Corrected likely OCR word: "ਗੁਰੂ ਗੋਬਿੰਦ" -> "Hargobind" (Guru Hargobind - context of Bibi Viro).
- Corrected likely OCR word: "198" -> "1908" (Year of bill presentation).

ਖੜ੍ਹਾ ਕਦ		 English (Meaning Translation)

Taking it to a popular position is the fruit of the labor of Singh Sabha servants.
In this aspect, the labor of **Bhai Hira Singh Ji** is significant. Bhai Hira Singh Ji's own marriage, which took place at a young age in **1894**, was also performed with Brahmanical rites. But when he came to Sri Amritsar in **1896** and came in contact with Singh Sabha servants, he presented himself at Sri Akal Takht and got his marriage performed again according to Gur-Maryada! Here itself he administered Amrit to his wife (Singhni) and kept her name **Prem Kaur**.
The service of Kirtan and Preaching he started later from **1897**.

Facing many difficulties and opposition, he not only did solid preaching of Gur-Maryada but also made this custom successful. Wherever Bhai Hira Singh Ji reached for Gurmat Anand Karaj, he would create such an impact that listening to his oratory, many families would pledge to follow Gur-Maryada. Some samples of such many incidents are given below.
It is a matter of year **1904** that Bhai Sahib reached **Mardan** in connection with preaching. Here **Doctor Diwan Singh Ji**, famous historian **Baba Prem Singh Ji** and **Sardar Sant Singh Ji** of Garhi Kapura etc. Guru's beloveds had established a beautiful Satsang Mandal. Here he had been performing Kirtan for only a few days when a unique incident happened.

About 12 miles from **Hoti Mardan**, right on the border of non-settled (Ghair-Ilaka, tribal) area, a small village existed, whose name in Pashto was **'Sara Cheena'** (Cold Spring). A poor devout Sikh **Bhai Visakha Singh** lived here and about 9-10 households were of other faiths also.
Two of [his sons?] were killed by the bullets of Pathans of non-settled area. Bhai Visakha Singh...
...
[Bhai Sahib was asked to perform Anand Karaj there?]

Notes
- "Vaktrita" means Oratory/Speech.
- "Ghair-Ilaka" refers to the tribal frontier areas not fully under British administration.

_ ੧੧		 English (Meaning Translation)

...[People advised him against going], but the more they stopped Bhai Sahib, the more he insisted on going. Finally, he got ready to go with his Jatha.
In those days cars were not yet prevalent, so arrangements of horses and Tongas were made. Traveling overnight, they all reached the border of Yagistan area at Amrit Vela.

...Around Bhai Visakha Singh's house, gunman Pathans brought along were made to stand guard. Now **Sri Guru Granth Sahib Ji** was installed (Prakash). This Holy Bir they had taken along from Hoti. Bhai Hira Singh Ji started Kirtan of **Asa Di Var**.
The sweetness [of his voice] and love-soaked explanation was casting a magical spell on the listeners.
He completed this Anand Karaj according to time, his distinctive wisdom, and such ability that the onlookers were overwhelmed.

**Amazing Scene:** When Bhai Hira Singh Ji was performing Kirtan, **Chaudhary Mahesha Mal** from the opposing faction of the village, either to see the spectacle of Gur-Maryada marriage or with the intention of creating disturbance, came and sat in the Sangat covering his face. The Amrit Kirtan of Bhai Sahib and the holy Gur-Maryada had such a magical effect on his mind that he got up and went out, and then in a short while came back to the Diwan bringing other companions of his faction along, and stood in the Sangat with folded hands and said, "If this is Gur-Maryada, then first of all we pledge to be followers of Gur-Maryada today."

According to the statement of **Baba Prem Singh Ji Hoti**, "This success had such an effect on Bhai Hira Singh Ji's mind that the glowing redness of his face turned into an unbearable spiritual radiance. At this time, in the passion of youth, he roared such thunderous **Jaikaras** (Bolay So Nihal), the echo of which made the local hills tremble. This was the effect of his captivating Kirtan, listening to which the whole village of staunch opponents became friends and loving devotees of Guru's house."
(Khalsa Samachar, 30 August 1951)

Another incident is of **Chakk 77** of Lyallpur. From here, after performing the Anand Karaj of the daughter of **Daffadar Ganda Singh**, Bhai Sahib met **Bhai Sudh Singh Ji** at Sargodha and...

- "Vashisht Budhi" means Distinctive/Special Intellect or Wisdom.
- "Yagistan" refers to the tribal/rebel area (land of rebels).

ਹੋ ਜਾਓ।' ਇਹ ਸੁਣ ਕੇ ਮੈਂ ਉਸ ਸਰਦਾਰ ਨੂੰ ਕਿਹਾ, 'ਅਸੀਂ ਚਲੋ ਤਾਂ ਜਾਵਾਂਗੇ ਪਰ ਜਾਣ ਤੂ
ਪਹਿਲਾਂ ਕਾਕੀ ਦੀ ਮਾਤਾ ਨੂੰ ਸਤਿ ਸ੍ਰੀ ਅਕਾਲ ਤਾਂ ਬੁਲਾ ਆਈਏ। ਉਹ ਆਖਣ ਲੱਗਾ, ਰਾਈ
ਸਾਹਿਬ ! ਆਪ ਨਾ ਚਲੋ ਤੇ ਆਪਣੀ ਬੇਇੱਜ਼ਤੀ ਨਾ ਕਰਾਓ।' ਪਰ ਮੈਂ ਬਦੋਬਦੀ ਉਸਦੇ ਨਾਲ
ਉਸਦੇ ਘਰ ਚਲਾ ਹੀ ਗਿਆ ਤੇ ਜਾ ਕਿਹਾ, ਬੇਬੇ ਜੀ ! ਸਤਿ ਕਰਤਾਰ ।' ਉਸ ਨੇ ਅੱਗੋਂ ਕਿਹ,
'ਆਓ ਭਾਈ ਜੀ, ਸਤਿ ਸ੍ਰੀ ਅਕਾਲ!
'ਬੇਬੇ ਜੀ ! ਕੀ ਤੁਹਾਡੀ ਹੀ ਕਾਕੀ ਦਾ ਵਿਆਹ ਹੈ ?'
'ਜੀ ਹਾਂ, ਭਾਈ ਜੀ, ਮੇਰੀ ਹੀ ਕਾਕੀ ਹੈ।'
'ਕੀ ਤੂੰ ਸਕੀ ਮਾਂ ਹੈਂ ਜਾਂ ਮਤਰੇਈ ? ਸੱਚੀ ਸੱਚੀ ਦੱਸੋ।'
ਨਹੀਂ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ, ਸੁਖ ਨਾਲ ਬੋਲੋਂ।
'ਅਸੀਂ ਪੁੱਛਦੇ ਹਾਂ ਕਿ ਤੂੰ ਸੱਕੀ ਮਾਂ ਹੈਂ ? ਸਾਨੂੰ ਸ਼ੱਕ ਪਿਆ ਹੈ ਕਿ ਤੂੰ ਸੱਕੀ ਮਾਂ ਨਹੀਂ,
ਕਿਉਂਕਿ ਮੈਂ ਸੁਣਿਆ ਹੈ ਤੁਸੀਂ ਆਖਿਆ ਹੈ ਕਿ ਜੇ ਮੇਰੀ ਕਾਕੀ ਦੇ ਵਿਆਹ ਵਿੱਚ ਗੁਰੂ ਨਾਨਕ
ਦੇਵ ਜੀ, ਗੁਰੂ ਗੋਬਿੰਦ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਸੱਚੇ ਪਿਤਾ ਆਏ ਤਾਂ ਮੈਂ ਖੂਹ ਵਿੱਚ ਛਾਲ ਮਾਰ ਕੇਂ ਡੁੱਬ
ਹਿੰਦੀਆਂ ?'
__ਐੱਗੋਂ ਹੱਥ ਜੋੜ ਕੇ ਉਸ ਬੀਬੀ ਨੇ ਕਿਹਾ, 'ਵਾਹਿਗੁਰੂ ਵਾਹਿਗੁਰੂ, ਮੈਂ ਕਦੋਂ ਇਹ ਆਖਿਆ
ਹੈ, ਮੇਰਾ ਮੂੰਹ ਸੜ ਜਾਏ, ਮੇਰੀ ਬੇਟੀ ਦੇ ਅਨੰਦ ਕਾਰਜ 'ਤੇ ਮੇਰੇ ਘਰ ਗੁਰ ਨਾਨਕ, ਗੁਰੁ
ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਕਹਿਣ ਲੱਗੇ, 'ਸ਼ਾਬਾਸ਼ ਮਾਤਾ, ਧੰਨ ਹੈਂ ਤੂੰ, ਲੈ ਫਿਰ ਗੁਰੁ ਬਾਬਾ ਜੀ ਆਏ
ਸਮਝ, ਤੂੰ ਦਰੀਆਂ ਵਿਛਾ ਰ ਰ੍‌
___ ਗੁਰਦੁਆਰੇ ਜਾ ਕੇ ਸ੍ਰੀ ਗੁਰੂ ਬਾਬਾ ਜੀ ਦੀ ਸਵਾਰੀ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਕਰਦਿਆਂ, ਜੈਕਾਰੇ ਗਜਾਂਦਿਆਂ
ਆ ਗਿਆ। ਗੁਰਮਤਾ ਸੋਧ ਦਿੱਤਾ। ਇਹ ਗੁਰੂ ਦੀ ਕਰਾਮਾਤ ਵਰਤੀ ਤੌਂ £
ਵਿ ਕੂ ਭਚ ਦਾ”		 English (Meaning Translation)

[Someone said]: "...[opposition/trouble] is happening... so you go back.
Forgive me, here many settlers are owners of Murabbas (squares of land) [and vast properties], first of all [I] was going to perform the Anand of my daughter, but all these people do not agree in any way. So you please go back."
Hearing this I said to that Sardar, "We will go, but before going let us at least say Sat Sri Akal to the mother of the girl. He said, 'Bhai Sahib! You don't go and don't get yourself insulted.' But I forcibly went to his house along with him and went and said, 'Bebe Ji! Sat Kartar.' She replied, 'Come Bhai Ji, Sat Sri Akal!'

'Bebe Ji! Is it your own daughter's wedding?'
'Yes, Bhai Ji, she is my own daughter.'
'Are you real mother or step-mother? Tell the truth.'
'No Bhai Sahib, speak auspicious words.'
'We ask are you the real mother? We have a doubt that you are not the real mother, because I have heard that you have said "If Guru Nanak Dev Ji, Guru Gobind Singh Ji True Father come in my daughter's wedding, then I will jump in the well and drown"... Do [mothers] say this?'

Next, with folded hands that lady said, 'Waheguru Waheguru, when did I say this? May my mouth return [words]... At my daughter's Anand Karaj, Guru Nanak, Guru [Gobind Singh]... come to my house?'
Bhai Sahib said, 'Bravo Mother, blessed are you. Then consider Guru Baba Ji has come, you spread the mats...'

Going to the Gurdwara, performing Kirtan [in front of] the simple Palanquin of Sri Guru Baba Ji, roaring Jaikaras... came [to the house]. Reformed the Gurmata. This miracle of Guru happened...

Notes
- "Murabba" is a unit of land measurement (approx 25 acres).
- "Matrei" means Stepmother.

ਪਿਆਰ ਬਾਈ ਨੂੰ ਇਹ ਕਾਰਜ ਗੁਰ-ਮਰਯਾਦਾ ਅਨੁਸਾਰ ਕਰਨ ਲਈ ਮਨਾ ਕੇ ਇਲਾਕੇ ਦੀਆਂ ਸਿੱਖ
ਸੰਗਤਾਂ ਨੂੰ ਸੌਦਾ ਦਿੱਤਾ ਕਿ ਇਸ ਅਨੰਦ ਕਾਰਜ ਵਿੱਚ ਸ਼ਾਮਲ ਹੋ ਕੇ ਆਪਣਾ ਸਹਿਯੋਗ ਦੇਣ । ਇਸ
ਦੀ ਉਥੇ ਕਾਫ਼ੀ ਵਿਰੋਧਤਾ ਹੋਈ ਤੇ ਬਰਾਦਰੀ ਦੇ ਕਈ ਸੱਜਣਾਂ ਨੇ ਵਿਆਹ ਵਿੱਚ ਸ਼ਾਮਲ ਨਾ ਹੋਣ

ਇਸ ਅਨੰਦ ਕਾਰਜ ਦਾ ਐਸਾ ਸੋਹਣਾ ਪ੍ਰਭਾਵ ਪਿਆ ਕਿ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਦੀ ਅਪੀਲ 'ਤੇ

ਹ
ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਵਿੱਚੋਂ ਸਭ ਤੋਂ ਪਹਿਲੇ ਸਨ, ਭਾਈ ਅਮਰ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਗੰਢ। ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਦੀ ਪੋਤਰੀ ਤੇ ਭਾਈ
ਲਾਲ ਸਿੰਘ ਦੀ ਸਪੁੱਤਰੀ ਬੀਬੀ ਰਣਜੀਤ ਕੌਰ ਦਾ ਸਬੰਧ ਇਲਾਕੇ ਦੇ ਇੱਕ ਮੰਨੇ-ਪ੍ਰਮੰਨੇ ਸਿਰਕੱਢ
ਸਿੱਖ, ਭਾਈ ਨਿਰਮਲ ਸਿੰਘ ਤਰਖਾਨਾ ਵਾਲੇ ਦੇ ਭਤੀਜੇ ਭਾਈ ਹਰਵੰਦ ਸਿੰਘ ਨਾਲ ਨੀਯਤ ਹੋ
ਚੁੱਕਾ ਸੀ। ਜਦ ਵਿਆਹ ਦਾ ਸਮਾਂ ਆਇਆ ਤਾਂ ਇੱਕ ਭਾਰੀ ਅੜਚਨ ਖੜ੍ਹੀ ਹੋ ਗਈ। ਭਾਈ
ਅਮਰ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਪੱਕੇ ਸਿਦਕੀ ਸਿੰਘ, ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਵੇਲੇ ਉੱਠ ਕੇ ਬਾਣੀ ਪੜ੍ਹਣ ਵਾਲੇ ਪ੍ਰੇਮੀ ਸੱਜਣ
ਖ਼ਿਆਲਾਂ ਦੇ ਸਨ। ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੇ ਪੱਕਾ ਇਰਾਦਾ ਕਰ ਲਿਆ ਕਿ ਗੁਰੂ ਦੀ ਓਟ ਲੈ
ਕੇ ਇਹ ਕਾਰਜ ਗੁਰ-ਮਰਯਾਦਾ ਅਨੁਸਾਰ ਹੀ ਕਰਨਾ ਹੈ। ਕਿਉਂ ਜੋ ਇਹ ਦੋਵੇਂ ਸੱਜਣ ਇਲਾਕੇ
ਦੇ ਸਿਰਕੱਢ ਤੇ ਮੰਨੇ-ਪ੍ਰਮੰਨੇ ਸਨ। ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਦੇ ਐਸਾ ਕਰਨ ਨਾਲ ਅੱਗੋਂ ਸਾਰਿਆਂ ਲਈ ਰਾਹ ਸਾਫ਼
ਹੋ ਜਾਂਦਾ ਸੀ। ਇਸ ਲਈ ਆਪ ਨੇਂ ਪੂਰੇ ਅਠਾਰਾਂ ਦਿਨ ਫਿਰੂਕੇ ਰਹਿ ਕੇ ਗੁਰਮਤਿ ਦਾ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ
ਬਾਹਮਣੀ ਤਰੀਕੇ ਦਾ ਹੀ ਹੋਵੇਗਾ। ਬਹੁਤ ਸਾਰੈ ਰਾਤ ਗਈ ਤਕ ਯਤਨ ਹੁੰਦੇ ਰਹੇ ਕਿ ਕਿਸ
ਤਰੀਕੇ ਲੜਕੇ ਵਾਲੇ ਮੰਨ ਜਾਣ ਪਰ ਉਹ ਜ਼ਿਦ 'ਤੇ ਕਾਇਮ ਰਹੇ। ਅਖ਼ੀਰ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਨੇ
ਵਿੱਚ ਪੈ ਕੇ ਇਹ ਫ਼ੈਸਲਾ ਕਰਵਾਇਆ ਕਿ ਸਿਰਫ਼ ਲੜਕੇ ਨੂੰ ਲਿਜਾ ਕੇ ਲਾਵਾਂ ਲਈਆਂ ਜਾਣ
ਅਤੇ ਬੇਸ਼ਕ ਬਰਾਤੀ ਕੋਈ ਵੀ ਸ਼ਾਮਲ ਨਾ ਹੋਵੇ।
ਕੀਰਤਨ ਸ਼ੁਰੁ ਹੋਇਆ ਤੇ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੇ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਬਾਣੀ ਦੀ ਬਰਖਾ ਸ਼ੁਰੂ ਕੀਤੀ, ਸਾਰੇ
ਵਿਆਖਿਆ ਸਣ ਕੇ ਸਭ ਹਿੰਦੁ ਮੁਸਲਮਾਨ ਦੰਗ ਰਹਿ ਗਏ। ਸਭ ਮਾਫ਼ੀਆਂ ਪਏ ਮੰਗਣ, ਆਖਣੇ
ਨੂੰ ਤਾਂ ਪਤਾ ਹੀ ਨਹੀਂ ਸੀ ਇਹੋ ਜਿਹੀ ਹੈ ਗੁਰੂ ਦੀ ਮਰਜਾਦਾ। ਅੱਗੇ ਲਈ ਸਾਹੀ
ਬਰਾਦਰੀ ਨੇ ਅਨੰਦ ਕਾਰਜ ਕਰਨ ਦੇ ਪ੍ਰਣ ਕੀਤੇ। ਇਹ ਅਨੰਦ ਕਾਰਜ 27 ਅਗਸਤ
ਨੰ ਹੋਇਆ। ਇਸ ਤੋਂ' ਪਿੱਛੋਂ ਉਸ ਇਲਾਕੇ ਵਿੱਚ ਹਰੇਕ ਸਿੱਖ ਬੱਚੇ-ਬੱਚੀ ਦਾ ਵਿਆਹ ਗੁਰ-		 English (Meaning Translation)

...Convincing **Pyar Bai** (likely the name of the lady in previous page) to perform this task according to Gur-Maryada, invitation was given to Sikh Sangats of the area to join this Anand Karaj and give their cooperation. There was considerable opposition to this there and many gentlemen of the community [threatened] not to participate in the wedding...
This was the first Anand Karaj in that area which took place in **May 1900**.

This Anand Karaj had such a beautiful effect that on Bhai Sahib's appeal... many Gursikhs took a pledge to perform their children's weddings according to Gur-Maryada.
Among them first were **Bhai Amar Singh Ji Gandha**. The relationship of his granddaughter and daughter of **Bhai Lal Singh**, **Bibi Ranjit Kaur**, was fixed with **Bhai Harwand Singh**, nephew of a prominent and respected Sikh of the area **Bhai Nirmal Singh Tarkhana Wale**.
When the time of wedding came, a huge obstacle arose. Bhai Amar Singh Ji was a firm devout Singh, who used to wake up at Amrit Vela and recite Bani... [but the other side] was of [Sanatan?] views.
Bhai Hira Singh Ji made a firm resolve that taking the shelter of Guru, this task must be performed according to Gur-Maryada only. Because both these gentlemen were prominent and respected in the area, their doing so would clear the way for everyone in future. Therefore, staying in **Faruka** for full eighteen days, he preached Gurmat...
[Opponents insisted] it will be by Brahmanical method only. Many efforts were made till late night that the boy's family might agree, but they remained firm on their stubbornness. Finally Bhai Sahib... intervening got this decision made that only the boy (groom) should be taken and Lavan (marriage rounds) be performed, and let no Barati (wedding guest) join.

Kirtan started and Bhai Hira Singh Ji started the rain of Amrit Bani... listening to the explanation all Hindus and Muslims were left stunned. All started asking for forgiveness, saying "We didn't know that Guru's Maryada is like this..."
For future... the brotherhood pledged to perform Anand Karaj. This Anand Karaj took place on **27 August**...
After this, every Sikh boy and girl's wedding in that area [started happening according to Gur-Maryada].

Notes
- "Tarkhana Wale" likely refers to the village name or sub-caste identification used in the area.

ਰਾਤ ਗਈ ਤਕ ਕਰਨਲ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਨੂੰ ਮਨਾਉਣ ਦੀ ਕੋਸ਼ਿਸ਼ ਕਰਦੇ ਰਹੇ ਪਰ ਉਹ ਕਿਵੇਂ ਵੀ ਅਨੰਦ
ਕਾਰਜ ਲਈ ਨਾ ਮੰਨੇ। ਜਦ ਇਸ ਗੱਲ ਦਾ
ਲਈ ਨਾ ਸੰ ਪਤਾ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੂੰ ਲੱਗਾ ਤਾਂ ਉਹ

ਅਤੇ ਭਾਈ ਰੀਗ ਸੰ. ਤਦ ਭਾਗ ਸਿੰਘ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੇ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਦਾ ਰਸ ਬੰਨ੍ਹਿਆ

<= ” 74, ਜੋ ਸਾਰਾ ਪੋਗਰਾਮ ਧਿਮਾਨ ਜਡ ੩੨ -% ੮੮੨ ੨੩ ੮੨੨ ਦ੨ ਨੀ ਮਸੰਨ
ਲਿਜਾ ੨੬੫੬		 English (Meaning Translation)

...[The other party] was not ready... and he wanted to perform Lavan with Bedis (around fire?), while for this the boy's father was not ready. The situation reached a point of dispute and Sardar Ji brought the Barat back. Upon this **Sardar Ram Singh General Merchant** accepted with great pleasure to perform the Anand of his daughter with that Sardar's son right then.
...It was considered necessary to celebrate [this event]. For this **Bhai Bhag Singh Hira Singh Ji** were called by telegram and for three days full Diwans were held on the occasion of the wedding.

An interesting incident of an Anand Karaj was narrated to us in **August 1967** by Gurmukh Pyare **Sardar Gurmukh Singh Ji**, Retired Engineer. He was a Satsangi gentleman of very high life and spiritual enjoyment. After living an age of about **95 years**, he left for Guru's feet on **4 September 1968**. He narrated the story of the marriage of his elder son **Sardar Kulwant Singh Ji**, which took place in **1914** in **Jammu** with the daughter of **Colonel Anant Ram**.
Both gentlemen were on high posts in the State and Colonel Sahib hesitated from Maharaja Sahib because he (Maharaja) did not like marriages to happen by any other custom than Bedis (Hindu ritual) in his state.
On this side **S. Gurmukh Singh Ji** was a follower of Singh Sabha objectives and also he had called Bhai Hira Singh Ji for this task. He kept trying to convince Colonel Sahib till late night but he did not agree for Anand Karaj in any way.

When **Bhai Hira Singh Ji** came to know about this... he also came there and started talking to Colonel Sahib. Meanwhile, a Pandit came and said, "Sir, the time for Mahurat has passed."
On this Bhai Hira Singh Ji [seized the opportunity] and said, "Your Mahurat time has passed, but our Mahurat (Amrit Vela) is yet to come."
So... Prakash was done... Bhai Bhag Singh Hira Singh Ji bound the essence of Kirtan...
When the Anand Karaj was performed according to Gurmat, [seeing the glory] Maharaja... was very pleased...

Notes
- "Vedi" refers to the act of circling the fire in Hindu marriage ritual.
- "Mahurat" is the auspicious time calculated by astrologers.

੭		 English (Meaning Translation)

**Sikh Educational Conference**
Coming back from there, **S. Sundar Singh Ji Majithia**, who was in that Jatha, held a select gathering of Panth on **9 January 1908** at his residence...
In which gentlemen from Lahore, Amritsar and Gujranwala marking their presence...
proceedings took place under the presidentship of **Sardar Tarlochan Singh Ji**, **Bhai Jodh Singh Ji** was appointed Secretary.
Then after holding one or two more meetings, the foundation of the Conference was laid with consensus and it was decided to hold the first conference at **Gujranwala**. And it was held there on **17-18-19 April 1908**.

In the issue of **23-9-26** of 'Khalsa Samachar', printed 3 weeks after Bhai Hira Singh Ji's passing, the kind editor started the main article with these lines:
"The picture of religious Diwans of the time of Conference comes before eyes. Anand...
Exactly such was his relation with the Conference, as if one's name [is associated with] the other...
[The Diwan], which used to be the main part of the Conference, used to be such a gathering that attracted Sangats the most and in this Bhai Hira Singh Ji's [role] was [vital]. In the newspapers, the call given to reach the Conference... generally the map of religious Diwan was drawn to attract Sangats...
For example, to reach the Fourth Conference at **Sialkot**, in 'Khalsa Samachar' of **7 March 1911**..."

'ਹੇ ਦੁਨੀਆ ਦੇ ਲੋਕੋ ! ਜਸ ਸੰਤਗੁਰੂ ਨੰ ਸਾਰੇ ਸੰਸਾਰ ਨੂੰ ਤਾਰਿਆ, ਮਨੁੱਖ ਤਾਂ ਕਿਤੇ ਰਜੇ
ਹੂ		 English (Meaning Translation)

...Guru Nanak Dev Ji came [under the shade of a Ber tree at Sialkot], this was also an ordinary Ber tree like others, but Satguru rested under it and touched it with his feet, [so] this Ber tree obtained the greatness of Satguru's glimpse. Today 400 years have passed, this Beri became **Ber Sahib**.
This Ber is now preaching to us - 'O lovers! I was a rooted-plant (Jarrh) and by seeing Satguru I reached this status. You being humans are still blank? Reethas (Soapnuts) became sweet by touching Satguru and you are still bitter? Being called Sikhs of Guru Nanak, you are still like others? Come! Touch the feet of Satguru and get softened...'
Hearing this explanation from his (Bhai Hira Singh's) mouth, "Dhan Guru Nanak, Dhan Guru Nanak" used to come out from every pore of loving Sikhs and their soul used to fall at Guru's feet and plead, 'Beloved Guru Nanak! Save us too.' At that time that Ber Sahib comes before eyes...
"Beloved Gursikhs! Now the Conference is at the same place where Ber Sahib is. There itself Bhai Hira Singh Ji will perform loving Kirtan and when facing Ber Sahib he will [sing] Satguru's... Come and reach in large numbers."

On **page 79** [of Golden Jubilee Book?] it is written:
"One used to take all kinds of benefit from Conferences. But the greatest spiritual benefit was from these Conferences. In religious Diwans, top Ragis of the Panth used to perform **Asa Di Var** and after that Katah of Sri Guru Granth Sahib Ji used to take place..."
In the open and vast grounds of religious Diwans, under canopies, Sangats used to gather in thousands and listen to nectar-like Kirtan, Katah and Lectures. **Sriman Sant Attar Singh** and **Bhai Hira Singh Ji** through Kirtan...
"O people of the world! That Satguru who saved the whole world... humans aside..."

Notes
- "Jarrh" refers to inanimate/vegetative life (immobile).
- "Reetha Mithay" refers to the Reetha Sahib incident where bitter soapnuts became sweet for Mardana.

ਆਈ ਬਾਣੀ ਦੇ ਉਚਾਰਨ ਨੇ ਸੰਗਤ ਨੂੰ ਰੱਬੀ ਰੰਗ ਵਿੱਚ ਰੰਗ ਦਿੱਤਾ ਤੇ ਸਾਰੇ ਪਾਸੀਂ ਮਗਨਤਾ
ਦੀ ਹਾਲਤ ਤਾਰੀ ਕਰ ਦਿੱਤੀ। ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਨੇ ਅੱਜ ਦੀ ਵਿਖਿਆ ਵਿੱਚ 'ਅਛੂਤ ਉਧਾਰ'
ਦੇ ਵਿਸ਼ੇ 'ਤੇ ਜ਼ੋਰ ਦਿੱਤਾ ਤੇ ਵਿਆਖਿਆ ਇਸ ਤੁਕ ਦੇ ਆਧਾਰ 'ਤੇ ਸ਼ੁਰੂ ਕੀਤੀ - “..ਜਿਸੁ
ਨਾਹੀ ਸੋ ਚੁਣਿ ਕਢੀਐ”।
ਬੜੀ ਮਧੁਰ ਧੁਨੀ ਨਾਲ ਅੱਗੇ-ਅੱਗੇ ਆਪ ਤੇ ਪਿੱਛੇ-ਪਿੱਛੇ ਸੰਗਤਾਂ ਨੂੰ ਸ਼ਬਦ ਪੜ੍ਹਾ ਕੇ ਐਨ
ਇਕਾਗਰ ਕਰ ਦਿੰਦੇ। ਕਦੇ-ਕਦੇ ਕੁਝ ਮਿੰਟਾਂ ਲਈ ਸਾਰੀ ਹਾਜ਼ਰੀ ਨੂੰ ਅੰਤਰ ਧਿਆਨ ਹੋ ਵਾਹਿਗਰ
ਅਪ੍ਰੈਲ 1917 ਵਿੱਚ ਦਸਵੀਂ ਕਾਨਫ਼ਰੰਸ ਲਾਹੌਰ ਦੇ ਮੌਕੇ 'ਤੇ ਜਦ ਮਲੇਰਕੋਟਲਾ ਦੇ ਨਵਾਬ
ਜ਼ੁਲਫ਼ਕਾਰ ਅਲੀ ਪੰਡਾਲ ਵਿੱਚ ਪੁੱਜੇ ਤੇ ਸਰਦਾਰ ਹਰਬੰਸ ਸਿੰਘ ਨੇ ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਦੀ ਜਾਣ-ਪਛਾਣ
ਕਰਾਈ, ਤਾਂ ਦਰਸ਼ਕਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਸ਼ਾਇਦ ਇਸ ਗੱਲ ਦੀ ਹੈਰਾਨੀ ਹੋਈ ਜੋ ਇਹ ਮੁਸਲਮਾਨ ਹੰਦੇ ਹੋਏ
ਇਸ ਕਾਨਫ਼ਰੰਸ ਵਿੱਚ ਕਿਸ ਤਰ੍ਹਾਂ? ਤਾਂ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਉੱਠ ਥਲੋਤੇ ਤੇ ਕਿਹਾ : ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ
ਦੇ ਹੀ ਬਜ਼ੁਰਗ ਸ਼ੇਰ ਖ਼ਾਨ ਨੇ ਨਵਾਬ ਨੂੰ ਆਖਿਆ ਸੀ -
ਗ. ਘੂਮ ਹੈ. ਣਾ ਇਆ ਹੈਂ... ਮੋਰੀਆਂ ਅੱਖਾਂ ਅੱਗੇ ਗੁਰੂ ਨਾਨਕ ਪਾਤਸ਼ਾਹ ਦੀ ਆਤਮ
7 ਅੰ ਪੰਜ ਨਰਾਨੀ' ਜਿਜਜੇ ਛਾਜ ।ਵਿਤਤ' “ਭਜ=੩੦ ੩ 0੬੮੦ ੧%੩੦ ੨੦੬੦ <੨-੨-੨ ੨.		 English (Meaning Translation)

...In the Pandal (tent), the sermon of religious life is given in the name of Kalgidhar, Guru Nanak...
Someone singing - "Kalgidhar Aabe-Hayat Pilate Hain" (Kalgidhar makes us drink the water of life/Amrit) and on this everyone crying...
The report of the religious Diwan of **15th Conference** which was held at **Patiala** in **April 1924**, is found on page 61 of Golden Jubilee Book as follows:
"[Kirtan] was to happen, so Sangats attracted by the pull of sitting in front of Bhai Sahib, reached the Diwan place at 3:30 AM itself.
Recitation of Bani colored the Sangat in divine color and a state of absorption prevailed on all sides. Bhai Sahib in today's discourse emphasized on the topic of **'Untouchable Upliftment'** (Achhut Udhar) and started explanation based on this line - *"...Jis Nahi So Chun Kadhiai"* (The one who doesn't have [Him/Naam] is picked and thrown out?).
With very sweet tune, reciting Shabad himself first and making Sangats recite after him, he would make them absolutely focused. Sometimes for a few minutes he would make the whole audience close eyes and meditate on Waheguru...
On the occasion of **10th Conference** at **Lahore** in **April 1917**, when **Nawab Zulfiqar Ali** of **Malerkotla** reached the Pandal and **Sardar Harbans Singh** introduced them, the audience might have been surprised that how is he in this conference being a Muslim? Then Bhai Hira Singh Ji stood up and said: 'His ancestor **Sher Khan** had said to the Nawab [of Sirhind] -
[Persian/Urdu couplet about Sher Khan's protest against killing Sahibzadas]...
Guru Nanak Patshah's [grace] is before my eyes..."

Notes
- "Achhut Udhar" refers to the movement for upliftment of untouchables/dalits.
- Nawab Sher Khan of Malerkotla famously raised the "Ha-Da-Naara" (Voice of Truth/Justice) against the bricking alive of younger Sahibzadas.

...are martyred in the battle of Bhangani and this man of God, **Sayyad [Budhu Shah]** considers himself blessed.
In Chamkaur, **Nabi Khan** and **Ghani Khan** made Sri Guru Ji sit on a cot, lifted him on their heads and gave the call, "Uch Da Pir Hai" (Here is the Pir of Uch).
With these incidents, what is the surprise in this meeting?'
(Khalsa Samachar, 12-4-1917)

From the first Conference held in **Gujranwala in 1908** till 17th... in 1926...
In the great successes [of Sikh Educational Conferences], Bhai Hira Singh Ji kept dedicating his selfless service to the Panth.
At the time of First Conference, the impact of his dedication on the Panth leaders was such that the service of **Asa Di Var Kirtan** on the first day of religious Diwan was entrusted to Bhai Hira Singh Ji, and then he was also chosen to offer the **Ardas** (prayer) for the successful completion of this conference in the Pandal.
He performed this Ardas in such impressive and heart-touching words that **'The Tribune'** newspaper made a special mention of it in its issue of **23.4.1908** and wrote:
"[English quote about the impressive prayer...]"

Some original words of this Ardas, which have been obtained from **Khalsa Youngmen's Magazine, May 1908, page 208**, are as follows:
"First of all... [thanksgiving for seva]...
...that came to your share and... this service with ability...
power to do...
In the appeal for funds... hearts [were melted]... stone hearts turned to wax...
Words used to... [pierce] the depths of heart...
rupees used to jump out from pockets...
For example..."

Notes
- "Pir of Uch" refers to the disguise Guru Gobind Singh Ji took to escape Machhiwara.

ਵੱ ਅਸੀਰਨੀ ਸ। ਉਸ ਸਮੇਂ ਰੂਰ ਦੇ ਹਸਪਤਾਲ ਵਿਚ ਡਾਕਟਰ ਹਰਾ ਸਮ ਜੀ ੇ ਜਰ

<< ਆ ਨਗਨ ਨੂੰ ਜਾਂਫਲੀ' ਹੈ ਚਰ ਸਾੱ/		 English (Meaning Translation)

**17th Conference which was held in May 1926 in Lahore**, was the last [conference] for Bhai Hira Singh Ji. At that time **Dr. Hira Singh Ji** was under treatment in **Kasur** hospital and could not be present physically. But he sent a written message through his younger brother **Bhai Pardhan Singh Ji** to Lahore, instructing him to read this last message of his in the Conference. Hearing this message hearts were moved and when finally this Slok written [in it] was read:
*Pankhi Chale Disavri Kirpa Sufal Falant ||*
(The bird flies to foreign lands; by Grace, it bears good fruit.)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 1376)
Then everyone's eyes became wet.

**Giani Sant Singh Kamalia**, who had read out this message, describing the glory of Kirtan in Guru's house, in very learned and loving words, expressed the virtue of accompanying those attached to Guru Nanak's hem and said: "Bhai Mardana was extremely dear to Guru Nanak Dev Ji. The reason for this as written in **Nanak Prakash**, is as follows:
[Poetry quote: He plays the Rebeck... pleasing to my mind...]
Therefore, it is the duty of all of us to support those attached to Guru Nanak Dev Ji...
**700 Sikhs** gave five hundred rupees each for this Conference and became Life Fellows...
Master, on this many gentlemen announced becoming Life Fellows right there!
This was his love with the Conference which lasted till the last breaths.

**18th Conference which was held in April 1927 in Rawalpindi**, after Bhai Sahib's departure to Sach Khand...

Notes
- "Disavri" means foreign lands/directions.

ਫਿਰੂਕੇ ਦਾ ਸਕੂਲ ਚੂੰਕਿ ਨਿਰੋਲ ਆਪ ਦੀ ਜ਼ਾਤੀ ਮਿਹਨਤ ਤੇ ਮਾਇਕ ਕੁਰਬਾਨੀ ਨਾਲ
ਵਜੂਦ ਵਿੱਚ ਆਇਆ ਸੀ, ਇਸ ਲਈ ਉਸ ਦਾ ਉਚੇਚਾ ਵਰਣਨ ਕਰਨਾ ਜ਼ਰੂਰੀ ਹੈ।
_ ਖ਼ਾਲਸਾ ਹਾਈ ਸਲੂਲ ਫਿਰੂਕਾ : ਇਹ ਸਕੂਲ ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਗਿਣਵੇ ਖ਼ਾਲਸਾ ਸਕੂਲਾਂ ਵਿੱਚੋਂ ਇੱਕ ਹੈ,		 English (Meaning Translation)

When efforts for educational progress started in the Panth and Khalsa Schools or Colleges started opening... then Bhai Hira Singh Ji offered his services for every institution and collected money and presented it. In this regard **Bhai Sahib Bhai Vir Singh Ji** wrote in **Khalsa Samachar** of **30 August 1951**, "...Almost every High School that was built has a share of his earnings. At the time of building of every Ashram (institution), he used to perform Ardas of his one or two months' income and give all offerings received during that time to that Ashram. **Faruka School** was almost entirely the fruit of that enthusiastic lover's labor. We know personally that for years he contributed to the success of this Ashram from his hard-earned income...
He was among the old and founding servants of **Central Khalsa Orphanage Amritsar**, **Khalsa College Amritsar** and **Orphanage Gharjakh (Gujranwala)**.

At **11th Sikh Educational Conference** at **Gujranwala**, for **Sri Guru Nanak Khalsa College**, in **1919**, he appealed for **forty thousand rupees** in very simple but heart-attracting sentences, because 12th class could only open there if this amount was collected. And on this appeal, **30-35 thousand cash** and **eight thousand rupees** as pledges were collected within minutes. Besides offering all the money that came on the harmonium (Vaja), Bhai Sahib also dedicated his one month's service to the college. This was just a sample of the effect of his appeal.

In appreciation of his services rendered in the educational field in **1915**, a certificate was sent to him by **[Lt. Governor of Punjab?]**, some words of which were as follows:
*"...I have heard much of you, that you have... shown great worth in the cause of education, this Sanad (Certificate) is given to you in recognition of your value."*

**Khalsa High School Faruka:** Since the school of Faruka came into existence purely by his personal effort and financial sacrifice, it is necessary to describe it specially.
This school is one of those few Khalsa schools...

Notes
- "Vaja" refers to Harmonium.

...[The Patwari said], "Baba! [By God] No! Allah has sent you as some angel. Your Kalam (speech/Kirtan) has melted me... Blessed is the mother who gave birth to you."
...Upon the settlement of Land matter, a wave of happiness ran through the Sangats.
Congratulations were received by Bhai Sahib from all sides. On the other side, **S. Sundar Singh [Majithia]**, **Bhai Sahib Bhai Arjan Singh Ji Bagrian** also reached. Since the Diwan place was near the road, ... Sangat ran and met them ahead and Sardar Sahib reached the Diwan place with the Sangat, where he was requested to perform the service of Jathedar (preside over), but Sriman Ji (Sardar Majithia) in humble words stated the purpose of his coming for ten minutes and sat in the Tabya (attendance) of Guru Granth Sahib Ji. The entire Hindu-Muslim Sangat was feeling blissful seeing the holy saintly nature of Sriman Ji.

After that, performing Ardas, the **Foundation Stone** was laid by **Singh Sahib Jathedar S. Sundar Singh Ji Majithia** with his lucky hands.

Among the poems read at that time, the following poems by **Kavi Santokh Singh**...:
[Poem roughly translates to praising the event, the foundation stone laying, and the glory of the school]
"...A school inside which beautiful education will be given, where Sikh children will study..."

Notes
- "Tabya" refers to the position behind Guru Granth Sahib Ji, waving the Chaur Sahib.

ਦੇ ਮੈਨੇਜਰ ਥਾਪੇ-ਗਏ ਤੇ ਇਹ ਸੇਵਾ ਆਪਣੇ ਉਮਰ ਪ੍ਰਯੰਤ ਯੋਗਤਾ ਨਾਲ ਨਿਭਾਈ। ਆਪ ਸੁਲਝੇ
ਹੋਏ, ਦੂਰ ਅੰਦੇਸ਼ ਤੇ ਦਾਨੇ ਪੁਰਸ਼ ਸਨ। ਆਪ ਦਾ ਚੇਹਰਾ ਜਥੇ ਵਾਲਾ ਸੀ ਤੇ ਆਪ ਚੰਗੇ ਪ੍ਰਬੰਧਕ
ਸਨ। ਸਹਿਨ ਸ਼ਕਤੀ ਬਹੁਤ ਸੀ ਤੇ ਟੀਕਾ ਟਿੱਪਣੀ ਦੇ ਬਾਵਜੂਦ ਠੰਢੇ ਜਿਗਰੇ ਨਾਲ ਕੰਮ ਕਰੀ
ਜਾਂਦੇ ਸਨ। ਆਪ ਨੂੰ ਆਪ ਦੇ ਭਰਾਤਾ, ਭਾਈ ਹਰਸਾ.ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ, ਜੋ ਪਹਿਲੋਂ ਫਿਰੁਕੇ ਹਿਕਮਤ
ਕਰਦੇ ਸਨ ਤੇ ਫਿਰ ਲਾਇਲਪੁਰ ਜਾ ਕੇ ਮਸ਼ਹੂਰ ਹੋ ਗਏ ਸਨ, ਨੇ ਆਪਣਾ ਕੰਮ ਧੁੱਤਰਾਂ (ਭਾਈ
ਨਿਧਾਨ ਸਿੰਘ, ਜਗਤ ਸਿੰਘ) ਦੇ ਹਵਾਲੇ ਕਰਕੇ, ਫਿਰੂਕੇ 67 ਮਹੀਨੇ ਰਹਿ ਕੇ ਭਾਈ ਸ਼ਾਮ ਸਿੰਘ

[Poem contd.] "...Guru Himself will show Grace..."
...Only two-three rooms were ready when classes were shifted there.
It got affiliated [to University?]. In **January 1911**, recognition was received from Education Department and in **1921** High [School] classes started and in **1924** the first batch was sent for Matriculation examination, of which all students passed.

**Manager Bhai Sham Singh:**
Bhai Sham Singh Ji was earlier a Patwari in **Jhawarian**. Around **1903**, he met Bhai Hira Singh Ji and when preparations for Faruka School started, he came into the selection of Bhai Hira Singh Ji's companions. Upon formation of School Committee, being an educated gentleman, he was appointed Manager of the school and he performed this service with ability throughout his life. He was a sorted, farsighted and wise person. His face was like a Jathedar (leader) and he was a good administrator. He had great tolerance and despite criticism used to work with a cool heart.
His brother **Bhai Harsa Singh Ji**, who earlier used to practice Hikmat (medicine) in Faruka and then became famous in Lyallpur, handed over his work to his sons (**Bhai Nidhan Singh, Jagat Singh**) and stayed in Faruka for 6-7 months to teach Bhai Sham Singh the work of [Hikmat/Management?]. So his work also started running and school work also started running [smoothly?]. He passed away in **1946** after living an age of 80 years.

**Facing Financial Crisis:**
To start the school was easy but [to run it was difficult]...
[Funds] were needed... not being able to bear expenses... money had to be collected from outside...

Notes
- "Hikmat" refers to traditional Unani/Ayurvedic medical practice.

ਵਜਾ ਫ਼ਜ਼ਲ ਅਜ਼ਨਨ ਲੰ ਸੋਵਾਂ - 6		 English (Meaning Translation)

...It is known that from laying the foundation stone till the completion of the building [Bhai Sahib] served the school day and night.

At the **6th Sikh Educational Conference** which was held in **Ambala** in **March 1913**, in its Pandal, Bhai Hira Singh Ji took a pledge that as long as **twenty thousand rupees** are not collected for the fixed fund of this school, till then...
In **Khalsa Samachar** of **30-9-1913**, Bhai Sahib clarified about this pledge and written that "My pledge is of **30 thousand** and not 20 thousand... because till this 20 thousand is collected, 10 thousand is also needed for running expenses..."
In this pledge, not only was it that he will not use the money received during Kirtan for his personal use, but also that until this pledge is fulfilled, whenever he would come to Faruka for some school work or committee meeting, he would not step into his own house, but would come and stay in a **Gufa** (Cave/Underground room) which he had earlier built for **Sant Attar Singh Ji** near the school outside.
To the extent that once when there was some trouble in the house, **Bhai Sham Singh Ji** called him by telegram but he did not enter the house.
This pledge was fulfilled after about **16 months** in **Kohat** and the Sangat of Kohat offered **2800 rupees** instead of the fixed 1800 rupees.
(Khalsa Advocate, 2 October 1926)

**Boarding House, Gurdwara and Hospital:**
The number of students had started increasing day by day. With the settlement of **Sargodha Bar**, Sikh population in Chakks (villages) had increased and then in the whole district apart from one Government School Bhera, there was no other school.
[Students] had started coming... and the issue of their residence became important. For this sake, near the school **thirty bighas** of land was purchased from Muslim landlords. For this much effort had to be made because according to **Land Alienation Act**, non-cultivator could not buy land of cultivator. To settle this matter Bhai Sahib had to [work hard/face difficulty]. Finally success was achieved and a plan of a large Boarding House was made in which buildings of magnificent Gurdwara, Hospital and Girls School [were included].
On this project large expense was to come and for this Bhai Hira Singh Ji started effort and after labor of three-four years in **1916**...

Notes
- "Intkal Arazi Act" refers to the Punjab Land Alienation Act of 1900 which restricted sale of land from agricultural tribes to non-agricultural tribes. Bhai Sahib likely faced hurdles if he wasn't classified as an agriculturist "Jat".

ਰੁਮਰਡਿੰ ਹਸਪਤਾਲ ਤੇ ਇੱਕ ਗੁਰਦੁਆਰੇ ਦੀਆਂ ਇਮਾਰਤਾਂ ਤਿਆਰ ਹੋ ਗਈਆਂ।
ਬਾਕੀ ਦੀ ਜ਼ਮੀਨ ਵਿੱਚ ਖੇਡਾਂ ਤੇ ਵੱਡੇ ਮੈਦਾਨਾਂ ਤੋਂ ਇਲਾਵਾ ਇੱਕ ਖੂਹ ਲਗਵਾਇਆ ਗਿਆ,

ਟੈਕਨੀਕਲ ਸਕੂਲ ਅੰਬਾਲਾ, ਨੇ ਸਾਡੀ ਪੁੱਛ ਦੇ ਉੱਤਰ ਵਿੱਚ ਇਸ ਤਰ੍ਹਾਂ ਬਿਆਨ ਕੀਤਾ ਹੈ :
'ਆਪਣੇ ਇਲਾਕੇ ਦੇ ਇਕੋ ਇਕ ਮਿਡਲ ਸਕੂਲ ਨੌਸ਼ਹਿਰਾ ਜ਼ਿਲਾ ਸਰਗੋਧਾ ਤੋਂ ਛੇ ਜਮਾਤਾਂ
ਪਾਸ ਕਰਕੇ ਮਿਸ਼ਨ ਸਕੂਲ ਗੁਜਰਾਤ ਜਾ ਦਾਖ਼ਲ ਹੋਇਆ, ਜਿੱਥੇ ਮੇਰੇ ਵੱਡੇ ਭਰਾ ਜੀ ਓਵਰਸੀਅਰ
ਲੱਗੇ ਹੋਏ ਸਨ। ਪਹਿਲੇ ਹੀ ਇਮਤਿਹਾਨ ਵਿੱਚ ਮੇਰੇ ਫ਼ਸਟ ਆਉਣ ਪਰ ਸਕੂਲ ਦੇ ਨੋਕ
ਹੰਡਮਾਸਟਰ ਨੇ ਮੈਨੂੰ ਸੱਦ ਕੇ ਸ਼ਾਬਾਸ਼ ਦਿੱਤੀ ਤੇ ਨਾਲ ਹੀ ਧਾਰਮਿਕ ਉਸਤਾਦ ਨੂੰ ਤਕੀਦ ਕੀਤੀ
ਕਿ ਮੇਰਾ ਖ਼ਾਸ ਸ਼ਿਆਲ ਰੱਖੋ। ਉਸ ਦਿਨ ਤੋਂ ਉਹ ਖ਼ਿਆਲ ਰੱਖਣ ਲੱਗੇ ਕਿ ਮੈਂ ਕਿਸੇ ਤਰ੍ਹਾਂ ਲਾਲਚ
ਯਾ ਪਿਆਰ ਨਾਲ ਈਸਾਈ ਬਣ ਜਾਵਾਂ। ਈਸਾਈ ਮਤ ਦੀਆਂ ਕਿਤਾਬਾਂ ਮੈਨੂੰ ਮੁਫ਼ਤ ਮਿਲਣ
ਸਿਰ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਨੇ ਘਰ ਸੱਦ ਕੇ ਧਰਮ ਬਦਲਣ ਲਈ ਪ੍ਰੇਰਿਆ। ਮੈਂ ਆ ਕੇ ਆਪਣੇ ਇੱਕ
ਵਡਾ ਫਰੂਕਾ ਵਿੱਚ ਮਾਲਸਾ ਸਕੂਲ ਹੈ ਜੋ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੀ ਸਰਪੁਸਤੀ
ਤਰਹ ੈ ਤੇ ਇੰਕ ਆਦਰਸ਼ਕ ਸਕੂਲ ਹੈ। ਰ ਰ੍‌
ਗਲ ਨਾਲਾ ਜ਼ਰ ਦੇਣ 'ਤੇ ਮਨੂੰ ਸਰਟੀਫ਼ਿਕੇਟ ਮਿਲਿਆ ਤੇ ਮੈਂ 1918 ਵਿੱਚ ਅਠਵੀਂ
99 - ਔਲਕ ਲੋਨ `-----------
( ਫੋੱਡੋਤੇ ਹੂੰ ਹੁੰ] ਤ0 ਡੇਲ		 English (Meaning Translation)

...buildings of Boarding, Hospital and one Gurdwara were completed.
In the remaining land, apart from sports and big grounds, a **Well** was installed, from which arrangements were made for growing vegetables etc. for Langar in the remaining land.

**Education and Religious Instruction:**
From the beginning, it was the effort of organizers that staff appointed should be most capable and of religious inclination. Due to this, school results always came out good. Along with studies, special attention was paid to religious education, Kirtan, Paath and Gurbani.
It was Bhai Hira Singh Ji's own rule that whenever he returned home from preaching tours outside, he would first mark his attendance in the school! He would give [instruction/lecture] to the senior class. His great desire was that students passing out from this school should be samples of Sikhism and a mission in themselves.
[Due to this influence] students used to come out becoming firm Gursikhs. Even now students educated at Faruka are met who have the influence of Bhai Sahib's teachings and they [recite Gurbani] while sitting and standing...

Hearing this fame, many students from far off places used to come to take admission in Faruka. For example, **Sardar Sahib Lakhmi Singh**, Retired Principal Government Technical School Ambala, has stated in answer to our query:
"After passing six classes from the only Middle School of my area **Naushehra** District Sargodha, I took admission in **Mission School Gujrat**, where my elder brother was working as overseer. Upon coming First in the very first exam, the pious Headmaster of the school called me and gave Shabaash (praise) and also instructed the religious teacher to take special care of me. From that day they started taking care that I should become Christian by some greed or love. Christian religious books were given to me for free... Headmaster Sahib called me home and persuaded me to change religion. I came and [told] one of my [relatives?]...
[He said] 'There is a Khalsa School in **Faruka** which is under the patronage of Bhai Sahib Bhai Hira Singh Ji... and is an ideal school.'
...I got the certificate and in **1918** passed eighth class..."

Notes
- "Overseer" is a rank in engineering/public works.

੪ ੮--ਫੜ ਫ਼		 English (Meaning Translation)

[Sardar Lakhmi Singh continues]: "...which was longing for his glimpse, got cooled. Sunday he came and Kirtan started at 4 AM in school Gurdwara and I was the first one to be present. In young age itself that color of Kirtan climbed which shines till now."
In this school, apart from free education to a large number of orphan and destitute children, free Langar and books etc. were also provided.
In this regard a letter from a gentleman **Mr. Johar** was published in **'The Tribune'** of **17 August 1917** addressed to the Editor, which the same newspaper repeated in its '75 years ago' column on **17 August 1992**. For the interest of readers, the exact words of that letter are given below:

*The Tribune, 17 August 1917*
*To The Editor,*
*THE KHALSA HIGH SCHOOL FARUKA*
*Sir - It is doubtful whether even the Sikh public are aware of the existence of a high school in the Shahpur District, fed and nurtured by the sole energy and the spirit of service of Bhai Hira Singh Ragi...*
*...has added a new chapter to the history of the Sikh educational activities...*
*...not from wealthy treasuries... but he has managed to raise 50,000 rupees...*
**(Johar)**

About [the school] always good opinion continued to be published. As a sample, in the **1922-23 Report** it is recorded as follows:
"**Khalsa High School Faruka (Shahpur)**
This school is the result of the labor of Bhai Hira Singh Ji Ragi. School has its own building. Boarding House is very big. There is space for **170 students**. Nearby the school is **30 Bighas of land** which is cultivated. Along with it a **Dispensary** is built. **Gurdwara** is separate, where all boarders mark daily attendance and recite **Jaap Sahib** together. Every Sunday they perform **Asa Di Var** with Vaja-Jori (Harmonium-Tabla). There are **328 students**. Number of Hindu Muslim students is almost equal to Sikh students. Muslims also compete with Sikh students in reading Punjabi and memorizing Sakhis.
In this school there is arrangement to give **free education** up to Tenth class to **orphan children**. Till today **12 students** have passed Entrance (Matric) under this scheme and right now are earning their livelihood. The Committee has made arrangement for assistance of **30 such children**..."

Notes
- "Vaja-Jori" means Harmonium and Tabla pair.
- "Jaap Sahib" is a morning prayer by Guru Gobind Singh Ji.

ਦੇ ਲੰਗਰ ਲਈ ਗੁਰਮੁਖ ਪਿਅਰੇ ਭਾਈ ਅਮਰ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਗੰਢ ਨੇ 6 ਮੁਰੱਬੇ (150 ਦ ) ਜ਼ਮੀਨ

'ਫਿਰੂਕਾ ਸਕੂਲ ਮੇਰੀ ਪਿਆਰੀ ਵਸਤ ਤੇ ਪੰਥ ਗੁਰੂ ਦਾ ਮਾਲ ਹੈ। ਸਰਬ ਸੰਗਤਾਂ ਜੋ ਇਸਨੂੰ ਵਧਾਣ
ਫੁਲਾਣ ਵਿੱਚ ਸਹਾਈ ਹੋਸਨ, ਗੁਰੂ ਕੀਆਂ ਖ਼ੁਸ਼ੀਆਂ ਪ੍ਰਾਪਤ ਕਰਸਨ। ਖ਼ਾਸ ਕਰ ਸਕੂਲ ਸਬੰਧੀ

ਨ ਟਰ 5੪		 English (Meaning Translation)

...For the Langar of [Orphans], Gurmukh Pyare **Bhai Amar Singh Ji Gandha** offered **6 Murabbas** (150 acres) land from his Chitraur land to the school... this transfer was registered in the name of the school in **1922-23**.

**Servant's Love Lasted till the End:**
Bhai Sahib departed for Gurpuri (passed away) on **2 September 1926**. His passing caused an unbearable loss to the whole Panth generally and to Faruka School [specifically].
In the speech **Bhai Sham Singh Ji** gave with a heavy heart at his Bhog (last rites), the estimate of his grief can be made from just one sentence. He said, "People while condoling me say 'Your arm is broken', but I say my whole body is gone, I am left as just one arm."

Bhai Sahib had immense love for Faruka School. In his **Will** [he wrote]:
"Faruka School is my beloved object and property of Guru Panth. All Sangats who will help in its growth and blossoming will obtain Guru's pleasure. Especially regarding school, the running of Hospital and building of beautiful Gurdwara, these are my strong desires which are yet in between (unfinished), Satguru's Rangeela Panth will fulfill them."
Committee had been formed and Bhai Sham Singh Ji was performing the service of Manager since then.

**After passing of Bhai Hira Singh Ji:** [School continued...]

**Re-establishment:**
The Partition of **1947** [destroyed] the vast belongings of Faruka School...
...Establishment of Khalsa High School 1908...
...Selfless and unique service of Panth Jewel Bhai Sahib Bhai Hira Singh Ji Ragi...
...was in (Pakistan).
[The buildings were left in Pakistan but the spirit crossed the border.]

Notes
- "Murabba" is approx 25 acres. Bequest of 6 Murabbas is a huge donation.

ਇਸ ਬੂਟੇ ਦੀਆਂ` ਜੜ੍ਹਾਂ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਭਾਈ' ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ' ਦੇ ਸਿਦਕ ਅਤੇ ਤਪ ਦਾ ਬਲ
ਸੀ, ਇਸ ਲਈ ਇਹ ਇਤਨਾ ਵੱਡਾ ਬੂਚਾਲ ਬਰਦਾਸ਼ਤ ਕਰ ਗਿਆ। ਸਤਿਗੁਰਾਂ ਨੇ ਬਖ਼ਸ਼ਿਸ਼
ਕੀਤੀ ਅਤੇ ਸੌਨ !949 ਵਿੱਚ ਇਹ ਫਿਰ ਅੰਬਾਲੇ ਛਾਉਣੀ ਵਿਖੇ ਪਿਆ। ਕੁਝ ਹੀ' ਸਾਲਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ
ਉਹੀ ਪੁਰਾਣੀ ਭਾਐ ਆ ਗਈ। ਅੱਜ ਖ਼ਾਲਸਾ ਪੰਥ ਦਾ ਇਹ ਆਸ਼ਰਮ ਮੁੜ ਚੜ੍ਹਦੀਆਂ ਕਲਾਂ
ਵਿੱਚ ਹੈ। ਸਕੂਲ ਦਾ ਸਥਾਨ ਬਦਲ ਗਿਆ ਹੈ, ਇਸਨੇ ਜਾਮਾ ਵੀ ਨਵਾਂ ਪਹਿਨ ਲਿਆ ਹੈ ਪਰ
ਇਸ ਦੀ ਸੁਰ ਵਿੱਚ ਉਹੀ ਭਾਈ` ਸਾਹਿਬ ਦੀ ਲੈਅ ਹੈ। ਇਸਦੀ ਹੋਂਦ ਇਸਦੇ ਅਸਤਿਤਵ ਦਾ
ਕਾਰਣ ਉਹੀ ਹੈ - 'ਵਿਦਿਆ ਵੀਚਾਰੀ ਤਾ ਪਰਉਪਕਾਰੀ”।
ਸਾਡੀ ਅਰਦਾਸ ਹੈ ਕਿ ਗੁਰੂ ਗੋਬਿੰਦ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੀ ਇਹ ਫੁਲਵਾੜੀ ਹਮੇਸ਼ਾਂ ਇੰਵ ਹੀ ਖਿੜ੍ਹੀ
ਰਹੇ। ਇਸ ਸਕੂਲ ਨੂੰ ਕਦੇ ਤੋਟਾ ਨਾ ਆਵੇ ਅਤੇ ਸਾਡੇ ਮੁਲਕ ਦੇ ਪੁੰਗਰ ਰਹੇ ਨੌਜੁਆਨ ਇਸ
ਪੁਨੀਤ ਸੰਸਥਾ ਵਿੱਚ 'ਸ਼ੁਭ ਕਰਮਨ ਤੇ ਕਬਹੂੰ ਨਾ ਟਰੋਂ' ਦਾ ਨਾਅਰਾ ਲਗਾਉਂਦੇ ਵਿੱਦਿਆ ਗ੍ਰਹਿਣ
ਕਰਨ ਤੇ ਫਿਰ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਛੱਕ ਕੇ ਤਿਆਰ-ਬਰ-ਤਿਆਰ ਸਮਾਜ ਵਿੱਚ ਦਾਖ਼ਲ ਹੋਣ।
ਸਕੂਲ ਦੀ ਮੌਜੂਦਾ ਹਾਲਤ : ਇਸ ਸਬੰਧ ਵਿੱਚ ਇੱਕ ਪੁੱਛ ਦੇ ਉੱਤਰ ਵਿੱਚ ਫਿਰੂਕੇ ਦੇ
ਵਰਤਮਾਨ ਮੁਖੀ ਮੀਆਂ ਸ਼ੇਰ ਮੁਹੰਮਦ ਕਲੀਆਰ ਦੇ 21.10.1976 ਦੇ ਪੱਤਰ ਦੇ ਕੁਝ ਲਫ਼ਜ਼ ਇਸ
ਪ੍ਰਕਾਰ ਹਨ :
'ਖ਼ਾਲਸਾ ਹਾਈ ਸਕੂਲ, ਉਸਦਾ ਬੋਅਰਡਿੰਗ ਹਾਉਸ ਤੇ ਡਿਸਪੈਨਸਰੀ ਦੀਆਂ ਵਿਸ਼ਾਲ ਅਤੇ
ਰੈ ਕੀਤੀ ਅਤੇ ਅਜਿਹੀ ਸੰਸਥਾ ਬਣਾਈ ਜਿਸ ਵਿੱਚ ਗ਼ਰੀਬ ਅਮੀਰ ਤੇ ਹਰ ਮਜ਼ਹਬ ਤੇ ਜਾਤੀ
ਦੇ ਬੱਚੇ ਅੱਜ ਤਕ ਤਾਲੀਮ ਪਾ ਰਹੇ ਹਨ। ਜੋ ਸਿੱਖਿਆ ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਨੂੰ ਇਥੋਂ ਮਿਲਦੀ ਹੈ, ਉਸ ਨਾਲ
ਉਹ ਸਹੀ ਤੇ ਸਿੱਧੇ ਰਸਤੇ 'ਤੇ ਚਲ ਕੇ ਆਪਣਾ ਜੀਵਨ ਬਤੀਤ ਕਰਦੇ ਹਨ। ਇਸ ਸਕੂਲ ਦਾ
ਬਾਨੀ ਭਾਵੇਂ ਨਹੀਂ ਰਿਹਾ ਪੁਰ ਉਸਦੀ ਪਵਿੱਤਰ ਯਾਦ ਸਾਡੇ ਕੋਲ ਹੈ ਤੇ ਰਮੇਸ਼ਾਂ ਰਹੇਗੀ। ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ
ਇਮਾਰਤਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਸਾਨੂੰ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੀ ਰੂਹ ਨਜ਼ਰ ਆਉਂਦੀ ਹੈ ...।		 English (Meaning Translation)

...handing over [magnificent] buildings to Pakistan, the soul of the school crossed the border.
Roots of this plant were watered by the strength of **Bhai Hira Singh Ji's** faith and penance, that is why it could withstand such a huge earthquake [of Partition]. Satguru blessed and in **1949** it was re-established at **Ambala Cantt**. In a few years, the same old glory returned. Today this Ashram of Khalsa Panth is again in Chardi Kala (High Spirits).
The location of the school has changed, it has worn a new body, but in its tune is the same rhythm of Bhai Sahib. The reason for its existence and survival is the same - *"Vidiya Vichari Tan Parupkari"* (True learning leads to altruism).

It is our prayer that this garden of Guru Gobind Singh Ji always blooms like this. May this school never face any lack and the budding youth of our country receiving education in this holy institution, raising the slogan of *"Shubh Karman Te Kabhoon Na Taron"* (May I never shy away from good deeds), enter the society as Tyar-Bar-Tyar (Ready) Singhs.

**Present Condition of School:**
In this regard, in response to a query, some words from the letter dated **21.10.1976** of **Mian Sher Muhammad Kaliyar**, the present Head of Faruka [Pakistan] are as follows:
"Khalsa High School, its Boarding House and Dispensary's vast...
...and built such an institution in which children of poor and rich and every religion and caste are receiving education till today. With the education they get from here, they live their life walking on true and straight path. Although the founder of this school is not here, his holy memory is with us and will always remain. In these buildings we see the spirit of Bhai Hira Singh Ji..."

Notes
- "Kalyar/Kaliyar" is a Muslim surname/clan.

ੇਸਾਧਾਰੀ ਸਿੱਖ, ਦਸਤਾਰ ਦੀ ਬਜਾਏ ਇੰਕ ਪਗੜੀ ਵਰਗੀ ਟੋਪੀ ਸਿਰ ਉਤੇ ਰੱਖ ਲੈਂਦੇ
ਤੇੜ ਸਭ ਦੇ ਧੋਤੀਆਂ ਸਨ ਤੇ ਤੰਬਾਕੂ ਢੀ ਪਰੀ ਵਰਗੀ ਟੋਪੀ ਸਿਰ ਉਤੇ ਰੱਖ ਦਰ
&% - ਆ ਲੋ `--------------		 English (Meaning Translation)

**How Sikhi reached Sindh and why it declined:**
There is no doubt that in difficult and tough times of the Panth, Saints and Mahants of **Udasi Samparda** kept Sikhi alive and maintained the service of Sikh Gurdwaras and shrines. Wherever Udasis went, they gave sermon of Sikh religion to the locals and by installing **Sri Guru Granth Sahib**, established a source of Gurmat preaching.

In Sindh also, Udasis established many Deras and preached Sikhi. Then Khalsas took this preaching forward, as a result of which thousands of Sehajdhari loving Sikhs were created in Sindh and they made their sons keep Kesh.
But then such a time came that due to lack of preaching, Sikhi in Sindh became loose/diluted. There was no such organization of Khalsa which could keep the chain of preaching running.
The result was that the servitors of those very Gur-Asthans started falling from Sikhi. They started taking waves of Charas, Tobacco and Cannabis (Bhang).

In the issue of **Khalsa Samachar dated 12 August 1908**, it is mentioned that once at **Garhi Yasin**, at **Baba Ganga Ram's** place, when some Singhs went for Darshan, ahead Rababis were performing Kirtan but alongside many people were unhesitatingly smoking Hookahs. Upon asking of those Singhs, Hookahs were stopped. But in Sindh it had become a common custom that tobacco was smoked in Gur-Asthans. The only lack remaining was that Hookah had not reached inside the room of Guru Granth Sahib.

Then Yogis, Bairagis and Sanyasis caused even more damage. These people themselves smoked tobacco and were clean-shaven (Rund-Mund). Seeing the Sikh faith in Sindh, these people installed Guru Granth Sahib in their Deras but along with it placed idols of their deities. In this way started misleading Sikhs away from Sikhi. In Sindh, Sadhus had great respect, whichever garb they belonged to. All men and women blindly followed these Sadhus...
So slowly reading Gurmukhi was abandoned. Then whatever word of Guru Granth Sahib they used to hear in morning was abandoned...
Condition became so pathetic that **Keshadhari Sikhs**, instead of Dastar (Turban), used to keep a Pagri-like Topi (Cap) on their head... and Dhoti on loin...

Notes
- "Rund-Mund" refers to shaven heads/faces.
- "Garhi Yasin" is a town in Sindh (now Pakistan).

#ੱਥਾ ਦਾ ਪਰਚਾਨ - 6?		 English (Meaning Translation)

...[Sikhi] was given up. In this way, slowly the Sikhi of Sindh kept falling.

**Preaching of Sikhi in Sindh from scratch:**
Fortunately, when **Sardar Sadhu Singh** of Forest Department, who was posted towards **Balochistan**, saw these conditions in the beginning of the twentieth century, he challenged **Chief Khalsa Diwan** for preaching in Sindh.
On this, Diwan started sending preaching Jathas from **1904**. In these Jathas **Sardar Sundar Singh Majithia**, **Sardar Harbans Singh Attari**, **Professor Jodh Singh** and **Bhai Hira Singh**...
**Bhai Bhag Singh Hira Singh Ji's Jatha** used to tour Sindh for about two months in winters every year and return after sounding the drum of Guru Nanak everywhere. In the Deras mentioned above, reaching every such place they would preach against the desecration of Gur-Dhams. This preaching put quite a halt [to bad practices] and reform happened in Deras.

Upon the publication of the above conditions about **Garhi Yasin**, a special Jatha was sent by the Diwan in **December 1909** in which **Professor Jodh Singh** and **Bhai Bhag Singh, Bhai Hira Singh Ji** were included. Hookah and Tobacco were stopped in the Dera and pledges were taken from Mahants for the future.

Although after some years Diwan's Jathas stopped going, **Bhai Bhag Singh Hira Singh Ji's Jatha** continued to tour for about two months every winter. The preaching of Sikhi done in these tours is hard to find a parallel. Thousands of people were made to quit Hookah, Tobacco, Alcohol and Charas. Sikh Gurdwaras were established and the lost faith in Sikhi was brought back. Hundreds of families took Amrit and became Tyar-Bar-Tyar Singhs.

**S. Tirath Singh Lalvani** from **Castophone** wrote in his letter of 13.12.1961 from **London**:
"[English Quote: ...Bhai Hira Singh's... contribution... great awakening...]"

In **1967**, the author had the good fortune of meeting **Diwan Parmanand Singh Ji Vakil** (1883-1971) when he had come to **Dagshai** to spend some summer days with his daughter **Bibi Nanki Ji**. Gurmukh Darshani Singh, stroking his white long beard said, "This gift was given to me by **Bhai Hira Singh Ji**." And with this he narrated the whole story of how he was a Parmanand who was very far from Sikhi Mandal and then how he became a Tyar-Bar-Tyar Singh and how now he is a lover of Naam Bani, waking at Amrit Vela and spending time in Simran...

Notes
- "Castophone" - likely a company or organization name associated with S. Tirath Singh.

? - ਨਲਕੇ ਗੰਨਾ		 English (Meaning Translation)

...He was a close acquaintance of the famous scholar and writer **Sardar Gobind Singh Mansukhani**. Along with this, he [mentioned] names of many other Gurmukhs whom Bhai Hira Singh Ji awakened and by administering Amrit made them Tyar-Bar-Tyar Singhs. Some names that Das (servant/author) remembers are - **Diwan Hira Singh**...

**Wave of Sikh Preaching in Burma:**
In **1919**, Bhai Hira Singh Ji got the opportunity to go to **Burma** with his Jatha, when he was invited by the Sangat of **Mandalay** to reach the Diwan. Here the Sikh population was second only to **Rangoon** and Sangats from other towns of Upper Burma also reached the Diwan in large numbers.
Here for the first time a **Nagar Kirtan** (Procession) was taken out with royal grandeur (Shah-i-Jalal). This was a new kind of program at that place, seeing which the residents there were highly impressed and attended the Diwan congregations in large numbers.
Great preaching of Gurmat took place.
On the last day of the Diwan, Bhai Sahib made a strong appeal for the establishment of a **Khalsa School** and by collecting thousands of rupees laid the foundation of the school.
...
[Invitation from Rangoon]
Accepting the invitation of Burma Sangats, [they went to] Rangoon...
[Nagar Kirtan was taken out with Guru Granth Sahib's Sawari...]

Notes
- "Mandalay" and "Rangoon" are major cities in Burma (Myanmar).

**Abbottabad (Hazara):**
In the **Hazara District** of Frontier Province (now Pakistan), **Abbottabad** is a prominent town and military cantonment. From here a road goes to Kashmir via **Muzaffarabad (Domel)** and another reaches **Murree** via Galiyan (hills). **Mansehra** and... are beautiful places from Abbottabad, whose sceneries are very captivating. Due to being a cold region, rich people used to spend summer months [here]. The Headquarter of British Government of Frontier Province also used to shift from Peshawar to **Nathia Gali** in summers. Many offices were in Abbottabad also. Due to this, there used to be lot of hustle-bustle in this area in summer months. Hundreds of officers, lawyers and other government employees, Babus etc. used to be there. Civilians also used to reach in large numbers. So there was a good opportunity for preaching here.

**Radha Soami:**
The founder of **Radha Soami** sect **Sri Shiv Dayal Singh (1818-1878)** was a Khatri of **Agra**, whose background was from Lahore. His ancestors were Sehajdhari Sikhs believing in **Guru Nanak Sahib Ji**. In Agra, Sri Shiv Dayal Singh used to do Bhajan Simran and Satsang. His lovers used to address him as 'Soami'. **'Radha'** was the name of his wife. That is why his successors named the sect **'Radha Soami'**.
**Baba Jaimal Singh**, the founder of **Beas** seat of Radha Soamis, was in Army service in those days. His platoon being in Agra, he used to go to **Gurdwara Mai Than**. Sri Shiv Dayal Singh used to perform **Katha of Gurbani** there first. Listening to Katha of Gurbani, he became his Satsangi.

Later Baba Jaimal Singh retired from Army service and in **1891** settled near village **Waraich** and **Ball Saran** on the bank of river Beas. The Sikhs of Ball Saran, considering him a Sikh Sadhu, gave **ten kanals sixteen marlas** of land from the common land of the village for building a **Dharamsala**, the registry of which was done in the name of **Guru Granth Sahib**.
In **1903**, after the death of Baba Jaimal Singh... [Successor]...
Original place of Dera remained in the name of Guru Sahib. Later it was [encroached/changed?]...
(These facts are taken from the book **'Radha Soami Mat Darpan'** written by **Giani Pratap Singh Ji**, Ex-Jathedar Akal Takht Sahib).
[Mention of someone] who later became famous as Radha Soami Beas wale, was posted as S.D.O... and through his influence and preaching gave Radha Soami Mantra to many...

Notes
- "Radha Soami" is a spiritual movement. The text presents the Sikh perspective/critique of its origin, emphasizing its roots in Gurbani and the original land grant being for Guru Granth Sahib.

ਦੀਵਾਨ ਸੱਜੇ, ਜਿਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਇਲਾਕੇ ਦੀਆਂ ਸਾਰੀਆਂ ਬਸਤੀਆਂ - ਅਣਖੋਹਾ, ਮਕੇਲ, ਨਾੜਾ,
ਸਤੌੜਾ, ਮੋਰੀ, ਵਡਬੈਣ, ਜਾਬਾ, ਧਣਕ, ਕੜਛ, ਮੁਰਾੜੀ, ਕਾਲਾ ਬਾਗ਼ ਤੇ ਨੱਥਿਆ ਗਲੀ

ਦੇ ਮਹਾਂਵਾਕਾਂ ਦੀ ਬੜੀ ਅਸਰ ਭਰਪੁਰ ਵਿਆਖਿਆ ਕੀਤੀ ਤੇ 'ਗੁਰ ਕੀ ਵਸਤੁ ਹੈ ?, ਸਤਿਗੁਰ
ਜੋਤਿ ਪ੍ਰਤੱਖ ਸ੍ਰੀ ਗੁਰੂ ਗ੍ਰੰਥ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਜੀ ਹਨ, ਗੁਰੂ ਧਾਰਨ ਦੀ ਰੀਤੀ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਛੱਕਣ ਤੋਂ ਬਿਨਾ
ਹੋਰ ਕੋਈ ਨਹੀਂ” - ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਵਿਸ਼ਿਆਂ ਉਤੇ ਪੁਰਦਲੀਲ ਤੇ ਅਸਰ ਭਰਪੂਰ ਭਾਸ਼ਨ ਦਿੱਤੇ ਅਤੇ ਐਸੀ
ਯੁਕਤੀ ਪੂਰਬਕ ਰੌਸ਼ਨੀ ਪਾਈ ਕਿ ਰਾਧਾ ਸੁਆਮੀ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਦਾ ਸਾਰਾ ਅਸਰ ਖ਼ਤਮ ਕਰ ਦਿੱਤਾ।
ਅਨੇਕਾਂ ਸੱਜਣਾਂ ਨੂੰ ਫਿਰ ਆਪਣੇ ਇਸ਼ਟ ਸੀ੍‌ ਗੁਰੂ ਗ੍ਰੰਥ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਵੱਲ ਮੋੜਿਆ।
ਗਲੀਆਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਬੜਾ ਅਸਰ ਭਰਪੂਰ ਸਿੱਖੀ ਦਾ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਕਰਕੇ ਜਦ ਵਾਪਸ ਐਬਟਾਬਾਦ ਆਏ
ਤਾਂ ਉੱਥੇ ਸਿੰਘ ਸਭਾ ਦੇ ਗੁਰਦੁਆਰੇ ਵਿੱਚ ਇੱਕ ਖ਼ਾਸ ਜੋੜ ਮੇਲਾ ਹੋਇਆ। ਇਸ ਵਿੱਚ ਨੱਥਿਆ
ਗਲੀ ਦੇ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਵਿੱਚ ਹਾਜ਼ਰੀ ਭਰ ਕੇ ਆਏ ਵਕੀਲਾਂ ਦੀ ਪ੍ਰੇਰਨਾਂ ਨਾਲ ਸਿੱਖਾਂ ਤੋਂ ਛੁੱਟ, ਹਿੰਦੁ
ਮੁਸਲਮਾਨ ਅਫ਼ਸਰਾਂ ਨੂੰ ਉਚੇਚਾ ਨਿਮੰਤਰਨ ਦਿੱਤਾ ਗਿਆ। ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਆਏ ਸੱਜਣਾਂ 'ਤੇ ਇਤਨਾ
ਸੋਹਣਾ ਪ੍ਰਭਾਵ ਪਿਆ ਅਤੇ ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਨੇ ਇਤਨਾ ਪਿਆਰ ਪ੍ਰਗਟ ਕੀਤਾ ਕਿ ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਦੀ ਬੇਨਤੀ
ਪਰ ਇੱਕ ਹੋਰ ਇਹੋ ਜਿਹਾ ਜੋੜ ਮੇਲਾ ਕਰਨ ਦਾ ਫ਼ੈਸਲਾ ਕੀਤਾ ਗਿਆ, ਤਾਂ ਜੋ ਜਿਹੜੇ ਹਿੰਦੁ
ਮੁਸਲਮਾਨ ਅਫ਼ਸਰ ਤੇ ਕਰਮਚਾਰੀ ਪਹਿਲੇ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਵਿੱਚ ਨਹੀਂ ਸੀ ਆ ਸਕੇ, ਉਹ ਵੀ ਪੁੱਜ ਕੇ
ਲਾਭ ਉਠਾਉਣ। ਇਸ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਵਿੱਚ ਸਿੱਖ ਸੰਗਤਾਂ ਤੋਂ ਛੁੱਟ ਬਾਹਰੋਂ ਆਏ ਅਫ਼ਸਰ ਤੇ ਹੋਰ ਮਤਾਂ
ਦੇ ਸੱਜਣ ਇਲਾਹੀ ਬਾਣੀ ਦੇ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਤੇ ਵਖਿਆਣ ਸੁਣ ਕੇ ਅਤੀ ਪ੍ਰਭਾਵਿਤ ਹੋਏ ਤੇ ਸਤਿਗੁਰੂ
ਦਾ ਅਥਾਹ ਪਿਆਰ ਆਪਣੇ ਹਿਰਦਿਆਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਲੈ ਕੇ ਗਏ।
ਇਸ ਸਮੇਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਆਈ ਸਾਰੀ ਮਾਇਆ, ਸਦਾ ਵਾਂਗੂ, ਪ੍ਰਬੰਧਕਾਂ ਰਾਹੀਂ ਚੀਫ਼ ਖ਼ਾਲਸਾ ਦੀਵਾਨ
ਭੇਜ ਦਿੱਤੀ ਜਾਂਦੀ ਰਹੀ।
ਨੋਟ : ਉਪ੍ਰੋਕਤ ਹਾਲਾਤ ਸੰਤ ਜੀਵਨ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਐਬਟਾਬਾਦ ਵੱਲੋਂ ਭੇਜੀ ਰਿਪੋਰਟ ਦੇ
/#ੱਨੀਂ ਦਾ ਪ੍ਚਾਨ - 73		 English (Meaning Translation)

**Abbottabad Singh Sabha** was making considerable efforts to save Sikhi from this declension. **Sardar Lakhmi Singh**, **Sardar Gulab Singh**, **Malik Deva Singh** and **Sardar Narain Singh** (Father of Giani Bhupinder Singh, Ex-MP) were Granthis of Singh Sabha Gurdwara. This was the time of end of the second decade of 20th century.
On the strong request of **Sri Guru Singh Sabha Abbottabad**, the first month (July) [of the tour] was given to District Hazara. During this one month, Bhai Sahib traveled from Abbottabad to **Mansehra**, **Nathia Gali**, **Dunga Gali** and other small settlements like **Malach**, **Baffa**, covering miles of journey on foot, often getting drenched in rain, and sounded the conch of Guru Nanak.

**Malach** was the center of preaching gatherings of **Babu Sawan Singh**, where through his chosen hymns and verses, highlighting the importance of a living Guru, he was preaching hundreds of innocent Sikhs against the spirit of Gursikhi. The local sewadars felt a dire need to counter this. Keeping this in mind, organizers arranged a program of Bhai Hira Singh Ji's divine Kirtan in Malach.
Here huge Diwans were held, in which all settlements of the area - **Ankhoba, Makel, Nara, Satoura, Mori, Vadbain, Jaba, Dhanak, Karch, Murari, Kala Bagh** and **Nathia Gali** participated.
Here Bhai Sahib gave very effective explanations of great sentences like *"Bani Guru Guru Hai Bani"* (Bani is Guru, Guru is Bani) and *"Shabad Guru Surat Dhun Chela"*. On topics like *"Gur Ki Vast Hai?"* (What is Guru's commodity?), "True Guru Light is manifest Sri Guru Granth Sahib Ji", "There is no other way to adopt Guru except taking Amrit" - he gave argumentative and effective speeches and threw light with such logic that the entire effect of Radha Soami preaching was nullified.
He turned back many gentlemen towards their deity **Sri Guru Granth Sahib**.

After doing effective Sikhi preaching in Galiyan (Hills), when he returned to Abbottabad, a special **Jor-Mela** (Congregation) was held in Singh Sabha Gurdwara. In this, upon persuasion of Lawyers who had attended the Diwan at Nathia Gali, besides Sikhs, **Hindu and Muslim officers** were specially invited. Such a beautiful impression was cast on these visiting gentlemen and they expressed so much love that on their request, it was decided to hold another such Jor-Mela so that those Hindu-Muslim officers and employees who could not come in the first Diwan could also come and take benefit. In this Diwan, apart from Sikh Sangats, officers and gentlemen of other faiths were extremely impressed listening to Kirtan and discourse of Divine Bani and took immense love of Satguru in their hearts.

All money received during this time, like always, kept being sent to **Chief Khalsa Diwan** through organizers.

**Note:** Above facts are written based on report sent by **Sant Jiwan Singh Ji Abbottabad**. This report is found published in **Khalsa Samachar dated 2.8.1920**.

Notes
- "Babu Sawan Singh" refers to the second Satguru of Radha Soami Satsang Beas (Great Master). The text reflects the ideological clash between mainstream Sikhism (Guru Granth Sahib as Guru) and Radha Soami sect (Living Guru).
