**Preaching Tours in Quetta (Balochistan)**
In **Quetta**, lovers like **Rai Bahadur Kabla Singh** and **Sardar Bahadur Gurdit Singh Ji** had established a center for Sikh preaching by forming **Sri Guru Singh Sabha**. A **Khalsa High School** was also running very successfully there, whose Headmaster **Late Giani Sadhu Singh Ji** was a great lover of Guru's house and an enthusiastic gentleman. He became a victim of the **Earthquake of 1935**.

For the month of **August 1920**, **Chief Khalsa Diwan** gave permission to Bhai Hira Singh Ji to go to Quetta and he reached there on **30th July**. On the first day a huge Procession and then for three days religious Diwan congregations were held. From 2 AM in the morning (Amrit Vela) Sangats started arriving and by 4 AM the whole Pandal was packed...
Besides Sangats, gentlemen of other faiths also joined and were satisfied by enjoying the holy Bani of Satguru.
To the extent that **Lat Sahib (Governor/Agent to Governor General) of Balochistan** served Langar and Chhabeels (sweet water stalls) at his Government House (Residency)...

(Khalsa Samachar 30 August 1951, From Quetta Preaching Tours, Written by **S. Kahan Singh Ji**, President Sri Guru Singh Sabha, Lodhi Road New Delhi)

Notes
- "Lat Sahib" refers to the Agent to the Governor General (AGG) in Balochistan. The mention of him serving Langar is significant.

/ਨੈੱਦੀ ਦਾ ਪਚਾਨ - 5		 English (Meaning Translation)

[Context: Likely referring to a program in Arya Samaj Mandir where initially they refused something, perhaps Parkash of Guru Granth Sahib]
...refused. The Sindhi Seth pleaded a lot but he didn't agree. On this side [the time was passing?], so he became very worried. Finally he offered his resignation. On this the Babu of the Samaj got worried because that Sindhi Seth used to do limitless financial service to the Samaj.
Therefore they agreed to do Parkash of Guru Baba and Bhai Sahib's divine Kirtan happened in the presence of **Sri Guru Granth Sahib** in **Arya Samaj Mandir**. He explained the importance of Guru Granth Sahib being the 'Eternal Guru' and the love of Guru's court was overflowing through the eyes of listeners. From everyone's mouth the holy tune of **'Dhan Guru Gobind Singh Ji'** was coming out.

This was a unique event in itself - going to the religious temple of another faith, preaching one's own faith and then convincing them. Sikh Sangats celebrated endlessly on this, perhaps this was the first such occasion.

**Kirtan in Military Platoon:**
One Diwan was held in **Platoon Number 107**. The city Sangat also arrived in crowds from three miles distance. The arrangement of Diwan and decoration of Pandal by Singhs of the Platoon was worth seeing. The Secretary of the Commanding Officer of the Platoon, **Sardar Sewa Singh Ji** was translating to him side by side. The Commanding Officer was so happy that at the end of Kirtan he said, "In future, whichever Jawans want to go to the weekly Diwan of Singh Sabha on Sunday, can go without any restriction. I will happily grant leave." Remember that in those days **Akali Movement** was in full swing in Punjab and British officers used to be afraid of such Diwans.

*Jithe Jai Bahai Mera Satguru So Than Suhava Ram Raje ||*
(Wherever my True Guru goes and sits, that place becomes beautiful, O Lord King.)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 450)

In the vast ground of **Sanatan Dharam Mandir**, doing Parkash of Sri Guru Granth Sahib Ji... [Bhai Sahib] expressed that our every pore is under debt of Satguru Ji. When Bhai Sahib narrated the martyrdom of **Sri Guru Tegh Bahadur**, 'Hind Di Chadar', everyone's eyes started flowing like streams. Then Bhai Sahib painted the picture of Waheguru's Court where lakhs of Brahmas, Bishnus, Maheshs are standing...

Notes
- "Platoon Number 107" likely refers to 107th Pioneers.

2		 English (Meaning Translation)

That time was extremely blissful when along with Khalsa Ji, all Sindhis and Sanatanis were reciting behind the Ragi Singhs:
[Kirtan Lines]
...and dyed in the color of Unity were doing Simran of 'Ik Oankar'. In this Kirtan, a full wave of Gurmat preaching flowed and episodes were narrated showing Prema Bhakti (Loving Devotion) as superior to numerous rituals. While saying and telling all this, Bhai Sahib did not speak anything against any sect, elderly, Prophet or Rishi-Muni. He told everyone to walk on Truth, do honest labor and have heartfelt love for humanity.

Note: News of above Diwans are taken from reports sent by **S. Kartar Singh**, Asst. Secretary, Reception Committee Quetta, which [appeared] in issues of **August and September 1920**...

Such a flow of Kirtan ran that the **Lat Sahib (Governor)** of Balochistan held a Diwan in his own Kothi (Residence). The story of this, which my friend Late **Major Prem Singh Ji** (1902-1972) who was posted in Quetta at that time, wrote and sent is as follows:
"...The Agent to Governor General for Balochistan, whom common people used to call 'Lat', used to live in the Residency. There was always a strict guard at every gate of the House... This officer used to tour every बस्ती (settlement) on horse with a stick in hand. No one dared to go near this officer.
The Head Peon of the Residency was an elderly Sikh Sardar who looked very impressive in his royal red uniform and polished brass belt. His double turban, beautiful beard and red glowing face doubled his awe and he used to get his legitimate demands accepted by Lat Sahib with boldness.
One day after coming from Diwan, he thought why not have Parkash of Sri Guru Granth Sahib in Lat Sahib's Kothi and hold a Diwan with Bhai Hira Singh Ji's Kirtan. So he went to Lat Sahib and said, 'Huzoor, I have a request...'"

Notes
- "Late Major Prem Singh Ji" is the source of the anecdote about the Head Peon arranging Kirtan at the Governor's house.

ਲਨ ਛਾ ਪੁਦਾਨ - 77		 English (Meaning Translation)

"'...A great Priest Sahib has come from Punjab to our [place]. His [Kirtan/Sermon] takes place daily till 12 o'clock. All city judges and officers go to listen. If you allow, we may also hold his Kirtan in the Kothi here, so that you may also see...'"
Lat Sahib was a bit surprised at this unique request and after thinking a little... looked at Sardar Bahadur's intent face and said...
He called [someone] and asked who this Priest is? They told that he is a religious leader of very high stature.
On this Lat Sahib ordered that preparation for the next Diwan be done in his Lawn.
So next morning, Parkash of **Sri Guru Granth Sahib Ji** was done in the Lawn of Lat Sahib's Kothi and Diwan was held in which **Bhai Bhag Singh Hira Singh Ji** performed captivating Kirtan and blessed thousands of Sangat.
Apart from Lat Sahib, all officers of his Residency, Government employees, Hindus, Sikhs, Muslims, Parsis, everyone sat for the full time and listened to Kirtan and enjoyed the bliss - *"Taha Baikunth Jah Kirtan Tera"* (There is heaven where Your Kirtan is performed).

Regarding the effect of this one month's preaching, some words from the report sent by **Rai Bahadur Kabla Singh**, President Sri Guru Singh Sabha Quetta to Chief Khalsa Diwan are as follows, which appeared in the supplement of **Khalsa Samachar dated 16 August 1920**:
"giving the swing/joy of Gurbani Kirtan to Sikh Sangat all day, Bhai Hira Singh Ji showed a glimpse of Baikunth Dham (Heaven) on this earth. The flow of Satsang and essence of Gursikhi - waking at late night (Amrit Vela), reading Gurbani etc. - was revived anew.
Shopkeepers and families sitting in homes discuss the morning Diwan all day... come to Bhai Sahib to understand Gursikhi...
Those who in earlier days used to sit with naked heads like strangers... today they rub their nose before Guru Granth Sahib and bow... and offering Karah Parshad get Ardas performed...
Many gentlemen took pledge that after 4 o'clock they will never stay [at shop/work] and will come to Gurdwara daily to do Satsang...
The Kirtans held in Arya Samaj and Sanatan Dharam Mandirs after Parkash of Sri Guru Granth Sahib Ji, their effect was worth seeing there itself..."

Notes
- "Rai Bahadur Kabla Singh" provides the official report cited.
Page 0076

ਰਾਮ ਜੀ ਨੇ ਉਨ ਕਾਰੇ ਗਜਾਏ ਜਏ। ਚਰ ਪ੍ਰਭਾਵ ਐਸਾ ਚਲਿਆ ਬਿ ੨9 ਦਿਤਾ
ਵਿੱਚ ਕੋਈ ਨਾ ਕੋਈ ਲੋੜਵੰਦ ਉੱਠ ਕੇ ਸਿੱਖੀ ਦੀ ਅਭਿਲਾਸ਼ਾ ਪ੍ਰਗਟ ਕਰਦਾ। ਜਿਹੜੇ ਸਿੰਘ
ਲਾਲ ਰਾਮ ਲਭਾਇਆ ਮਲ ਜੀ, ਲਾਲ ਗਣੇਸ਼ ਦਾਸ ਜੀ, ਦੀਵਾਨ ਮੂਲ ਚੰਦ ਸਿੰਧੀ ਮਾਸਟਰ
ਵੀਰ ਭਾਨ ਜੀ ਇਤਿਆਦਿਕ। ਰ੍
ਦੀਵਾਨ ਦੇ ਅਰਪਣ ਕੀਤਾ ਹੋਇਆ ਸੀ, ਇਸ ਕਰਕੇ ਜੋ ਮਾਇਆ ਸ਼ਬਦ ਭੇਟ ਰੰਦੀ ਰਹੀ, ਸਭ
ਫ਼ ਖ਼ਾਲਸਾ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਦੇ ਪ੍ਚਾਰ ਫ਼ੰਡ ਲਈ ਸੁ. ਚੇਤ ਸਿੰਘ ਸੌਦਾਗਰ ਈਰਾਨ ਦੇ ਹੱਥੀ ਜਮ੍ਹਾ
ਹੁੰਦੀ ਰਹੀ। ਕੋਇਟਾ ਨਿਵਾਸੀ ਸਿੱਖ ਸੰਗਤ ਚੀਫ਼ ਖ਼ਾਲਸਾ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਦੇ ਅਤੀ ਧੰਨਵਾਦੀ ਹਨ
ਜਿਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਨੇ ਪੰਥ ਦਾ ਸ਼੍ਰੋਮਣੀ ਜੱਥਾਂ ਭੇਜ ਕੇ ਕੋਇਟੇ ਵਿੱਚ ਐਸਾ ਅਦੁੱਤੀ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਕਰਵਾਇਆ ਹੈ।
ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਦਾ 248.1920 ਦਾ ਅਖ਼ੀਰਲਾ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਸੀ। ਇਹ ਅਸਚਰਜ ਵੈਰਾਗ ਤੇ
ਕਰੁਣਾ ਰਸ ਦਾ ਭਰਿਆ ਹੋਇਆ ਸੀ ਤੇ ਸਟੇਸ਼ਨ ਤੋਂ ਤੁਰਨ ਸਮੇਂ ਦਾ ਨਜ਼ਾਰਾ ਵੇਖਣ ਯੋਗ ਸੀ।
ਕੋਇਟੇ ਵਿੱਚ ਹੋਈ ਪ੍ਰਸੰਸਾ ਨੂੰ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੇ ਆਪਣੀ ਆਤਮਾ 'ਤੇ ਇੱਕ ਬੋਝ ਮਹਿਸੂਸ
ਕੀਤਾ ਤੇ ਆਪਣੇ ਪਰਮਾਰਥਕ ਜੀਵਨ ਲਈ ਹਾਨੀਕਾਰਕ ਸਮਝਿਆ। ਇਸ ਲਈ ਜਦ ਆਪ ਵਾਪਸ
ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤਸਰ ਜੀ ਪੁੱਜੇ (ਜਿੱਥੇ ਉਹ ਉਨ੍ਹੀਂ ਦਿਨੀਂ ਨਿਵਾਸ ਰੱਖਏ ਸਨ) ਤਾਂ ਗੱਡੀ ਤੋਂ ਉਤਰ ਕੇ ਬਾਝ
ਜੀ ਤੇ ਜੱਥੇ ਨੂੰ ਸਿਧਾ ਘਰ, ਚੌਂਕ ਕਰੋੜੀ ਭਜ ਦਿੱਤਾ ਤੇ ਆਪ ਸ੍ਰੀ ਹਰਮੰਦਰ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਪੁੱਜ ਕੇ ਸਾਰੀ
ਦਰ ਰੱਥੀਂ ਜੇਵਾ ਕਰਕੇ ਆਪਣੀ ਸੁਰਤ ਦਾ ਇਸ਼ਨਾਨ ਕੀਤਾ ਅਤੇ ਇਹ ਸ਼ੋਭਾ ਤੇ ਪਰਸ ਸਰੀ ਗਰ
ਰਮ ਦਾਸ ਜੀ ਦੇ ਪਵਿੱਤਰ ਚਰਨਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਰੱਖ ਕੇ ਅਰਦਾਸਾ ਕੀਤਾ “
ਗੁਰੂ ਨਾੜਗ ਸਝ' ਤੈਦੀ ਵਲਿਆਈ।, ਕੋਈ ਨਾਉ ਨ ਜਾਣੈ. ਸੋਫਾ।।
(ਗੁਗ੍ਰੰਸਾ. ਅੰਗ 383)
ਤੇ ਇਸ ਤਰ੍ਹਾਂ ਉਹ ਆਪਣੇ ਆਪ ਨੂੰ ਹਲਕਾ ਮਹਿਸੂਸ ਕਰਕੇ ਘਰ ਆਵੋ
% - ਅਨੰਲਕ` ਗੰਣਾ		 English (Meaning Translation)

[Context: Bhai Hira Singh Ji's Kirtan effect continues]
...One [Lala Ram Ji?] got up and requested that "Please make me a Keshadhari Singh."
[Many] Karahs were prepared. The influence was such that [every day] some seeker would get up and express desire for Sikhi. Some Singhs [who took Amrit/Kesh?]... **Lala Ram Labhaya Mal Ji**, **Lala Ganesh Das Ji**, **Diwan Mul Chand Sindhi**, **Master Vir Bhan Ji** etc.

Since Bhai Sahib had dedicated [himself/everything?] to the Diwan, whatever money was received as Shabad-Bheta, was all deposited for the Preaching Fund of **Chief Khalsa Diwan** through **S. Chet Singh Saudagar (Merchant) Iran**.
Quetta dwelling Sikh Sangat is extremely thankful to Chief Khalsa Diwan who sent the Shiromani Jatha of Panth and got such unique preaching done in Quetta.

Bhai Sahib's last Diwan was on **24.8.1920**. It was full of amazing Vairag (dispassion) and Karuna Ras (Pathos). The scene at the station at the time of departure was worth seeing.
Bhai Hira Singh Ji felt the praise received in Quetta as a burden on his soul and considered it harmful for his spiritual life. So when he reached back **Amritsar Ji** (where he was residing those days), getting off the train... he sent the Jatha straight home to **Chowk Karori** and himself reached **Sri Harmandir Sahib**. Doing service of dusting shoes (Jora-Ghar) with his own hands, he bathed his consciousness (Surat) and offered all this praise and honor at the holy feet of **Sri Guru Ram Das Ji** and performed Ardas:
*"Guru Nanak Sabh Teri Wudiyayi, Koi Nao Na Janai Mera"*
(Guru Nanak, all this glory is Yours, no one knows my name.)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 383)

And in this way feeling himself light, he came home.

Notes
- "Chowk Karori" is a locality in Amritsar.
- "Vairag" refers to spiritual detachment/longing.

/ਸ਼ੱਖੀ ਦਾ` ਪਚਾਨ - 7?		 English (Meaning Translation)

**Preaching at Nankana Sahib:**
When **Chief Khalsa Diwan** was established in **1902**, it was felt that on the occasion of this huge fair [at Nankana Sahib], good preaching of Dharma can be done. Keeping this in view, it was decided to send one Preacher Jatha. The first Jatha was sent in **November 1903**. In this Jatha **Bhai Bhag Singh Hira Singh Ji** Ragi, **Bhai Amrik Singh Ji Chune Wale** and Diwan's Updeshak (Preacher) were included...
Gathering Sangat from **Amritsar, Tarn Taran** and **Gujranwala**, a Jatha for Amrit preaching [led by] Bhai Lal Singh...
**Bhai Amrik Singh Ji Chune Wale (1868-1943)** was a great lover of Guru's house and spirited gentleman. His lecture used to be argumentative and pulling for the audience. He was among the founders of the Diwan and every year reaching Nankana Sahib on this Gurpurab, he used to perform the service of Dharma Prachar and Amrit Prachar for a week. He was arrested for being a member of the first **Shiromani Committee** which was declared illegal, and served two and a half years of rigorous imprisonment in Mianwali Jail.

Under the management of Chief Khalsa Diwan, preachers were sent.
**Bhai Amrik Singh Chune Wale** used to arrive every year for service, and bringing Langar material etc. collected from **Lahore** was his responsibility. In Lahore collecting utensils etc. from **S. Mehar Singh Chawla** and flour ration etc. from **S. Harnam Singh Attewale** [was his duty].
With the caravan (Vaheer) there used to be a Palanquin (Palki) of **Sri Guru Granth Sahib** and wherever stops were made, morning Diwans were held there.
With the divine Kirtan of **Bhai Bhag Singh Hira Singh Ragi**, such a mood was set that it seemed as if *"Dhan Guru Nanak"* was echoing even from the Karir and Wan trees.

At **Nankana Sahib**, there wasn't much population then. The **Bar** (wild land) was not yet settled, everywhere there were only Wan and Karir trees. On every side of the old building of **Gurdwara Janam Asthan**, only Sadhus were visible. In the Tabia (service) of Sri Guru Granth Sahib Ji also, a long-haired (Jatadhari) Sadhu used to be established. Rababis used to do Kirtan and offerings were taken by Udasi Saint only.
At that time **Mahant Kishan Das** (mentioning before **Mahant Narain Das** of the Saka/Massacre) used to sit on a cushion (Gadela) in the presence of Guru Maharaj.

It was natural for **Chief Khalsa Diwan** to oppose such anti-Gurmat activities. On this, the Mahant banned holding Diwan at Janam Asthan. Sikh Sangats used to pay obeisance at Gurdwaras but Diwan could not be held...
To the extent that in **1906** when Chief Khalsa Diwan's Jatha in Katak [month]...

Notes
- "Chune Wale" - likely his trade/business family name (Lime merchant).
- "Bar" refers to the wild, semi-arid area of Punjab before canal colonization.

[Context: Jatha arrived to celebrate Gurpurab of Puranmashi]
...reached to celebrate Gurpurab, then Mahant prohibited them from coming to Chhats (roofed place/platform) place. Because at Nankana Sahib [Mahant's guards were everywhere]. No other such place could be found [to hold Diwan]... on which Mahant had no control. So great difficulty [arose].
...found out that one **10 Bigha compound** belonging to **Sardar Balaka Singh** of village **Kaunke**... could be used for holding Diwan. So contacting **Bhai Kartar Singh Ji**, after much effort its usage [permission] was obtained.
In the night Diwan when Bhai Hira Singh Ji mentioned this incident, Sangats expressed great regret upon listening. On Bhai Sahib's appeal, immense money was collected to buy this compound and when it was bought, the Mahant by doing [mischief/litigation?] took it back. Again it was bought in the name of **Sardar Mangal Singh Man Kot Shera**.

In Diwans of following years, by appealing to Sangats, many rooms were built there for residence and every year maximum festivities used to be held at **Chief Khalsa Diwan's Diwan Asthan**. Bhai Hira Singh Ji throughout his life used to attend Sri Nankana Sahib every year on **Katak Puranmashi Gurpurab** and used to preach Dharma in Sangats through Kirtan for three days at Chief Khalsa Diwan's congregation place.
...
From the above difficulties it can be experienced how much pain Sangats must have felt inside. The huge income of Gurdwara property, instead of being spent on Gurmat preaching or service of Gurdwara buildings, was spent by Mahants on their luxury and debauchery. Result was that character of Mahants fell. Instead of Gurmat they started walking on Durmat (evil path). Sikh Sangats could not tolerate this. Slowly, resentment grew inside and finally on **20 February 1921**, with the martyrdom of Singhs, the Birth Place of World-Savior Guru Nanak Dev Ji was liberated from the rule of Mahants. Along with this enthusiasm in Akali movement increased.

After Panth's possession of Janam Asthan, the Janam-Raat (Birth Night) Diwan again started being held fearlessly till Janam [time?] and Bhai Hira Singh Ji performed Kirtan service in **1925**...
In the end, upon Bhai Hira Singh Ji's departure to Gurpuri, in the Sikh number of **'Phulwari'**, the article which **Giani Hira Singh Ji 'Dard'** Editor published under title 'Crown of Panth's Immortal Martyrs', that is given in the end of this [chapter/book].

Notes
- "Saka Nankana Sahib" (Nankana Massacre) of 1921 is described here.

**Akali Movement and Gurdwara Reform Movement:**
As a Panthic Servant and Preacher, it was inevitable for **Bhai Hira Singh Ji** to be affected by the Gurdwara Reform Movement, and he felt the responsibility on his head, which he experienced fully. Panthic pain and enthusiasm were overflowing inside him. The need to [liberate Gurdwaras?] was felt by Panthic leaders. For this purpose, Bhai Hira Singh Ji kept dedicating his service to the Panth.

**Birth of Akali Movement:**
In **1919**, when the butcher of Jallianwala Bagh **Dyer** was given a **Siropa** (Robe of Honor) by the Sarbrah (Manager) and Pujaris of Sri Darbar Sahib, the blood of Sikhs boiled.
Agitation started for Gurdwara Management Reform and moving forward this agitation gave birth to the **Akali Movement**.

First of all voice was raised against the apostate Sarbrah of **Gurdwara Babe Di Ber, Sialkot**, **Ganda Singh?** and forming a Gurdwara Committee, the management was given to the Panth.
[Mention of Khalsa Baradri/low caste Sikhs?] started administering Amrit to untouchable castes and decorating them as Singhs and Khalsa Baradri Singhs in form of a procession reached Sri Darbar Sahib on **12 October 1920**.
After some dispute it was decided to take Hukamnama (Order) of Sri Darbar Sahib (Guru Granth Sahib). So this Hukam came:
*"Niguhre Ka Hai Nao Burra, Niguhra Hoe Na Koi ||"*
(The name of one without a Guru is bad, may no one be without a Guru.)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 636 - *Correction: Text says 638, Quote says 'Nigure Ka Hai Nau Bura', actually 'Sorath Mahala 3... Nigure Ka Hai Nau Bura' is Ang 636/637? The text quotes 'Gunviheen Bharam Apradhi Bhai...' which is Sorath M:3 Ang 638*).
*Correction reading Text Hukam:*
*"Gunviheen Bharam Apradhi Bhai, Poorai Satgur Layi Palaye || Rahao ||"*
(I am without virtue, wandering in doubt and a sinner, O brother; the Perfect True Guru has taken me into His care/hem. Pause.)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 638)

Hearing this Hukam, Pujaris ran away leaving Akal Takht empty and management came to the Panth. On this a committee of **9 gentlemen** was formed for management of Sri Darbar Sahib. Then on **13 November 1920**, **36 men** Gurdwara Parbandhak [Committee formed].
[On 15-16] November 1920, in a great Panthic gathering at Sri Akal Takht, **Shiromani [Gurdwara Parbandhak Committee]** of **175 members** [was formed].

Notes
- The text describes the pivotal moment when control of the Golden Temple shifted from British-appointed Mahants to the Sikh community (SGPC). The Hukamnama cited (Ang 638) was interpreted as Guru accepting the "sinners/low castes" into his fold.

ਹੇਠ ਤਕਰੀਬਨ 200 ਸਿੰਘਾਂ ਦਾ ਜੱਥਾ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਵੇਲੇ ਗੁਰਦੁਆਰਾ ਜਨਮ ਅਸਥਾਨ ਸ੍ਰੀ ਨਨਕਾਣਾ
ਜਿਉਂ ਹੀ ਜੱਥੇ ਦੇ ਸਿੰਘ, ਗੁਰਦੁਆਰਾ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਅੰਦਰ ਬੈਠ ਗਏ, ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਦਾ ਕਤਲੇਆਮ ਸ਼ੁਰੂ ਕਰ
ਦਿੱਤਾ ਗਿਆ। ਸਿੰਘਾਂ ਨੂੰ ਗੋਲੀਆਂ ਨਾਲ ਮਾਰਿਆ ਗਿਆ ਅਤੇ ਛਵ੍ਰੀਆਂ ਤੇ ਗੰਡਾਸਿਆਂ ਨਾਲ
ਟੱਕਿਆ ਗਿਆ। ਇਸ ਕੰਮ ਲਈ ਮਹੰਤ ਨੇ ਪਹਿਲੋਂ ਹੀ ਭਾੜੇ ਦੇ ਬੰਦੇ ਬਿਠਾ ਰੱਖੇ ਸਨ। ਫਿਰ
ਕਈਆਂ ਨੂੰ ਜੀਉਂਦੇ ਹੀ ਤੇਲ ਪਾ ਕੇ ਸਾੜਿਆ ਗਿਆ। ਜੱਥਾ ਪੁਰਨ ਸ਼ਾਂਤਮਈ ਰਿਹਾ ਤੇ ਸਿੰਘਾਂ
ਨੇ ਖਿੜ੍ਹੇ ਮੱਥੇ ਸ਼ਹੀਦੀਆਂ ਦਿੱਤੀਆਂ। ਸਰਦਾਰ ਦਲੀਪ ਸਿੰਘ, ਜੋ ਮਹੰਤ ਦੇ ਚੰਗੇ ਮਿੱਤਰ ਸਨ,
ਉਸ ਨੂੰ ਇਸ ਅਨਰਥ ਤੋਂ ਰੋਕਣ ਤੇ ਸਮਝਾਉਣ ਲਈ ਆਏ ਤਾਂ ਗੁਰਦੁਆਰਾ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਦੇ ਬਾਹਰ

(0 €%		 English (Meaning Translation)

...were elected. But soon in **January 1921**, due to being elected as Member of Executive of Punjab Government [Minister?], **Sardar Sundar Singh Majithia** had to resign from this post.

**Keys Morcha and Establishment of Akali Dal:**
Although the Committee (SGPC) was formed, the keys were still kept with the [Government appointed] Manager (Sarbrah), on which **Chabiyan Da Morcha** (Keys Agitation) started. On **14 December 1920** **Akali Dal** was formed and the agitation intensified. Then after struggle of full one year, on **19 January 1922** keys were handed over to the Panth and this Morcha was won. On this **Mahatma Gandhi** sent a congratulatory telegram to **Sardar Kharak Singh**, who was then called the Uncrowned King of Panth, writing: *"First decisive battle for India's freedom won."*

In the meantime, on **20 February 1921**, the **Saka Nankana Sahib** (Martyrdom Massacre) had happened.
...[Could not bear]. Finally on 20 February 1921, under the leadership of **Sardar Lachhman Singh Dharowali**, a Jatha of about **200 Singhs** reached Gurdwara Janam Asthan Sri Nankana Sahib at Amrit Vela...
As soon as the Singhs of the Jatha sat inside Gurdwara Sahib, their massacre was started. Singhs were killed with bullets and cut with Chhavis (axes) and Gandasas. For this work Mahant had already positioned hired goons. Then many were burnt alive by pouring oil. Jatha remained completely peaceful and Singhs gave martyrdoms with smiling faces.
**Sardar Dalip Singh**, who was a good friend of the Mahant, when came to stop him from this atrocity and reason with him, outside Gurdwara Sahib itself, Mahant cooled him down (killed him) with his bullet. All this [happened under the nose of?] English Government...
Next day when... [news reached]. Endless Sangats started marching towards Janam Asthan...

Notes
- "Chabiyan Da Morcha" was the first major victory of the Akali movement against the British Govt.
- Mahatma Gandhi's quote is famous: "First battle of India's freedom won..."

...In this connection, **Professor Sahib Singh Ji (1892-1977)** has written on page 105 of his autobiography **'Meri Jiwan Kahani'** -
"Seeing this massacre my tears flowed out, weeping could not be stopped... I returned, towards inside the Gurdwara. **Bhai Hira Singh Ji Ragi** was sitting in Tabia (service) of that Guru Granth Sahib, in which 5-7 bullets from Sadhus' guns had hit. Bhai Sahib seeing me said, 'Bhai Sahib Singh! Look, bullets have hit the chest of Satguru Ji' and saying this he wept bitterly!"

**Cremation of Martyrs:**
On **22 February 1921**, Panth leaders consulted and decided that cremation of martyr Singhs should be done only when the Governor Sahib himself comes and sees this painful scene with his own eyes. So according to this decision **Sardar Harbans Singh Attari** sent a telegram to the Lat Sahib... On **23 February**, **Sir Edward Maclagan** (Governor) came. All conditions inside were shown to the Lat Sahib... At that time Governor's attitude was full of sympathy and he said, 'Justice will be done.' ...
Akalis raised various slogans. At that time about 40-50 thousand Sangat [had gathered].
Bhai Hira Singh Ji Ragi taking Sangat along went outside near potters' (Kumhars) kilns to collect the bodies. They made a small palanquin and wherever they found any piece of flesh, picking it up they placed it in that...
Leading ahead...

ਇਧਰ ਠੀਕ 10 ਵਜੇ ਸ੍ਰੀ ਅਕਾਲ ਤਖ਼ਤ ਤੇ ਪੰਜ ਅਖੰਡ ਪਾਠਾਂ ਦਾ ਭੋਗ ਪਿਆ!
ਪਗ ਆਂ ਪਟਿਆਲਾ ਨੇ ਅਕਾਲ ਤਖ਼ਤ 'ਤੇ ਆ ਕੇ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਦੀ ਦਾਤ ਮੰਗ
ਤਨਖ਼ਾਹ ਲਾਉਣ ਉਪ੍ਰੰਤ ਅਸ ਦਇਆ ਗਿਆ ਤੋ ਫਿਰ ਮਹਾਰਾਜਾ ਨੇ ਕਾਰ ਸੇਵਾ ਕੀਤੀ'
ਹਕ ਗਨ ਤੇ ਗੁਰਦੁਆਰਾ ਡਾਨ ਠਉਰ - 2		 English (Meaning Translation)

**Morcha Guru Ka Bagh:**
In **August 1922**, for cutting wood for Guru Ka Langar from the land of Gurdwara Guru Ka Bagh which is few miles from Amritsar... on complaint of **Mahant Sundar Das**, **Panja Singh** was imprisoned. Challenging this... many Singhs reached there and they were also imprisoned. Enthusiasm increased further and on 26 August, 60 Singhs were arrested. Then on 31 August regular Morcha started.
ASP was one Englishman named **Beaty**, who had given order to beat Jathas with sticks (lathis). After getting beaten when Singhs used to become unconscious, they were brought back to Amritsar. These Jathas continued for many months. Finally **Sir Ganga Ram** intervened and paying the price of that garden from his own pocket to the Mahant, got the possession of garden given to Singhs. In this way Government saved its face and on **20 November 1922** the Morcha ended. In this Morcha **5605 Singhs** were arrested.

For this Morcha, daily in the evening huge Diwans used to be held at **Guru Ka Bagh (near Manji Sahib)** in which **Bhai Hira Singh Ji** used to fill enthusiasm in Sangats by narrating martyrdom history along with Kirtan.

**Kar Sewa Sri Darbar Sahib Amritsar:**
During the days of Akali movement only, the program for **Kar Sewa** (cleaning of tank) of Sri Darbar Sahib was made. Therefore, an attempt is made to give a brief view of this unique service below.
The date for taking out silt from the Sarovar of Sri Darbar Sahib was fixed as **17 June 1923**. On 17 June at Amrit Vela, a huge Diwan of Khalsa was held at **Gurdwara Pipli Sahib**. In that the estimate of Sangat was about **three lakhs**. **Sri Sant Attar Singh Ji** was sitting in Tabia of Maharaj and Kirtan of Asa Di Var was performed by **Bhai Bhag Singh Hira Singh Ji's** Jatha. At quarter past five a miracle happened!
A Hawk (Baaz) came from Khalsa College side and after circumambulating (Parikarma) the Sangats went back. There was stir in Sangats but soon silence prevailed due to enjoyment of Kirtan.

After the Bhog of Diwan, the Sangat in form of a procession, amid the sound of love-filled Shabad and thunder of Jakaras, started moving towards Darbar Sahib. Akali Jathas in [blue?] dresses were showing a scene of heavenly glory. Then Nirmalas, Udasins...
Here exactly at 10 o'clock, Bhog of five Akhand Paths fell at Sri Akal Takht!
**Maharaja Bhupinder Singh of Patiala** came to Akal Takht and begged for Amrit. After imposing Tankhah (penance), he was administered Amrit and then Maharaja performed Kar Sewa...

Notes
- "Morcha Guru Ka Bagh" (1922) involved non-violent resistance against brutal police beatings.
- "Kar Sewa" of 1923 was a historic event attended by Sant Attar Singh and Maharaja of Patiala.

*Tudh Aage Ardas Hamari Jiyo Pind Sabh Tera ||*
...
*Guru Nanak Sabh Teri Wudiyayi Koi Nao Na Janai Mera ||*

[Someone] said, 'Bhupinder Singh's greatest happiness is in this matter... that he...
should do maximum service of Panth and not bring any pride or glory to self. I consider the treasury and rule of Patiala as trust of Akal Purakh...'

*Kabir Mera Mujh Meh Kichh Nahi Jo Kichh Hai So Tera ||*
(Kabir, nothing is mine within me. Whatever there is, is Yours.)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 1375)

Finally he asked this demand from Panth that "Pray that Satguru may accept me as humble servant of His house...".
Two thousand Namdhari Sikhs came forming a Jatha. **Chief Khalsa Diwan's** Jatha, under the leadership of **Bhai Hira Singh Ji** and **Sant Sangat Singh Ji** [participated] in Sri Darbar [Sahib]...

**Jaito Morcha:**
This started from agitation against the deposition of **Maharaja Ripudaman Singh** of Nabha (9 July 1923). On 9 September 1923, Panthic leaders announced to celebrate 'Nabha Day' and on this day Akhand Path was kept at Gurdwara Gangsar. On **14 September 1923**, Government employees forcefully interrupted the Path by lifting the reciters. This caused resentment in Sangat... arrested everyone. Agitation increased further.
[Jathas] started going after taking pledge and this series continued till January 1924. [Total] 5 thousand men were imprisoned like this. On 9 February first **Shahidi Jatha** of 500 [marched]...

Notes
- "Jaito Morcha" history.
- Maharaja Bhupinder Singh's humility during Kar Sewa is highlighted.
- Maharaja Ripudaman Singh of Nabha was deposed by British for his pro-Akali stance.

ਦਲ ਲੱ ਤੇ ਡਰਦਾ ਰਨ ਲਓ - 2		 English (Meaning Translation)

...Singhs were martyred and many injured. Second Martyrdom Jatha departed on 28 February and reached Jaito on **14 March**, which was imprisoned. In this way total **17 Jathas** departed for martyrdom. Finally on **21 July 1925**, with the start of Akhand Paths at Gurdwara Gangsar Jaito, the restriction was removed and thus the Morcha ended.

For the **Jaito Morcha**, **Bhai Hira Singh Ji** dedicated his service to the Shiromani Committee and performed Kirtan service at Sri Akal Takht for the departing Jathas. In these Kirtans, Bhai Sahib filled such spirit of Sikh Sidak (faith) that the Jathas which came prepared for martyrdom, would get ready for any sacrifice with smiling faces.
...dedicated to the service of Committee.

An eye-witness account of this time given in writing by **Bhai Teja Singh Kohli** is being given here, which was published in **February 1973** issue of **'Gurmat Parkash'**:
"English Government did not hesitate to riddle the first Jatha of 500 Sikhs with bullets. Government was happy. People also used to say that hardly any second Jatha of 500 will be ready to go to the Morcha of Sri Gangsar.
But Hukamnamas had been issued from Sri Akal Takht Sahib, Sri Amritsar to Sikhs of **Peshawar, Pothohar, U.P., C.P., Bombay, Madras** and **Calcutta** and respecting the Hukamnamas, Guru's Sikhs were immediately reaching Sri Amritsar Ji.
To address the Shahidi Jatha, **Bhai Hira Singh Ji Ragi** came. There was no place even to throw a sesame seed in front of Akal Takht. Bhai Sahib's Kirtan and explanation was mesmerizing the Sangats...
It was very impressive. Leaders proposed that the Jatha of 500 prepared [should be inspected?].
...was sitting right next to him. When Bhai Sahib came on stage he saw that Sikh youth were standing, on whose faces youthfulness was overflowing. Fearless, carefree and full of enthusiasm and zeal, Tyar-Bar-Tyar, they were eager to pick up Panth's order. Seeing this, he became absolutely silent for a while and when his love and juice filled tongue opened, he said -
'O Image of my Kalgidhar Ji! My worshipable Guru Khalsa Ji! My heart wants to kiss your feet, apply dust of your feet to my forehead. I [bow] to your high active principle of Sikhism standing right here...'"

Notes
- "Bhai Teja Singh Kohli" gives an eye-witness account of Bhai Hira Singh Ji addressing the 2nd Shahidi Jatha.
- Jaito Morcha saw 17 Shahidi Jathas of 500 each marching peacefully to arrest/bullets.

(ਗੁ.ਗੰ.ਸਾ. ਅੰਗ 1367)
ਡਿੱਗਣੋਂ ਬਚਾਉਣ ਲਈ ਸਾਰੀ ਰਾਤ ਵੇਸਵਾ ਦੇ ਦਰ 'ਤੇ ਪਹਿਰਾ ਦਿੰਦਾ ਰਿਹਾ ਹੈ, ਉਹ ਤੁਸਾਂ
ਨੂੰ ਧਰਮ, ਕੌਮ ਦੇ ਦੇਸ਼ ਨੂੰ ਬਚਾਉਣ ਵਾਲੇ ਸੂਰਬੀਰਾਂ ਦੀ ਬਹੁੜੀ ਕਿਉਂ ਨ ਕਰੇਗਾ ? ਤੁਸ
ਦਸ਼ਮੇਸ਼ ਜੀ ਦੇ ਹੋ ਤੇ ਉਹ ਤੁਹਾਡਾ ਸਦਾ ਰਾਖਾ ਹੈ। ਮੇਰੇ ਪੂਜਯ ਗੁਰਸਿੱਖੋ ! ਆਉ, ਮੇਰੀਆਂ ਅੱਖਾਂ
ਨਾਲ ਵੇਖੋ ! ਉਹ ਅਰਸ਼ਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਖੜ੍ਹਾ ਤੇ ਸੀਸ 'ਤੇ ਖੰਡੇ ਚੱਕਰ ਲਗਾ ਕੇ, ਗਾਤਰੇ ਸ੍ਰੀ ਸਾਹਿਬੁ
ਸਜਾ ਕੇ, ਗੋਡਿਆਂ ਤਕ ਪਹੁੰਚਦੀ ਆਪਣੀ' ਲੰਮੀ ਬਾਂਹ ਦੀ ਸੈਨਤ ਤੁਹਾਡੇ ਵੱਲ ਕਰਕੇ ਇਹ
ਜੁੱਧ ਜਿਤੇ ਇਨ' ਗੀ ਕੇ ਪ੍ਰਸਾਦਿ,
ਇਲਰੀ ਗੇ ਪ੍ਰਸਾਦਿ ਸੂ ਵਾਲ ਗਫੇ |
ਇਨਹੀ ਕੇ. ਪ੍ਰਸਾਦਿ ਸੂ ਬਿਇਿਆ ਲਈ'
ਇਨਹੀ' ਕੇ ਪ੍ਰਸਾਦਿ ਫੂਨ ਧਾਮ ਭਗੇ |
ਇਲਹੀ ਕੀ ਲ੍ਰਿਪਾ ਕੇ ਸਜੇ ਹਮ' ਹੈ,
ਨਹੀਂ ਸੌ ਸੈ ਗ਼ਰੀਬ ਕ੍ਰੋਰ ਪਗੇ |
ਸ਼ਹੀਦੀ ਜੱਥੇ ਦੇ 500 ਸਿੰਘ ਹੀ ਨਹੀਂ, ਹਜ਼ਾਰਾਂ ਸਿੱਖ ਸੰਗਤਾਂ ਦੇ ਨੇਤਰ ਸੱਜਲ ਹੋ ਗਏ।
ਇੱਥੋਂ ਤਕ ਕਿ ਸੀ.ਆਈ.ਡੀ. ਦੇ ਸਿਪਾਹੀ, ਥਾਣੇਦਾਰ ਤੇ ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਦੇ ਪੁਲਿਸ ਅਫ਼ਸਰ ਨੇ ਆਪਣੇ
ਜੱਥਾ ਤੁਰ ਗਿਆ ਤੇ ਹਜ਼ਾਰਾਂ ਸੰਗਤਾਂ ਸ੍ਰੀ ਤਰਨ ਤਾਰਨ ਤਕ ਜੱਥੇ ਦੀ ਅਰਦਲ ਵਿੱਚ ਤੁਰਦੀਆਂ
ਗਈਆਂ।
ਇਹ ਪੁਲਿਸ ਅਫ਼ਸਰ ਜ਼ਿਲਾ ਰਾਵਲਪਿੰਡੀ, ਤਹਿਸੀਲ ਗੁਜਰਖ਼ਾਨ ਦੇ ਗੁਲਿਆਣੇ ਪਿੰਡ ਦਾ
ਰਹਿਣ ਵਾਲਾ ਸੀ। ਜਾਤ ਦਾ ਮੁਯਾਲ ਬ੍ਰਾਹਮਣ ਸੀ। ਸਿੱਖ ਲੀਡਰਾਂ ਦਾ ਖ਼ਿਆਲ ਸੀ ਕਿ ਭਾਈ
ਗੰਗਸਰ ਦੇ ਮੋਰਚੇ ਦੀ ਚਰਨ ਧੂੜੀ ਤੋਂ ਸ਼ਹੀਦ ਹੋਣ ਲਈ ਉਤਸ਼ਾਹਤ ਕੀਤਾ ਸੀ। ਪਰ ਇਸ
ਅਟਕਣ ਵਾਲੇ ਸ਼ੇਰਾਂ ਨਾਲ ਮੱਥਾ ਲਾ ਕੇ, ਸਰਕਾਰ ਆਪਣਾ ਰੋਹਬ ਗਵਾ ਲਵੇਗੀ ਤੇ ਅਖੀਰ
ਸਰਕਾਰ ਨੂੰ ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਜਾਨ ਤਲੀ 'ਤੇ ਰੱਖ ਕੇ ਜ਼ਿੰਦਾ ਸ਼ਹੀਦਾਂ ਨੂੰ ਹਰਾ ਸਕਣਾ ਕਠਿਨ ਹੀ ਨਹੀਂ,
ਇਸ ਹਕੀਕਤ ਦਾ ਗਿਆਨ ਜਦੋਂ ਗਵਰਨਰ ਨੂੰ ਹੋਇਆ ਤਾਂ ਸਰਕਾਰ ਨੇ ਆਪਣੀ ਪਾਲਿਸੀ
ਬਦਲ ਦਿੱਤੀ ਤੇ ਗੋਲੀ ਚਲਾਉਣ ਦੀ ਥਾਂ ਗਰਿਫ਼ਤਾਰੀਆਂ ਦਾ ਸਿਲਸਿਲਾ ਆਰੰਭ ਹੋ ਗਿਆ ਤੇ ਅੰਤ
66 - ਆਨੋਲਕ' ਹੀਰਾ		 English (Meaning Translation)

'...I bow a thousand times. You are fearless and steady [to go to] your Kalgidhar Father...'
...
*Muh Marne Ka Chao Hai Marau Ta Har Kai Duar ||*
*Mat Har Puchhai Kaun Hai Para Hamarai Bar ||*
(I have a longing to die; if I die, let it be at God's Door. Lest God asks, 'Who is this lying at My Door?')
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 1367)

...[Satguru], who saved the honor of a devotee who stood guard at a prostitute's door all night to save his friend from falling, why will He not help you brave warriors who save Dharma, Nation and Country? You belong to Dashmesh Ji and He is your protector forever. My worshipable Gursikhs! Come, see with my eyes! He (Guru Gobind Singh) is standing in the heavens, with Quoit (Chakar) on head, Kirpan in Gatra, and gesturing with his long arm reaching up to knees towards you...

*Inhi Ki Kirpa Ke Saje Hum Hain*
*Nahi Mo So Garib Kror Pare ||*
(It is by their grace that I am adorned, otherwise there are millions of poor people like me.)

Not only the 500 Singhs of Shahidi Jatha, but eyes of thousands of Sikh Sangat became tearful. To the extent that police constables, Thanedar and their Police Officer of CID also wiped their [tears?].
Jatha departed and thousands of Sangat walked in escort of the Jatha till **Sri Tarn Taran**.

This Police Officer was a resident of village **Gulyana**, Tehsil **Gujarkhan**, District **Rawalpindi**. He was a **Muyal Brahmin** by caste. Sikh leaders thought that Bhai Hira Singh Ji had encouraged the Jatha to become martyrs...
But confronting such lions... Government will lose its awe and finally it will be difficult for Government to defeat these living martyrs who keep their life on their palm...
When Governor realized this reality, Government changed its policy and instead of firing bullets, the series of arrests started and finally...

Notes
- The power of Bhai Hira Singh Ji's speech is described, moving even the police to tears.
- The shift in British policy from shooting to arresting (due to the moral force of Akalis) is noted.

2. ਸੰਗਤਾਂ ਦੇ ਜੋੜੇ ਸਾਫ਼ ਕਰਨੇ।

ਪੁਰ ਸੰਗਤਾਂ ਦੇ ਗੁਰੂ ਨਾਨਕ ਦਾ		 English (Meaning Translation)

..."Waheguru Ji Ka Khalsa Waheguru Ji Ki Fateh" - the miracle of fulfilling the command of Sri Guru Kalgidhar Father, [this victory] was the blessing of that Gursikhi life living Ragi, Bhai Sahib Bhai Hira Singh Ji's words, deeds and life-discipline.

[Context: Baba Kartar Singh Bedi]
...**Baba Kartar Singh Bedi**, son of **Baba Khem Singh Ji Bedi**, had hand [in opposition], who was a companion in this evil deed of the Mahant.
Therefore, according to the Gurmata passed in the Saka Nankana Sahib, Panth issued orders to boycott Baba Ji. On this Baba Ji faced such humiliation, which cannot be experienced now. In those days, the ballad (Qissa) of 'Punjabi de Shahidi Sake' had reached hands of lakhs of people. In this there was a 'Siapa' (mourning dirge) titled:
*Haye Haye Ve Kartar Sonya*
*Jiondiyan Yi Moyion Ve Kartar Sonya*
(Alas, Alas, O Kartar Singh beautiful/gold; You are dead while living, O Kartar Singh.)

When hawkers used to recite this Siapa in streets and bazaars effectively, huge number of people used to gather.
...until he made efforts to seek forgiveness. Panth is always forgiving, so Panth decided to accept his request made with true heart. But before this Baba Ji was ordered to give a writing. Regarding this it is found printed in **Khalsa Samachar**... **1924** - Bedi Ji gave this writing...
After that **Panj Pyare** pronounced the following **Tankhah** (religious penance) on Baba Ji:
1. From... date for five days, cleaning Parikarma of Sri Darbar Sahib with broom.
2. Cleaning shoes of Sangats.
(On pleading... this was forgiven/modified).

Notes
- "Baba Kartar Singh Bedi" was a descendant of Guru Nanak but opposed the Akali movement and supported Mahants/British. He was socially boycotted and later sought forgiveness.

ਪਿਆਰ ਸੀ, ਦਿਨ ਵਿੱਚ ਬਹੁਤ ਗਿਣਤੀ ਵਿੱਚ ਜਪੁਜੀ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਦੇ ਪਾਠ ਕੀਤਾ ਕਰਦੇ ਸਨ ... ਤੇ

ਪਾਠ ਕੀਤਾ ਕਰਦੇ ਸਨ। ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਦੀ ਪੁਰ ਅਸਰ ਕਥਨੀ ਦਾ ਅਜਿਹਾ ਅਸਰ ਪਿਆ ਕਿ ਬਾਝਾਂ
ਕਰਤਾਰ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੀ ਧਰਮ ਪਤਨੀ ਵੈਰਾਗ ਵਿੱਚ ਆ ਕੇ ਭੂੱਬਾਂ ਮਾਰਦੀ ਹੋਈ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਦੇ
ਚਰਨਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਗੁਰੂ ਬਾਬਾ ਜੀ ਦੇ ਹਜ਼ੂਰ ਆ ਡਿੱਗੀ। ਇਸ ਵਾਕਿਆ ਉੱਤੇ ਅਰਦਾਸਾ ਸੋਧ ਕੇ ਸੀ

(6		 English (Meaning Translation)

4. Journey bare-footed from Sri Amritsar to Nankana Sahib. Ardas there...
5. **25,000 Rupees** for Martyrs' Memorial (this was later reduced to 10,000).

In presence of Sangat, Baba Ji accepted this decision and Jakaras were sounded. This story is of **23 May 1924**.
[Jatha/Sangat] started [journey]. Stopped for 20-22 days [on the way]. Wherever they stayed at night, Diwans were held.
...note printed in **15 November 1924**:
"On 4 November 1924, at about 3 o'clock Jatha reached. For 24 hours Baba Ji and family kept cleaning the floor. Seeing the places of Martyr Singhs, stream of tears started flowing from Baba Ji's eyes..."

Next day morning, a huge Diwan was held at Sri Janam Asthan, regarding which **Bhagat Puran Singh Ji** founder of Pingalwara (1904-1992) has described his eye-witness account which was printed in **Khalsa Samachar of 28 August 1952**:
"I got the opportunity to listen to Bhai Hira Singh Ji's Kirtan only once in 1924... when Baba Kartar Singh Ji Bedi, due to Panthic displeasure, reached Nankana Sahib traveling on foot with his Jatha. Diwan was going on, Bhai Hira Singh Ji was giving lecture on the life of Baba Kartar Singh's father, **Baba Khem Singh Ji**. Narrating the Sakhi of Baba Khem Singh Ji's love for Japji Sahib and Gursikhi, he was telling that Baba Ji had immense love for Gurbani, used to recite many Japji Sahib paths in a day... that too reciting each word distinctly with understanding and feeling the emotion.
Bhai Sahib's effective speech had such an effect that Baba Kartar Singh Ji's wife, getting into Vairag (dispassion), screaming/sobbing fell at the feet of Bhai Sahib in presence of Guru Baba Ji. On this incident, Ardas was performed and Baba Kartar Singh Ji's mistake was forgiven before Sri Guru Granth Sahib Ji."

Notes
- "Bhagat Puran Singh Ji" (Pingalwara) gives eye-witness account of the reconciliation diwan.
- The forgiving nature of Panth is highlighted.

ਬਿਆਨ ਕੀਤਾ :
ਮਸ਼ਕਲ ਨਾਲ ਸਾਲ ਹੋਇਆ ਹੋਵੇਗਾ ਕਿ ਇੱਕ ਬਿਧ
ਮੁਸਲਮਾਨ ਫ਼ਕੀਰ, ਜਿਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਦੀ ਆਯੂ 70 ਸਾਲ ਦੇ ਕਰੀਬ		 English (Meaning Translation)

**Haji Muhammad Maskin and Sandalwood Whisk (Chaur):**
**Sir Mahadani Sardar Bahadur Dharam Singh Ji (1870-1933?)** ...was a Nitnemi Gursikh. He had immense love for **Sri Sant Attar Singh** and **Bhai Hira Singh**, and was a lover of their Kirtan.
In the second decade of 20th century when [work] of making **Delhi** the capital started... he started work. The red stone used on Government buildings of New Delhi, **Parliament House**, **Secretariat** and **Rashtrapati Bhavan** etc. is all done by Sir Dharam Singh Ji. Earning good profit in business, he spent immense wealth on religious works. Forming **Guru Nanak Vidya Bhandar Trust**, he started Gurmat Vidyala and many schools which are running beautifully till now. He built beautiful buildings of almost all historical Gurdwaras of **Delhi**.

In **December 1925**, on invitation of **Sardar Dharam Singh Ji Contractor**, Bhai Hira Singh Ji had gone to **Bharatpur** and from there Gwalior Sangat took him for Diwan program. There a Muslim Fakir, **Haji Muhammad Maskin** was staying.
Though Sai essentially belonged to **Lahore** but for more than half [century?] he lived in **Mecca** and **Medina**... and prepared a **Sandalwood Chaur (Whisk)** with his own hands there...
...after departure to Gurpuri... on **23.9.1926**, described like this:
"Hardly a year would have passed that an elderly Muslim Fakir, whose age was about **70 years**..."

Notes
- "S. Dharam Singh Contractor" - Famous philanthropist and builder of New Delhi.
- "Haji Muhammad Maskin" - A Muslim Fakir who made a unique Sandalwood Chaur for Golden Temple.

੪੧੧੫ _ 'ਹੂ੧੪ ਚ”		 English (Meaning Translation)

...came. Upon asking he told that he is originally from Lahore, but for more than half a century he has lived in **Mecca and Medina**, where sitting he has prepared a precious 'Chaur'. He told that he was staying in **Gwalior**, [where] Bhai Sahib Hira Singh Ji also reached due to Diwan. He (Muslim Fakir) got the good fortune of listening to Bhai Sahib's Kirtan. Bhai Sahib's speech triggered such a vibration of **Guru Nanak's love** that he writhed like a wounded bird and thinking that to reach Guru Nanak's Court and offer the Chaur... such a high [personality is needed?]...
Reaching **Amritsar**, Haji Sahib stayed at Bhai Hira Singh Ji's residence for many days. (Haji Maskin is sitting with Bhai Sahib).
Here only on the top roof of Bhai Sahib's house, with the arrangement of **S. Gurbakhsh Singh Narang**, Editor **'Preetam'**, a group photo was taken which was published in 'Preetam' issue of **January 1926**, which is given here also.
During this time Bhai Sahib consulted officials of Sri Darbar Sahib Committee and made a program for a special congregation to offer the Chaur.
So on **31 December 1925**, a huge Diwan was held at **Sri Akal Takht**, in which after conclusion of Kirtan, Bhai Hira Singh Ji addressing the Sangats told -
"This Muslim Fakir who is with me, has traveled around the world. Now dyed in the supreme color of Guru Nanak Dev Ji, he has reached here. Working continuously for **five years and seven months** with love, he has prepared this Sandalwood Chaur, which has **one lakh forty-five thousand** strands like hair. These strands are prepared from **9 maunds 14 seers (approx 370 kg)** of Sandalwood. Haji Muhammad Maskin Ji has come to offer this Chaur to Sri Darbar Sahib."
...
[Another] Banarasi... of [different] faith...

Notes
- The story of Haji Maskin offering the Sandalwood Chaur to Golden Temple via Bhai Hira Singh Ji is a famous example of inter-faith harmony.
- The weight of sandalwood used (9 maunds) is massive.

95		 English (Meaning Translation)

**Ek Lakh Paintalis Hazar Baal**
**Kara Yeh Chaur,**
**Samjho Haji Maskin Dastkar Asal Chandan Ne Banaya,**
**Baag Ki Khidmat Mein Laya Gaya**
(This Chaur with one lakh forty-five thousand hairs, understand that artisan Haji Maskin made it from real Sandalwood, and it has been brought for service of the Garden [Guru's Court].)

This **'Chaur of Sandalwood'** was included in the Jalau (treasure display) of Sri Darbar Sahib and when on special days Jalau is decorated, Sangats have Darshan of this Chaur also.

**Note:**
1. The news of congregation at Akal Takht is based on article published in **'Gurdwara Gazette' July 1972** by **S. Ravel Singh Advocate Chandigarh**.
2. In **Tribune** newspaper issue of **7 January 1979**, mentioning the items of Jalau of Sri Harmandir Sahib, **S. Jitvesh Singh Maini** wrote that the Muslim Fakir who offered Chaur was from **Turkey**. This point is not correct, Haji Sahib was originally resident of **Lahore**, not of Turkey.
3. Similarly in **Gurdwara Gazette September 72**, **Dr. Mohan Singh Ji** wrote: 'He spoke something in Arabic or Turkish, which one of his companion translated and told.' This is also not correct. We can say from personal knowledge... that Haji Sahib stayed alone at Bhai Sahib's residence. There was no other companion with him. Secondly he could speak **Hindustani** and **Punjabi** very well.

Notes
- Clarification on the origin of Haji Maskin (Lahore vs Turkey) and language skills.

**Shriman Bhai Sahib Bhai Vir Singh Ji (1872-1957)** was a great high soul and truthful poet, who did such solid work through his writings that its parallel is hard to find. Whether religious preaching, educational preaching or... he was master of [many qualities?]. His touch and glance of grace used to lift a man to higher realms. Remembering Waheguru always and remaining absorbed in Simran was his teaching and he himself used to do the same.

**Bhai Hira Singh Ji** met **Shriman Bhai Sahib Bhai Vir Singh Ji** first time in **1896** at **Lahore** and we have already mentioned about his joining work of **Khalsa Tract Society** under the title 'Early Life'. Although in this work he remained only for about a year, but the good fortune of his holy company (Satsang)...
When Ji used to come home from his preaching tours, after Darshan-Ishnan of Sri Darbar Sahib, he used to reach residence of Sri Bhai Sahib Ji, which used to be on upper floor of **Wazir Hind Press**, and spend considerable time in Satsang.

**Khalsa Samachar:**
[Regarding] newspaper **Khalsa Samachar** started by Sri Bhai Sahib...

- Introduces the deep spiritual bond between Bhai Hira Singh Ji and the legendary Bhai Vir Singh Ji.
- Mentions their meeting in Lahore (1896) and Khalsa Tract Society.

...used to try fully to [promote Khalsa Samachar] and during his tours... used to make effort to make maximum subscribers.
**(Gur Pratap) Suraj Parkash:**
Authored by **Bhai Santokh Singh Ji**, whose Katha (discourse) used to be held in Gurdwaras... in old times.
...[When editing/printing of Suraj Prakash] was accepted by **Bhai Vir Singh Ji**, then Bhai Hira Singh Ji started doing powerful propaganda for it and received hundreds of advance orders because this was a very big project. In this regard, Sri Bhai Sahib Ji has written in the preface of **Sri Gur Pratap Suraj Granth** on page 3:
"The dictionary/commentary of Sri Guru Granth Sahib became complete in about 7 years. Then this thought arose that... should be prepared and printed and plan should be made that first this matter be published. If some gentlemen become desirous of taking the Granth then work should be started. In those days famous **Bhai Hira Singh Ji Ragi** was staying with us. Learning about our this resolution, Bhai Hira Singh Ji became happy and said that indeed many difficulties are faced while contemplating this Granth, if footnotes/meanings are added then it will become easy. Bhai Sahib (Hira Singh Ji) himself used to contemplate this Granth then.
After some days he went out and upon returning said that 'I mentioned about your proposed annotated Suraj Prakash outside, people became happy with this idea but want that difficult matters in this Granth should be opened (explained) and objection-able places and historical errors should also be corrected/reconciled, so that gentlemen of every view may start reading this Granth.' After some thought, the advice to do exactly this was confirmed."
In its footnote it is also written - 'Due to Bhai Sahib's effort, many people had agreed to take the Granth then only.'
Keeping... in view, this work was started soon and preparing its first written volume, it was sent to **Kasur** to Bhai Hira Singh Ji, so that seeing the start of this work he may be satisfied. This story is of **May 1926**.
How much yearning Bhai Hira Singh Ji had for preparation of this Granth and its preaching, can be estimated from... which is found written in **Khalsa Samachar 28 May 1926**:
"...In few days only the proof-reading, correction... of Gur Pratap Suraj Granth... which Bhai Vir Singh Ji had started due to supreme keen desire of Bhai Hira Singh Ji, was going on... I received. I read it daily for one hour..."

Notes
- Detail about Bhai Hira Singh Ji's pivotal role in encouraging Bhai Vir Singh Ji to edit and publish the monumental "Gur Pratap Suraj Granth" (Suraj Parkash) with commentary.
- He secured advance orders and provided feedback from Sangat to include historical corrections.

9? - #ਜੰਲਕ' ਹੀਰਾ		 English (Meaning Translation)

...Poet Santokh Singh's devotion-filled verses, the way he glorified [Guru], feeling that from heart... [Bhai Hira Singh Ji] used to get absorbed in the juice of Satguru's praise and used to grant a particle of this juice to this slave (Bhai Vir Singh) also...

*Keh Ravidas Akath Katha Bahu Kahi Karijai ||*
*Jaisa Tu Taisa Tuhi Kia Upma Dijai ||*
(Says Ravidas, Your story is ineffable, what more can be said? You are like Yourself only, what comparison can be given?)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 858)

...wrote soaked in love and Blessed Commentator Bhai Sahib...
Bhai Hira Singh Ji said in extreme love and humility, 'Bhai Sudh Singh, they will be blessed people who will see this Suraj Prakash complete and realized and will read it. May my Giver Satguru grant me long life, Bhai Sudh Singh, may you live long, [so that] you may express my keen desire and heart's wish in Guru Sangats... wherever... establish Gur-Pratap Suraj Granth under Maharaj's Peehra (throne) or in the lower shelf of cabinet. Along with Satguru's Holy Form, may they read Satguru's history also with enthusiasm and drink nectar of Guru's praise. The garden of Guru Baba's praise...'
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 1376)

**Bhai Sahib Bhai Vir Singh Ji's love for Bhai Hira Singh Ji:**
Where Bhai Hira Singh Ji had deep love and respect for Shriman Bhai Sahib Bhai Vir Singh Ji in his heart, there Sri Bhai Sahib Ji also had deep love and pain for Bhai Hira Singh Ji in his heart and this love lasted till the end of Bhai Hira Singh Ji's body.
On Bhai Hira Singh Ji becoming ill, he came twice to enquire about his health. First time, in **March 1926**, when he was staying at **Lahore** in the bungalow of **Sardar Bahadur Hari Singh Deputy Commissioner**, then Sri Bhai Sahib Ji met him with great love... and after sharing spiritual words when he started to leave, he asked, 'Any service for me, please tell?' Bhai Hira Singh Ji had horripilation (hair stood on end) and said, 'You already take much trouble. Now do one favor, please send **Bhai Sudh Singh Ji**...'

Notes
- "Bhai Sudh Singh" - Associate/Assistant.
- Bhai Vir Singh Ji visited the ailing Bhai Hira Singh Ji twice, showing their close bond.

ਆਪਸ ਚਿੱਠੀ ਪਤਰ ਰਾਹੀਂ ਤੇ ਆਏ-ਏ ਰਾਹੀਂ ਮਗਵਾਉਂਦ ਰਹੇ ਅਤੇ ਆਪਣੀਆਂ ਝਝ
<੧ ੨ =,		 English (Meaning Translation)

'...send him to me for some days. If he comes, then continuous rain of Naam-Bani will start and my soul bathing in that pure shower will keep flying in higher realms.'
Bhai Sahib left saying 'Very Good' and reaching Amritsar wrote a postcard to Bhai Sudh Singh Ji, 'Bhai Hira Singh Ji desires that you go and stay with him for some days and read Naam-Bani together, do Satsang. His body is unwell and he is getting treatment.'
A few days after this, Bhai Sudh Singh Ji reached Bhai Hira Singh Ji, by then he had moved from **Lahore** to **Kasur**.

Second time **Bhai Sahib Bhai Vir Singh Ji** came to visit **Kasur Hospital**...
He sat on the chair and looking at the effect of the room said, 'Bhai Hira Singh Ji! This room does not look like a sick-room at all; here the fragrance of Gurbani is permeating in the atmosphere.' Bhai Hira Singh Ji with tearful eyes said, 'It is [result of] your blessings and Doctor Sahib's kindness.'
Respected Bhai Sahib Ji then started natural spiritual discourse and said to Bhai Hira Singh Ji, 'Bhai Sahib! To conclude from bodily pain that the deeds of the being are not good, is not correct. All are not good, all are not bad. A thief and tyrant who commits theft and tyranny all his life, when suddenly police raids and catches him or shoot him dead, will that man dying instantly be considered good?'
'...knows, for us the Satguru's order is *"Jab Lag Jivah Kali Kal Meh, Jan Nanak Naam Sambhar"*. Pain and pleasure are all His command.'
*Hey Gobind Hey Gopal Hey Dayal Lal...*
*Arogam Maha Rogam Bismrite Karuna Mayah ||*
(To forget the Compassionate One is the greatest disease; remembering Him is health.)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 1326)

'...is, but if one is healthy, distinct, but forgetting the Ocean of Grace Sri Waheguru Ji, he is a great patient. Thus Satguru Ji has [done kindness?] on the one doing Simran...
...why not suffering... so now do Simran more than before...'
With these words Bhai Hira Singh Ji forgot his pain and his consciousness got fixed in Naam. And then till his last time, Bhai Sahib Ji and Bhai Hira Singh Ji kept exchanging letters and sending messages...

Notes
- Deep spiritual philosophy discussed between Bhai Vir Singh and Bhai Hira Singh regarding suffering and disease.
- Bhai Vir Singh emphasizes that physical pain doesn't imply bad karma; forgetting God is the real disease.

(ਭਾਨ		 English (Meaning Translation)

...[letter written by] Bhai Hira Singh in pain-filled words, reading which tears flow spontaneously... tried and warned the Panth many times. For example, a note published in **Khalsa Samachar** dated **7 October 1927** is as follows:
"**Priceless Diamond:** It has been only a few days that unique preacher of Sikh Panth **Bhai Hira Singh Ji Ragi** has passed away. Friend and foe alike are praising his capability with one voice and it is an accepted fact that the amount of Sikh Dharma preaching done by this solitary life, no single person has done in last 50 years... The question of establishing his memorial has come before Sikh public many times in one form or other, but till now no scheme seems to have matured. Appreciation of Arya Samaj for its servants and Khalsa Ji's..."
On the **25th Death Anniversary** of Bhai Hira Singh Ji, in the lead article of **Khalsa Samachar Special Issue (30 August 1951)** also, expressing a sweet complaint, Shriman Bhai Sahib Ji wrote:
"Today 25 years have passed since Bhai Hira Singh Ji Ragi went to the other world, as if an era has passed, but memory is still alive. Although the Panth whose unbroken service he did, has not established any memorial for him, but in hearts..."
[Bhai Sahib Bhai Vir Singh Ji] gave [some amount?] for 'Scholarship' to **Khalsa College Amritsar** and ordered that with the interest of this amount, scholarships should be given to Amritdhari and Kirtan performing students.
In **1967**, sons of Bhai Hira Singh Ji offered similar amount more and doubled the scholarships.

**Bhai Hira Singh Ji's...**
...kept taking care of his consciousness. On this writer [Bhai Vir Singh?] he had special blessing.
(Letter)

Notes
- Mentions the lack of a formal Panthic memorial for Bhai Hira Singh Ji despite his immense contribution.
- Bhai Vir Singh Ji established a scholarship in his memory at Khalsa College Amritsar.

੧		 English (Meaning Translation)

**Ik Onkar Sri Waheguru Ji Ki Fateh ||**

Shriman Respected Bhai Sang Singh Jio,
Your letter has been received. The date for Kaka and Kaki's wedding is to be fixed...
Whatever Waheguru Ji does, is good. May True King Guru accomplish both tasks with happiness.
Many many congratulations from my side to you and children's mother.
In this envelope there are **two handkerchiefs** and **one cheque**. Please accept this for both tasks...
May the couples be long-lived and possessors of Sikh Sidak. May the hand of your love remain on children's heads. Congratulations, Dhan Guru Nanak Dev, Dhan Guru Nanak Dev.

Notes
- A personal letter (likely from Bhai Hira Singh Ji or Bhai Vir Singh Ji) congratulating on a wedding and sending gifts. Content is brief.

3
/2.		 English (Meaning Translation)

**Sri Sant Attar Singh Ji Mastuana Wale (1866-1927)** was a great soul of meditation and earnings of Naam. Light used to drip from his face. His first visit to **Faruka** is written to be in **August 1903**, when he stayed in Faruka for full 18 days and showered rain of Kirtan and also accomplished a difficult Anand Karaj.

During these very days, one evening, Sri Sant Ji while walking went and sat on the top of the 'Pakka Khu' (bricked well) and got absorbed in Simran. When Samadhi opened, he made a utterance (Bachan), "Here some Gurmukh has practiced meditation, the Chit (consciousness) has blossomed."
Bhai Hira Singh Ji kept this thing in his heart and later buying that piece of land, got a **Gufa** (cave/meditation cell) built at that place.
The service of this Gufa, Bhai Sahib performed along with Sangat of the area while reciting Gurbani.
This Gufa was a small two-storied building, under which there was a basement (tekhana) and above a room (Chaubara). After that whenever Sri Sant Ji used to come to Faruka, [he] used to sit in this Gufa's solitary place to do Kirtan and Bhajan Simran and enjoy spiritual bliss. Sometimes some Satsangis also joined.

**Last Meeting:**
In **July-August 1926**, when Bhai Hira Singh Ji [was in] **Delhi**...

Notes
- Relation with Sant Attar Singh Ji Mastuana.
- Construction of a 'Gufa' in Faruka at a spot identified by Sant Ji as spiritually charged.

[Letter/Message]:
"His soul has such attraction that we are compelled to come here soon..."
**Bhai Pardhan Singh Ji**, who was sent by Bhai Hira Singh Ji to bring Saints from Bangla Sahib... was standing nearby. Placing head on Saints' feet [he said], 'Bhai Hira Singh Ji is also yearning for your Darshan...'
...Along with Jatha Sri Sant Ji reached Malik Sahib's bungalow.
...cars were parked towards the gate of the bungalow. Seeing Sant Ji... started reading:
*Amrit Neka Tan Haria Gur Peh Mo Ko Lavau ||*
*(Nectar rains, body becomes green, take me to the Guru)*
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 1018)

...folding hands, bowed head on [Sant Ji's] feet and taking him...
...garland... which was kept near... put in Sant Ji's neck...
[Spent] time in remembrance of Akal Purakh...

Notes
- Describes the last emotional meeting between Bhai Hira Singh Ji and Sant Attar Singh Ji in Delhi (1926).
- Bhai Hira Singh Ji was ill and Sant Ji visited him.

62 - #ਸੰਲਕਾ ਹਰਾ		 English (Meaning Translation)

'...is pure, is immaculate. Keep soul higher than body. Do not worry about bodily pain. This pain is in body but soul is healthy. True King wants to take you in His lap by liberating you from the cycle of birth and death in this birth itself...'
*Pivat Ram Ras Amrit Pivau Sila Bikh Jivau ||*
*Har Ka Naam Sada Nidh Nihchal Eh Dhan Jate Kau Devo ||*
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 496)

Interacting like this, Sant Ji departed from there. Bhai Sahib's heart got cooled, consciousness became high and soul peaceful.

**Sant Baba Nand Singh Ji (1879-1943):**
Who was an image of happiness and love, practiced, respected and preached his main ideal: accepting Sri Guru Granth Sahib Ji as Guru. Due to detachment (Upramta) and Vairag from young age, he did not marry. Blessed many places of Western Punjab and jungles with his touch. Left the arrangement of food and water to God and lived...
Bhai Hira Singh Ji's meeting with Baba Ji seems to have happened in **1920-21**. His younger brother, **Bhai Pardhan Singh Ji** has mentioned this small meeting in these words:
"Bhai Sahib went and met **Jagraon Wale Sant Baba Nand Singh Ji** at about midnight and folding hands requested, 'O Guru Beloved Gurmukh, *Deh Sajan Asisriyan Jiyo Hovai Sahib Sio Mel*'. Regarding this meeting whatever words happened between Bhai Sahib and Baba Ji, Bhai Sahib did not tell, but said this much: 'Sitting in this pleasure, it became almost Amrit Vela, time for Kirtan.' So Bhai Sahib Ji performed Kirtan of Asa Di Var, whose Bhog fell at sunrise. Upon Bhog, Sant Baba Ji said to Bhai Hira Singh Ji, 'What offering should I make for this Kirtan? You have blessed me with that thing, equal to which there is no material object on earth. Kirtan is Priceless Diamond (Nirmolak Heera)...'"
*(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 815)*

**Bhai Sahib Bhai Sudh Singh Ji**, with whom Bhai Hira Singh Ji had extreme love, was a great spiritual rasia, melodious Kirtaniya and sweet explainer. Living an age of about 90 years, he [passed away] on **13 November 1972**...

Notes
- Meeting with the great Saint **Baba Nand Singh Ji** of Jagraon (Nanaksar).
- Baba Nand Singh Ji's appreciation of Bhai Hira Singh Ji's Kirtan as "Nirmolak Heera".
- Mention of Bhai Sudh Singh Ji's passing in 1972.

**Bhai Sudh Singh Ji (Continued):**
He was born in **Jila Sargodha (Pakistan)** and after acquiring knowledge of Gurbani in childhood, when he arrived in **Gujranwala** in **1901** for business, he became the first student of Bhai Hira Singh Ji. The discussion about his first meeting with Bhai Hira Singh Ji in 1903 has been mentioned earlier.

[The Committee] sent Bhai Sudh Singh and **Bhai Lal Singh Pracharak** to foreign countries to collect funds. He took a vow to collect and bring **five thousand rupees** after performing Ardas and left home, and returned after about one and a half years after collecting funds from **Malaya, Singapore, Hong Kong**.

The acquaintance made with Bhai Hira Singh Ji in Gujranwala slowly turned into love. Both were from same region and had love for each other's qualities and region, which lasted till the end. Bhai Sudh Singh Ji along with his Jatha used to regularly attend religious Diwans at **Faruka**, where both used to enjoy the pleasure of Satsang together.

In 1919, **Bhai Ram Kishan Gurmat High School** was opened [in Faruka?] and Bhai Sahib performed almost all its service. To the extent that once he mortgaged his **Sargodha house** with bank and took loan of **ten thousand rupees** to pay off school's debt. Then he did not tell anyone about this and went to **Burma** with Jatha to collect funds for school. Slowly this news leaked out...
When they [Bhai Hira Singh Ji?] came to know about this sacrifice of Bhai Sudh Singh Ji... [he] kept it in heart and did not say anything covering his mouth. Then **Sardar [Lahora?]**...
When he told, 'Only ... are needed...'
Saying this Bhai Sahib's eyes filled with tears and sitting in front... **Sardar Sujan Singh Ji Vakil**, who was Bhai Sahib's...

Notes
- **Bhai Sudh Singh Ji's** dedication to Panthic causes (school in Faruka) is highlighted. He mortgaged his own house to clear school debts.
- He traveled to SE Asia (Malaya, Singapore, etc.) for fundraising.

ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੀ ਇਹ ਅਪੀਲ ਅਜਿਹੇ ਢੁੱਕਵੇਂ ਤੇਂ ਖਿੱਚ ਭਰੇ ਲਫ਼ਜ਼ਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਸੀ
ਕਿ ਸੰਗਤ 'ਤੇ ਡੂੰਘਾ ਪ੍ਰਭਾਵ ਛਾ ਗਿਆ ਅਤੇ ਸੰਗਤਾਂ ਨੇ ਉਸੇ ਵੇਲੋਂ ਰੁਪਿਆ ਇਕੱਠਾ ਕਰਕੇ
ਸਦ ਸਮੇਤ ਬੈਂਕ ਨੂੰ ਅਦਾ ਕਰ ਦਿੱਤਾ ਤੇ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੇ ਮਕਾਨ ਦੀ ਲਿਖਤ ਵਾਪਸ
ਲੈ ਕੇ ਉਸਦੇ ਟੁਕੜੇ-ਟੁਕੜੇ ਕਰਕੇ, ਡਾਕ ਰਾਹੀ ਭਾਈ ਸੁੱਧ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੂੰ ਬਰਮਾ ਭੇਜ ਦਿੱਤੀ। ,
ਇਸ ਦੇ ਮਿਲਣ 'ਤੇ, ਪਹਿਲਾਂ ਤਾਂ ਉਹ ਕੁਝ ਹੈਰਾਨ ਹੋ ਗਏ ਕਿ ਇਹ ਕੀ ਮਖੌਲ ਕਿਸੇ ਨੇ ਕਰ
ਦਿੱਤਾ ਹੈ, ਪਰ ਜਦ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੀ ਪੱਤ੍ਰਿਕਾ ਪੜ੍ਹੀ, ਤਾਂ ਪਤਾ ਲੱਗਾ ਕਿ ਇਹ ਸਭ
ਕੁਝ ਕਿਵੇਂ ਹੋਇਆ ਤੇ ਕਿਸ ਨੇ ਕੀਤਾ ਹੈ।
ਕਸੁਰ ਪੁੱਜਣਾ : ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੀ ਬੀਮਾਰੀ ਦੇ ਦਿਨਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਆਪ ਆਪਣੇ ਜੱਥੇ
ਸਮੇਤ ਪੁਰਾ ਇੱਕ ਮਹੀਨਾ ਕਸੂਰ ਆ ਕੇ ਟਿਕੇ। ਸਾਰਾ ਦਿਨ ਗੁਰਬਾਣੀ ਗੁਰ-ਇਤਿਹਾਸ ਤੇ
ਕੀਰਤਨ ਦੁਆਰਾ ਸਤਿਸੰਗ ਦਾ ਸੋਹਣਾ ਵਾਯੂਮੰਡਲ ਬਣਿਆ ਰਹਿੰਦਾ। ਸਵੇਰੇ ਨਿਤਨੇਮ, ਸੁਖਮਨੀ
ਸਾਹਿਬ ਤੇ ਬਾਵਨ ਅਖਰੀ ਦਾ ਪਾਠ ਹੋਣਾ ਤੇ ਪਿਛਲੇ ਪਹਿਰ ਸੁਰਜ ਪ੍ਰਕਾਸ਼ ਦੀ ਕਥਾ। ਸੁਖ ਸਾਂਦ
ਮੁੱਛਣ ਆਏ ਸੱਜਣ ਵੀ ਲਾਭ ਉਠਾਉਂਦੇ। ਸ਼ਾਮ ਦੇ ਵਕਤ ਇੱਕ-ਦੋ ਸ਼ਬਦ ਭਾਈ ਪ੍ਰਧਾਨ ਸਿੰਘ
ਜੀ ਨੇ ਗਾਇਨ ਕਰਨੇ, ਤੇ ਬੜਾ ਹੀ ਰਸ ਬੱਝਦਾ ਸੀ।
ਇੱਕ ਮਹੀਨੇ`ਦੇ ਬਾਅਦ ਜਦ ਭਾਈ ਸੁੱਧ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਵਿਦਾ ਹੋਣ ਲੱਗੇ ਤਾਂ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ
ਜੀ ਬੜੇ ਵੈਰਾਗ ਵਿੱਚ ਆ ਕੇ ਆਖਣ ਲੱਗੇ, 'ਭਾਈ ਸੁੱਧ ਸ਼੍ੰਘ ਜੀ ! ਤੁਸਹਾਂ ਜੋ ਗੁਰਬਾਣ] ਦੇ
ਪਾਠ ਮੈਨੂੰ ਲਗਾਤਾਰ ਸੁਣਾਏ ਹਨ, ਮੈਂ ਕਿਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਲਫ਼ਜ਼ਾਂ ਨਾਲ ਤੁਹਾਡਾ ਸ਼ੁਕਰ ਕਰਾਂ ? ਲੂੰ ਵੀ
ਥੋੜ੍ਹੇ ਹਨ, ਸ਼ਕਰ ਨਹੀਂ ਹੋ ਸਕਦਾ।ਫਿਰ ਉਨ੍ਹਾਂ 'ਭਾਈ ਸੁੱਧ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨੂੰ ਗਲ ਨਾਲ ਲਾਇਆ
ਤੇ ਆਖਿਆ, 'ਮੇਰੀ ਇੱਕ ਪ੍ਰਬਲ ਇੱਛਾ ਹੇ,ਕਿ ਮੇਰੇ ਅੰਤ ਵੇਲੇ ਤੁਸੀਂ ਜ਼ਰੁਰ ਮੇਰੇ ਕੋਲ ਹੋਣਾ।
ਗੁਰੂ-ਦਾਤਾ ਮੇਰੇ ਸਿਰ 'ਤੇ, ਮਰੇ ਅੰਗ-ਸੰਗ ਹੈ। ਤੁੰਸੀਂ ਅਰਦਾਸ ਕਰੋ, ਉਹ ਸਦਾ ਮੇਰੇ ਹਿਰਦੇ ਵੱਸੇ
। ਮੈਂ ਦਾਤੇ ਤੋਂ ਇਹ ਮੰਗਦਾ ਹਾਂ, ਤੁੰ ਅੰਤ ਵੇਲੇ ਮੇਰੇ ਕੋਲ ਹੋਵੇਂ ਤੇ ਗੁਰਬਾਣੀ ਸੁਣਾਂਦਿਆਂ,
ਗੁਰਬਾਣੀ ਦੀ ਗੋਦ ਵਿੱਚ ਹੀ ਮੈਨ ਗੁਰੂ ਦੇਸ਼ ਟੋਰੇਂ ' ਇਹ ਕਹਿੰਦੇ ਹੋਏ ਦੋਵੇਂ ਵੀਰਾਂ ਦੇ ਨੈਣਾਂ ਵਿੱਚੋਂ
ਨੀਰ ਆ ਗਿਆ ਤੇ ਭਾਈ ਸੁੱਧ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਫ਼ਤਹਿ ਗਜਾ ਕੇ ਸਰਗੋਧੇ ਵਿਦਾ ਹੋ ਗਏ। ਇਹ
ਵਿੱਥਿਆ ਮਈ 1926 ਦੀ ਹੈ। ਲੇਖਕ ਉਦੋਂ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਦੀ ਸੇਵਾ ਵਿੱਚ ਉੱਥੇ ਹਾਜ਼ਰ ਸੀ।
ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੇ ਪਿੱਛੋਂ, ਭਾਈ ਸੁੱਧ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਤਕਰੀਬਨ ਹਰ ਸਾਲ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ
ਦੀ ਯਾਦ ਵਿੱਚ ਕੁਝ ਨਾ ਕੁਝ ਲਿਖ ਕੇ 'ਮਾਲਸਾ ਸਮਾਚਾਰ' ਵਿੱਚ ਛਪਵਾਉਂਦੇ ਰਹੇ। ਉਹ ਕਹਿੰਦੇ
ਹੁੰਦੇ ਸਨ, 'ਜਦ ਸਤੰਬਰ ਦਾ ਮਹੀਨਾ ਨੇੜੇ ਆਉਂਦਾ ਹੈ ਤਾਂ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੀ ਯਾਦ
ਸਾਡੇ ਹਿਰਦੇ ਵਿੱਚ ਆ ਹੁਲਾਰਾ ਮਾਰਦੀ ਹੈ। ਅੱਜ ਮੈਨੂੰ ਪਿਆਰਾ, ਮਿੱਠਾ-ਮਿੱਠਾ ਰਸੀਆ ਵੀਰ

ਨ
ਤਦ		 English (Meaning Translation)

'...Bhai Sudh Singh, who is filled with spirit of sacrifice... who has made only Panth Sewa the goal of his life... and who paying off Panthic Ashram's debt by mortgaging even his own house... has now gone to Burma. Now it is our duty to pay off Bank's debt and release his house.'
Bhai Hira Singh Ji's this appeal was in such appropriate and attractive words that it had deep effect on Sangat and Sangat collected money at that very time and paid to the Bank along with interest. Bhai Hira Singh Ji took back the deed of house, tore it into pieces and sent it by post to Bhai Sudh Singh Ji in **Burma**.
On receiving it, first he was surprised... but when he read Bhai Hira Singh Ji's letter, he came to know how all this happened...

**Reaching Kasur:**
During the days of Bhai Hira Singh Ji's illness, he [Bhai Sudh Singh] came to **Kasur** with his Jatha and stayed for full one month. All day beautiful atmosphere of Satsang remained through Gurbani, Gur-History and Kirtan. In morning Nitnem, recitation of Sukhmani Sahib and Bavan Akhri, and in afternoon Katha of Suraj Prakash. Friends coming to enquire health also benefited. In evening time Bhai Pardhan Singh Ji used to sing one or two Shabads...
After one month when Bhai Sudh Singh Ji was about to leave, Bhai Hira Singh Ji getting very emotional said, 'Bhai Sudh Singh Ji! The continuous recitations of Gurbani you have made me listen to, in what words should I thank you? ...words are few... Then he hugged Bhai Sudh Singh Ji and said, 'I have one strong desire, that at my last time you must be with me. Guru-Giver is on my head, is with me. You do Ardas that He may always dwell in my heart. I ask this from Giver, that you be with me at last moment and reciting Gurbani, you should send me to Guru's Country in the lap of Gurbani.' Saying this tears flowed from eyes of both brothers and Bhai Sudh Singh Ji saying Fateh departed for **Sargodha**. This story is of **May 1926**. The writer was present there in Bhai Sahib's service then.
After Bhai Hira Singh Ji, Bhai Sudh Singh Ji used to write something in his memory almost every year and get it published in **'Khalsa Samachar'**. He used to say, 'When month of **September** comes near, the memory of Bhai Hira Singh Ji swings in our heart...'

Notes
- Moving story of community support: Bhai Hira Singh Ji raises funds to release Bhai Sudh Singh's mortgaged house.
- Bhai Sudh Singh spends a month with the ailing Bhai Hira Singh in Kasur, reciting Gurbani.
- Bhai Hira Singh's wish for Bhai Sudh Singh to be present at his final moments.

੧ ਰੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਗੁਰੂ ਕਾ ਅਦੁੱਤੀ ਕੀਰਤਨੀਆ ਚੇਤੇ ਆ ਰਿਗ ਨੈ
ਭਾਈ ਕੇ ਰਹਿਣ-ਬਹਿਣ ਅਤੇ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਸੁਨਣ ਉਰ ਨ ਦੇ ਹਉ
ਹਰੇ ਨਾਲ ਬਹੁਤਾ ਪਿਆਰ ਸੀ ਤੇ ਸਚਮੁਚ ਉਹ ਗੁਣਾਂ ਦਾ ਵਪਾਰ ਕਰਨ ਵਾਲਾ ਗੁਣ ਗ ਹ ਦਾਤ
ਗਰ ਦਾ ਮਹਰ ਪਾਤਰ ਤੇ ਨਿਰਵੈਰ ਮੰਡਲ ਵਿਚ ਪਡਣ ਕਾਲਾ ਮਹਾ ਖਲ ਅਉ
ਫ਼ਾਹਿਗੁਰੂ ਜੀ ਨੇ ਔਰਮਿ ਦੀ' ਵਿੱਦਿਆ ਬਮ਼ਸ਼ੀ' ਹੋਈ ਸੀ। ਉਸਦੀ ਰਸਨਾ 'ਤੇ ਉਇ
ਸੀ ਤੇ ਵਾਗ ਰਚਨਾ ਦਾ ਤਾਂ ਮਾਨੋ ਉਹ ਉਸਤਾਦ ਸੀ। ਹਜ਼ਾਰਾਂ ਸਰੋਤਿਆਂ ਨ ਰਤ
ਫਿਰ ਮਾਲਾਂ ਦੇ ਮਣਕਿਆਂ ਵਾਂਗ ਪਰੇ ਕੇ ਬੰਨ੍ਹ ਛੱਡਦਾ ਸੀ ਤੇ ਕਮਾਲ ਇਹ ਸੀ ਰਿ ਰਿ
ਰਾਰ-ਚਾਰ ਘੰਟਿਆਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਕਿਸੇ ਨੂੰ ਹਿਲਣ ਨਹੀਂ ਸੀ ਦਿੰਦਾ। ਉਸਦੇ ਵਕਤੱਵਯ ਦਾ ਮਿੰਨਾ ਰਸ
ਸੀ, ਕੋਈ ਕਮਾਈ ਸੀ...।
ਸੰਤ ਸੰਗਤ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਕਮਾਲੀਏ ਵਾਲੇ (1882-1950) ਇੱਕ ਮਹਾਨ ਅਧਿਆਤਮਕ
ਦੇ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਹਿਤ ਲਾਇਆ ਸੀ। ਆਪ ਜੀ ਦੀ ਕਥਨੀ, ਜਾਦੂ ਅਸਰ ਰੱਖਦੀ ਸੀ। ਜਦ ਆਪ ਸ਼ਬਦ
ਦੀ ਕਥਾ ਕਰਦੇ ਹੋਏ ਸਿੱਖੀ ਦੇ ਗੂੜ੍ਹ ਆਸ਼ੇ ਤੇ ਉੱਚੇ ਆਦਰਸ਼ 'ਤੇ, ਗੁਰਬਾਣੀ ਦੇ ਪ੍ਰਮਾਣਾਂ ਨਾਲ,
ਸੁਣ ਕੇ ਅਤੀ ਪ੍ਰਭਾਵਤ ਹੋ ਜਾਂਦੇ ਸਨ।
ਸੀ ਸੰਤ ਜੀ ਦਾ ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਨਾਲ ਗੂੜ੍ਹਾ ਪਿਆਰ ਸੀ ਅਤੇ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਜੀ
ਫਿਰਕੇ ਦੇ ਧਾਰਮਿਕ ਦੀਵਾਨਾਂ 'ਤੇ ਆਪ ਸਤਿਸੰਗ ਦਾ ਰਸ ਮਾਣਦੇ ਸਨ।
ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦੇ ਗੁਰਪੁਰੀ ਸਿਧਾਰਨ ਉਪਰੰਤ ਭੋਗ ਅਵਸਰ 'ਤੇ ਆਪ ਨੇ ਫਿਰੂਕ
ਦਰਸ਼ਨ ਦਿੱਤੇ ਤੇ ਆਪਣੇ ਭਾਸ਼ਨ ਦੇ ਅੰਤ ਵਿੱਚ ਫੁਰਮਾਇਆ ਸੀ :
ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਰੇਸ਼ਮ ਦਾ ਕੀੜਾ ਸੀ ਜੋ
ਰੇਸ਼ਮ ਕੱਢਦਾ-ਕੱਢਦਾ ਆਪ 'ਬਸ' ਹੋ ਗਿਆ।
੨ ਡਾਕਟਰ ਸਾਹਿਬ (1876-1934) ਦਾ ਆਦਰਸ਼ਕੇ ਜੀਵਨ ਸੀ। ਆ ੩
ਤੇ ਚੋਟੀ ਦੇ ਡਾਕਟਰ ਸਨ। ਸੋਹਣਾ ਸੁਡੌਲ ਭਰਵਾਂ ਸਰੀਰ, ਚਮਕਾ ਤਬੀਅਤ
ਕਰਨ ਨਾਲ ਹੀ ਦੁਰ ਹੋ ਜਾਂਦਾ ਸੀ। ਲੋਕ ਆਪ ਨੂੰ ਅਰੋਗਤਾ ਦਾ ਫਰਿੜਤਾ ਆਖਿਆ ਕਰਦ
ਸਨ। ੨
ਅਫ਼ਸਰ, ਸੂਬੇਦਾਰ ਰਤਨ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦ
ਆਪ ਧਮਿਆਲ (ਰਾਵਲਪਿੰਡੀ) ਦੇ ਇੱਕ ਫ਼ੌਜੀ
ਨਨ ਜਰ ਯਜਰਨੇ ਦਾ ਯਮਨ -		 English (Meaning Translation)

'...today sweet sweet Bhai Hira Singh, Guru's unique Kirtaniya is coming to memory... was very loving with everyone and truly he was a trader of virtues... recipient of Guru's grace and a great player in sphere of No-Enmity (Nirvair)... Waheguru Ji had blessed him with knowledge... On his tongue Saraswati resided and in speech-composition he was like a master. He used to bind thousands of listeners like beads in a rosary... and wonder was that for four-four hours he would not let anyone move. There was sweet juice in his oratory, it was some spiritual earning...'

**Sant Sangat Singh Ji Kamalie Wale (1882-1950):**
Was a great spiritual [soul]... had dedicated himself for preaching. His speech had magical effect. When he used to do Katha of Shabad, explaining deep meanings and high ideals of Sikhism with proofs from Gurbani... listeners used to get extremely impressed.
Sri Sant Ji had deep love with Bhai Hira Singh Ji and... used to enjoy Satsang at religious Diwans of **Faruka**.
After Bhai Hira Singh Ji's departure to Gurpuri, on the occasion of Bhog he visited Faruka and in the end of his speech said:
"Bhai Hira Singh Ji was a **silkworm** who... while extracting silk (virtues) ended himself."

**Dr. Sahib (1876-1934):**
[Dr. Diwan Singh/Dr. Ratan Singh?] had an ideal life. ...was a top doctor. Beautiful well-built body, shining nature... [disease] used to go away just by [his touch/sight?]. People used to call him Angel of Health.
**Subedar Ratan Singh Ji**:
He was a military officer from **Dhamial (Rawalpindi)**...

Notes
- Tributes from **Sant Sangat Singh Ji Kamalie Wale**. He compared Bhai Hira Singh to a silkworm giving silk (virtues) to others while consuming itself.
- Introduction of another personality, likely a Doctor (Military background).

ਗੁ ਇਤਿਹਾਸਕਾਰ, ਬਾਬਾ ਪ੍ਰੇਮ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਹੋਤੀ ਦੀ ਲਿਖਤ ਅਨੁਸਾਰ 'ਲਾਨ੍ੋ
ਲਾਲ ਸਨ ਸਿ ਪਤ ਕਰਕੇ, ਸਭ ਤੋਂ ਪਹਿਲਾਂ ਆਪ ਅਸਿਸਟੈਂਟ ਸਰਜਨ ਹੋ ਕੇ ਗਲਬਨ
1903 ਜਾਂ ਇਸ ਤੋਂ ਇੱਕ-ਦੋ ਸਾਲ ਪਹਿਲਾਂ, ਜਦ ਕਿ ਸਰਹੱਦੀ ਸੂਬਾ ਅਜੇ ਨਵਾਂ-ਨਵਾਂ ਬਣਿਆ
ਸੀ, ਤਾਂ ਮਰਦਾਨ ਪੋਸਟ ਹੋਏ ਸਨ। ਭਾਈ ਭਾਗ ਸਿੰਘ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦਾ ਰਾਗੀ ਜੱਥਾ ਉ ਰ੍
ਦਿਨਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਦੇ ਕਮਾਲ 'ਤੇ ਸੀ ਅਤੇ ਭਾਈ ਸਾਹਿਬ ਜੀ ਦਾ ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਨਾਲ ਪਿਆਰ
ਅਤਿ ਦਰਜੇ ਦਾ ਸੀ। ਉੱਥੇ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਦੀਵਾਨ ਗੁਰਪੁਰਬ ਸਮਾਗਮ ਬੋਅਤ ਹੱਏ ਤੇ ਆਤਮਕ
ਲਹਿਰੇ ਚਲੋਂ, ਜੋ ਬਾਹਰ ਉਜਾੜਾਂ, ਨਦੀਆਂ ਦੇ ਕਿਨਾਰਿਆਂ ਉੱਤੇ, ਪਹਾੜਾਂ ਦੀਆਂ ਚੋਟੀਆਂ
ਉਪਰ, ਤਖ਼ਤ ਬਾਈ ਸ਼ਾਬਾਜ ਗੜ੍ਹੀ ਜਿੱਥੇ ਅਸ਼ੋਕ ਦਾ ਖ਼ੁਤਬਾ ਪਿਆ ਹੈ ਤੇ ਹੋਰ ਕਈ ਇਕਾਂਤ
ਰਮਣੀਕ ਉਜਾੜਾਂ ਵਿੱਚ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਨਿਰਬਾਣ ਸਹਿਜ ਢੰਗ ਦੇ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਹੋਏ!
ਭਾਈ ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਦਾ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਸੁਣਨ ਵਿੱਚ, ਡਾਕਟਰ ਸਾਹਿਬ, ਬਹੁਤ ਵੇਰ ਸਜਲ
ਨੇਤਰ ਹੋ ਕੇ ਰਸ ਵਿੱਚ ਮਗਨ ਹੋ ਜਾਇਆ ਕਰਦੇ ਸਨ। ਹਾਂ, ਉਹ ਨਿਰੰਕਾਰੀ ਕੀਰਤਨ, ਜਿਸਨੂੰ
ਸਰਵਨ ਕਰਨ ਨਾਲ ਮਨ, ਬਾਹਰ ਮੁਖੀ ਧਾਵਨਾਂ ਨੂੰ ਛੱਡ ਕੇ, ਆਪਣੇ ਜੋਤ ਸਰੂਪ ਅਸਲੇ ਵਿੱਚ
ਇਕਾਗਰਤਾ ਕਰ ਲੈਂਦਾ ਹੈ :
ਸਤਿਸੰਗਤਿ ਸਾਈ ਹਰਿ ਤੇਰੀ ਜਿੜੂ` ਹਰਿ ਕੀਰਤਿ ਹਰਿ ਸੁਨਟੇ 11 ਹ

.. ੪ ਆ ਅੰ” %7 ੭੭		 English (Meaning Translation)

According to historian **Baba Prem Singh Ji Hoti**...
[Dr. Ratan Singh?] was son of... First he became **Assistant Surgeon** and approximately in **1903** or one-two years before that, when Frontier Province was newly formed, he was posted at **Mardan**. Bhai Bhag Singh Hira Singh Ji's Ragi Jatha was at peak of Kirtan in those days and Bhai Sahib Ji's love with them was of extreme degree. There Kirtan Diwans, Gurpurb congregations were held and spiritual waves moved... on secluded riverside, mountain peaks, **Takht-i-Bahi**, **Shahbaz Garhi** where Ashoka's inscription is lying and other secluded scenic wildernesses, Kirtan was performed in state of Nirban (bliss).

Listening to Bhai Hira Singh Ji's Kirtan, Doctor Sahib often used to get teary-eyed and absorbed in juice (Ras). Yes, that Nirankari Kirtan, listening to which mind leaving extroverted pursuits concentrates in its own light-form essence:
*Satsangat Sai Har Teri Jit Har Kirat Har Sunne ||*
(That is Your True Congregation, O Lord, where Your Praise is heard.)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 1135)

In **1908-09** he became **Civil Surgeon** and went to **Shimla**, then **Dera Ghazi Khan**, **Gurdaspur**, **Lyallpur**, **Jhang** etc. Wherever he went, he spread fragrance of Satsang. In **1926** when he went for tour of **England** (Vilayat), then Bhai Hira Singh Ji met him at **Jhang Station** and boarding the train went with him till **Lodhran** doing Satsang! While he was in England, Bhai Sahib passed away. From there he sent telegrams and letters of condolence.
Retiring in **1930**, he first came to Shimla and then **Rawalpindi**. In **April 1934** conference he met with great warmth and hugging me said, 'Today I have met beloved Bhai Hira Singh.' In June due to tooth extraction... trouble increased and finally in His Will on **15.9.1934** he went to Guru's feet.

**Bhai Sant Singh Ji Garhi Kapura:**
Four or five miles from **Mardan**, there was a village named **Garhi Kapura**. Here lived Gurmukh Beloved **Bhai Sant Singh Ji (1880-1965)**, whose fragrance of philanthropy was spread in whole Frontier, whose facial smile had magnetic attraction and whose quivering lips had vibration of Simran.
He was crazy (devotee) of Kirtan. Whenever Bhai Sahib went to Mardan, then [he visited] Garhi Kapura...

Notes
- **Dr. Ratan Singh (Civil Surgeon)**: Close friend of Bhai Hira Singh. They did Kirtan in wilderness of Mardan/Takht-i-Bahi.
- Bhai Hira Singh accompanied him in train till Lodhran when Dr. Ratan Singh left for England in 1926.
- **Bhai Sant Singh Ji (Garhi Kapura)**: Another devout Sikh of Frontier region.

ਸੰਤਾਂ ਅੜੇ		 English (Meaning Translation)

[Regarding Bhai Sant Singh Ji]:
...
**(Khalsa Samachar, 1966, written by S. Manohar Singh)**
On the passing away of Bhai Sant Singh Ji, Sachkhand-dweller Bhai Sudh Singh Ji wrote a letter to the bereaved family, in which refreshing the memory of his supreme love for Bhai Hira Singh Ji...
"Jio! Folding my hands, turning desires of mind, sitting with soul... cautious and one-pointed listener has come, Sultan of Beautiful ones... Court of... 'Tithey Bhagat Vasah Ke Loa'. In Bhai Sant Singh's [heart], wave of Kirtan has left..."

**Sardar Manmohan Singh Ji (Born 1893):**
Name practitioner (Naam Abhyasi) with high life...
Who got Satsang of Bhai Sahib Bhai Vir Singh Ji throughout life...
Always remained dyed in color of Naam-Bani.
...were residents of **Rawalpindi** or **Abbottabad**, but their [love] for Satsang was like...
Whenever [Bhai Hira Singh Ji came]... met him and got happy...
Later when S. Manmohan Singh Ji came to **Lahore**, he got more opportunity to meet.
When Bhai Sahib came to Lahore or Bhai Sahib went to Kasur... spiritual happiness was attained meeting him. Once he especially went to **Faruka** to visit... Meeting **Bhai Sant Singh Ji**...
And then spent [time] with Bhai Sahib Bhai Hira Singh Ji...
...For writing biography, Sardar Manmohan Singh gave... [help/material].

Notes
- Mentions **S. Manmohan Singh Ji**, another close associate of Bhai Hira Singh Ji and Bhai Vir Singh Ji, who provided material for this biography.
- Refers to a tribute letter by Bhai Sudh Singh on death of Bhai Sant Singh.

ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ' ਸਿੰਧ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਲਈ ਜਾਂਦੇ ਤਾੰ ਉਸ ਗੁਰਦੁਆਰ ਨ
ਸੀ। ਉਥੋਂ ਦੇ ਰਿਵਾਜ ਅਨੁਸਾਰ, ਇਸ ਵਿਧਵਾ ਬੀਬੀ ਨੂੰ ਘਰੋਂ ਨਿਕਲਣ ਦੀ ਮਨਾਹੀ ਸੀ ਤੁ
ਇਹ ਆਪਣੇ ਘਰ ਹੀ ਬੈਠੀ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਦਾ ਅਨੰਦ ਮਾਣਿਆ ਕਰਦੀ ਸੀ ! ਇਸ ਤੋਂ ਇਸ ਨੂੰ
ਕਰ ਦਿੱਤਾ। ਫਿਰ ਗੁਰ ਇਤਿਹਾਸ ਤੇ ਖ਼ਾਲਸਾ ਟ੍ਰੈਕਟ ਸੁਸਾਇਟੀ ਦੇ ਟੈਕਟ ਪੜ੍ਹਨੇ ਸ਼੍ਰ ਕੀਤੇ। ਕਈ
ਸਾਲ ਇਹ ਬੀਬੀ ਘਰ ਵਿੱਚ ਹੀ' ਸਿੱਖੀ ਦੇ ਮਾਰਗ 'ਤੇ ਚਲਦੀ' ਰਹੀ! ਅਖੀਰ ਇਹ ਰਹਿ ਨਾ ਸਕੀ
ਤੇ ਇੱਕ ਵਾਰੀ ਜਦ ਭਾਈ' ਹੀਰਾ ਸਿੰਘ ਜੀ ਫਿਰ ਉਸ ਨਗਰ ਗਏ ਤਾਂ ਆਪਣੇਂ ਮਾਤਾ-ਪਿੜਾ
ਨੂੰ ਮਨਾ ਕੇ ਗੁਰਦੁਆਰੇ ਜਾ ਕੇ ਕੀਰਤਨ ਵਿੱਚ ਹਾਜ਼ਰੀ ਭਗੀ । ਹੌਲੀ-ਹੌਲੀ ਰੰਗਣ ਚੜ੍ਹਦੀ ਗਈ
ਤੇ ਇੱਕ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਦੇ ਅਵਸਰ 'ਤੇ ਇਸ ਨੇ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤਪਾਨ ਕੀਤਾ ਤੋਂ ਨਾਮ ਬਿਸ਼ਨ ਦੇਈ
ਤੋਂ ਬਿਸ਼ਨ ਕੌਰ ਰਖਿਆ ਗਿਆ। ਕੁਝ ਚਿਰ ਬਾਅਦ ਇਨ੍ਹਾਂ ਦੇ ਪਿਤਾ ਜੀ ਵੀ ਅੰਮ੍ਰਿਤ ਛਕ ਕੇ
ਸੇਠ ਥਾਹਰੀਆ ਮਲ ਤੋਂ ਥਾਹਰੀਆ ਸਿੰਘ ਹੋਏ
ਇਸ ਬੀਬੀ ਨੇ ਫਿਰ ਸਿੰਧ ਵਿੱਚ ਸਿੱਧੀ ਦਾ ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਕਰਨਾ ਆਰੰਭਿਆ, ਮਗਰੋਂ ਕਰਾਚੀ ਵਿੱਚ
ਪ੍ਰਚਾਰ ਸੈੱਟਰ ਕਾਇਮ ਕੀਤਾ ਤੇ ਇੱਕ' ਗੁਰਦੁਆਰਾ ਮਹੱਲਾ ਖ਼ਾਰਾਦਾਰ ਵਿੱਚ ਬਣਵਾਇਆ ਜੋ

**Mata Bishan Kaur Ji (Karachi/Sindh):**
When Bhai Hira Singh Ji used to go for preaching in Sindh... Gurdwara...
According to custom there, this widow lady was forbidden to go out of home. So sitting in her home only she used to enjoy the Kirtan! This [Kirtan]... her...
Then she started reading Gur-History and tracts of **Khalsa Tract Society**. For many years this lady continued walking on path of Sikhism while being at home. Finally she could not resist and once when Bhai Hira Singh Ji went to that town again, she convinced her parents and went to Gurdwara to attend Kirtan. Slowly the color [of Naam] kept rising and on one occasion of Amrit Parchar, she took Amrit and her name was changed from **Bishan Dei** to **Bishan Kaur**. After some time her father also took Amrit and became **Thahriya Singh** from **Seth Thahriya Mal**.

This lady then started preaching Sikhism in Sindh, later established a Preaching Center in **Karachi** and got a Gurdwara built in neighborhood (Mohalla) **Kharadar**...
She used to lecture in [Sindhi?] words such that no one could say she was not Sindhi.
Attending **Sikh Educational Conference** congregations, she used to [promote] female education and...
Strong emotions for love of Sikhism used to rise in her.
(Adopted a child named **Keshdhari Singh**). Spirit of Sikhism was filled in this child so much...

Notes
- Story of **Mata Bishan Kaur**, a Sindhi widow who was inspired by Bhai Hira Singh's Kirtan (initially listening from home due to purdah/custom). She became a prominent preacher and established a Gurdwara in Karachi.

**Bhai Amar Singh Ji Nambardar of Gondal (1870-1926?):**
[Bhai Hira Singh Ji] had [love] with **Bhai Amar Singh Ji Gondal** (18??-1926) and used to do Satsang.
Their lands were in a village named **Gondal** and when Bhai Amar Singh Ji used to be on lands, then Bhai Hira Singh Ji especially used to go there covering distance...
Bhai Amar Singh Ji's life was like that of complete Gurmukh. Waking up at last watch of night (Pehla Pehar)... Nitnem and Bhajan...
At time of Parkash (opening) of Guru Granth Sahib, it was necessary for whole family (four sons and...) to be present there before taking Maharaj's Hukam.
He had deep love and sympathy for every being. *"Manas Ki Jaat Sabh Ekai Pehchanbo"*.
Once upon asking Bhai Amar Singh Ji the reason [for sadness?], he said, 'We have no place here now, because despite having majority we have been deprived of **Nambardari** (headmanship).' Hearing this Bhai Sahib was moved and inspired him to stay there only, and assured him that soon He will get **half Nambardari** registered in his name. Accepting his word he stayed back and within one year Bhai Amar Singh Ji got half Nambardari from Muslims.
After some time with the offspring of these very Muslims, Bhai Amar Singh Ji had some...

Notes
- **Bhai Amar Singh Ji Gondal**: A devout Nambardar (village head). Bhai Hira Singh Ji predicted he would get Nambardari, which came true.
- His daily routine of family Nitnem is described.

...dispute arose and they filed a suit against Bhai Amar Singh Ji. The case went from lower courts to **High Court**. In papers their [Bhai Amar Singh's] side was weak and contest was tough.
Bhai Amar Singh Ji was a Sidaki Sikh and had great faith in Guru House but this had become a question of honor. So he told his mind's pain to Bhai Hira Singh Ji. Bhai Sahib gave courage and recited this line:
*Tu Kahe Dole Paraniya Tudh Rakhaiga Sirjanhar ||*
(Why do you waver, O mortal? Create will protect you.)
And giving other proofs from Gurbani brought him in Chardi Kala and said:
*Jis Ka Sahib Dhada Hoi || Tis No Mar Na Sakai Koi ||*
(He closely on whose side is the Lord... no one can kill him.)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 842)
Let us give... Our Privy Council is Satguru's Court, so:
*Upav Chhod Gahu Tis Ki Ote || Nimakh Mahe Hovai Teri Chhot ||*
(Leave other efforts and grasp His Support; in an instant you will be released.)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 177)
"Therefore come, let us hold Akhand Path of Sri Guru Granth Sahib Ji and Ardas at Satguru's feet... whatever outcome comes from it... give to **High School Faruka**. With its income, poor and orphan children will get help in education and Langar." Bhai Amar Singh Ji accepted this proposal. So Akhand Path was held. On the day of Bhog many students of school reached there. **Bhai Bhag Singh Hira Singh Ji** performed Divine Kirtan of Asa Di Var...
*Prabh Jio Khasmana Kar Pyare || Bure Bhale Ham Thare ||*
(O Beloved Lord, make me Your own; good or bad we are Yours.)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 631)
*Mere Har Jio Sabh Ko Terai Vas ||*
(My Dear Lord, everything is in Your control...)
(Guru Granth Sahib, Ang 736)

On the other side, after some time, it was the first day of **High Court** [being upgraded/renamed from Chief Court?] and first case. Bhai Amar Singh Ji's lawyer with great wisdom...

Notes
- A legal dispute over land where Bhai Amar Singh's side was weak.
- Bhai Hira Singh Ji advised spiritual recourse: Akhand Path and Ardas, pledging the outcome to **High School Faruka**.
